# UniSat Wallet | UniSat

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet#unisat-wallet-home-for-your-bitcoin-assets)

**UniSat Wallet — Home for Your Bitcoin Assets**

_Easy and safe to trade, inscribe, and manage assets with UniSat_

UniSat wallet is the first fully open-source, non-custodial, and decentralized wallet built for Bitcoin’s innovative standards. it provides users with a decentralized, self-custody experience alongside a suite of integrated tools, including:

*   UniSat Marketplace
    
*   UniSat Inscribe
    
*   InSwap
    
*   UTXO Management Tool
    
*   DApp Center
    

Together, these services deliver a one-stop, seamless on-chain experience for Bitcoin and Fractal Bitcoin.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet#key-advantages-of-unisat-wallet)

**Key Advantages of UniSat Wallet:**

*   **Decentralized**/**Non-Custodial** **Control:** Your private keys, passwords, and seed phrases are never stored by UniSat. Users retain full control of their keys with no personal data collected.
    
*   **100% Open Source:** All code is available on GitHub, ensuring transparency, security, and community-driven development.
    
*   **Encryption & Security:** Private keys are encrypted locally with your password, providing robust protection for your assets.
    
*   **Privacy First:** UniSat does not track personal data. You can import private keys as "imported" accounts for flexible wallet management.
    
*   **All-in-One Bitcoin & Fractal:** UniSat Wallet supports Native SegWit, Taproot, Nested SegWit, and Legacy address types. You can manage BTC, Ordinals, Runes, and Alkanes in one place, with multi-seed import and batch address derivation. Seamlessly access UniSat Marketplace, Inscribe, InSwap, UniScan and other services, and switch between Bitcoin and Fractal with a single click.
    
*   **Multi-Platform Support:** Available on iOS, Android, and web browsers for convenient, cross-device access.
    

Being a non-custodial wallet means you will be in full control of managing and safeguarding your assets, including your seed phrase, private keys, and wallet password. You are the only one with access, and thus fully accountable for their security. You will need:

*   Back up your recovery phrase or private keys securely. Losing them means losing your assets permanently.
    
*   Set a strong wallet password and keep it safe. UniSat cannot help recover forgotten passwords.
    
*   Only download UniSat Wallet from the [official websitearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/download)
     to avoid fraud or phishing.
    
*   Be cautious when clicking links or downloading software from any source.
    

Stay safe and enjoy your journey with UniSat Wallet!

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet#disclaimer)

# How to Deposit/Withdraw Assets | UniSat

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-deposit-withdraw-assets#id-1.-download-or-update-unisat-wallet)

1\. Download or Update UniSat Wallet

Get the latest version of the UniSat Wallet here:

👉 [https://unisat.io/downloadarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/download)

To create a new wallet, follow this step-by-step guide:

👉 [https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-walletarrow-up-right](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-wallet)

Once your wallet is created, you can use UniSat to store, manage, transfer, or trade your assets.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F3hvON1xNDG788Hrm6eGv%252F1.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9a8fc93-3df1-421b-a39d-3ea80f80218d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21f28af0&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-deposit-withdraw-assets#id-2.-how-to-deposit-assets-into-unisat-wallet)

2\. How to Deposit Assets into UniSat Wallet

*   Open UniSat Wallet and tap **Receive** on the main Wallet page to view your UniSat wallet address, which can be used to receive BTC, Ordinals, Runes, and Alkanes assets.
    
*   Copy the address or use the QR code directly.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FOiA0OjqJf8goIFHiv3VJ%252F2.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D463f9d46-bddd-4371-8101-1b5f20e0ea49&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=295ad0d5&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F3UVver6lcIcIokHhGdQO%252F3.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd36074bc-60f0-4cf3-b33b-09d37f0ea2b4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d90ed3fb&sv=2)

*   Go to the withdrawal page of the exchange or platform you’re transferring from.
    
*   Paste your copied UniSat address, enter the amount, and follow their instructions to complete the withdrawal.
    
    *   Example:
        
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fw4nn6v61qSghb5Gpa9em%252F4.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a1fc09f-b9f8-4f1b-bf37-27cd3bb97376&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6dbf2be&sv=2)

**Note:**

UniSat supports 4 types of address formats for BTC, Ordinals, Runes, and Alkanes. Before depositing, make sure the address format in your UniSat Wallet matches the format used on the withdrawal platform. You can switch address type in: ⚙ Settings > Address Type For example, Taproot (bc1p...) is commonly used for receiving inscriptions.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-deposit-withdraw-assets#id-3.-how-to-transfer-assets-from-your-unisat-wallet)

3\. How to Transfer Assets from your UniSat Wallet

*   Open your UniSat Wallet and tap **Send**.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FxSjfm5zJ05gI0ACFNlYa%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ccccb70-eb06-4fa9-b480-0af403cff1ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd520b99&sv=2)

*   Enter the recipient address and the transfer amount.
    
*   Tap **Next**, review details, and **sign to confirm**.
    

> ✅ **Always double-check your inputs and outputs before signing the transaction.**

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FXTESMpwk6PSUzd7Gri3j%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf59909d-65f5-488e-92bf-4a8e56129aca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb87017f&sv=2)

📌 **Quick Tip for tickerTransfers (Ordinals / Runes / Alkanes)**

**For specific assets:**

*   Go to the **Assets** tab.
    
*   Tap on the ticker you want to transfer.
    
*   Enter the **ticker Details Page**, and tap **Transfer** to proceed.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Flqz1ATgil46e04S0j1xM%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3d3cfb4-9d97-422f-9976-e42f6718bdec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ca57f7a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FKNVLV5CViixkxvr6XpDg%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a718b74-2487-44f8-940a-9c98a2c5c98e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87f56628&sv=2)

# How to Create UniSat Wallet | UniSat

Follow the steps below to create your wallet and get started.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-wallet#id-1.-download-unisat-wallet)

1\. Download UniSat Wallet

Visit [here arrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/download)
to download UniSat Wallet. After installation, start creating your wallet.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FpC7bzBrh2xcSaTwxubB0%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df75e0ca5-bbcd-4a0e-8f4e-0fd5373832f3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=968dc2b5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-wallet#id-2.-create-or-import-a-wallet)

**2\. Create or Import a Wallet**

*   Click **Create New Wallet** to set up a new wallet.
    
*   If you already have a wallet, click **I already have a wallet** to import your wallet using your recovery phrase.
    
*   You can also click **Connect to Hardware Wallet** to link your hardware wallet. Currently, Keystone hardware wallets are supported (more options will be added in the future).
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FPgM2oWkGNYwZMerXUBja%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df44fb467-a74e-409b-88da-39c8f880f0e3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5659432&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-wallet#id-3.-set-a-login-password)

**3\. Set a Login Password**

This password is used to unlock your UniSat Wallet. **As a decentralized wallet, UniSat does not store your password and cannot help recover it if lost. Keep it safe.**

**Password Tips:**

*   Use a combination of uppercase, lowercase, numbers, and special characters.
    
*   Avoid personal information or common words.
    
*   Do not reuse passwords from other accounts—set a unique password for UniSat Wallet.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FTHlViorWbhBzTQlQ81rF%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D120f9d09-6f5d-474b-85a4-f8ac957cf2a9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=277d5941&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-wallet#id-4.-backup-your-recovery-phrase)

**4\. Backup Your Recovery Phrase**

**Your recovery phrase (seed phrase) is your key to accessing your wallet. If anyone obtains your recovery phrase, they can control your assets. Losing or exposing it can lead to permanent asset loss.**

**Important Security Reminders:**

*   NEVER screenshot, copy, or photograph your seed phrase.
    
*   Do not let anyone watch you create your wallet.
    
*   Avoid storing your seed phrase in cloud storage, emails, SMS, or any connected devices.
    
*   Never share your seed phrase through communication tools.
    
*   Do not store your seed phrase in one place or entrust it to others.
    
*   Keeping your seed phrase on internet-connected devices poses significant risks.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FhWPWdTZFLXWFFOO72S6x%252F3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D790bbcc6-7baf-4c30-9082-81055fd5173e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=756dbf5b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-wallet#id-5.-complete-wallet-creation)

**5\. Complete Wallet Creation**

At this stage, you will see four wallet address types. All four types of wallet addresses support receiving, sending, and storing BTC, Ordinals, Runes, and Alkanes assets.

The most commonly used types are **Native SegWit (bc1q)** and **Taproot (bc1p)**. You can choose based on your needs.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FnOMgpIEwrb7dCeRwGOoz%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2400a8bd-5106-47ca-9c35-d90d825ac36a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91689a4c&sv=2)

UniSat Wallet supports 4 Bitcoin address formats and allows switching between them in the settings.

Type

Script Type

Derivation

BIP

Native Segwit

P2WPKH

m/84'/0'/0'

[bip-0084arrow-up-right](https://github.com/bitcoin/bips/blob/master/bip-0084.mediawiki)

Nested Segwit

P2SH-P2WPKH

m/49'/0'/0'

[bip-0141arrow-up-right](https://github.com/bitcoin/bips/blob/master/bip-0141.mediawiki)

Taproot

P2TR

m/86'/0'/0'

[bip-0341arrow-up-right](https://github.com/bitcoin/bips/blob/master/bip-0341.mediawiki)

Legacy

P2PKH

m/44'/0'/0'

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-wallet#undefined)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-wallet#custom-hdpath-optional)

**Custom HdPath (Optional)**

The Custom HdPath defines how your wallet's hierarchical deterministic (HD) structure generates addresses. Different paths produce different wallet addresses.

Example: `m/84'/0'/0'/0/0` → Native SegWit (bc1q addresses)

*   `m`: Master key
    
*   `84'`: Purpose—BIP84 (Native SegWit)
    
*   `0'`: Coin type—Bitcoin Mainnet (0 for Bitcoin Mainnet, 1 for Testnet)
    
*   `0'`: Account: Account 0 (you can have multiple accounts)
    
*   `0`: Address Type: 0 = External (receiving) address, 1 = Internal (change) address
    
*   `0`: Address index (first generated address)
    

**Note:** If you use a custom HdPath or other wallet tools with different paths, you must enter the exact same path during recovery to restore the same wallet address.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-wallet#phrase-optional)

Phrase (Optional)

The Phrase is an optional additional password for enhanced security. It is NOT the same as the login password set in Step 3.Entering a different Phrase during wallet recovery generates valid wallets, but with different addresses. If you set a Phrase, make sure to remember it—it's required for wallet recovery.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-wallet#final-reminders-decentralization-full-responsibility)

Final Reminders: Decentralization = Full Responsibility

Using a decentralized wallet means you fully control your assets—and are responsible for your own security.

**Please remember:**

1.  UniSat never stores your recovery phrase or private keys. Back them up securely. Losing them means losing your assets permanently.
    
2.  Set a strong wallet password and keep it safe. UniSat cannot help recover forgotten passwords.
    
3.  Only download UniSat Wallet from the [official websitearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/download)
     to avoid fraud or phishing.
    
4.  Be cautious when clicking links or downloading software from any source.
    

####

# UniSat Wallet Safety Guide: Protecting Your Assets | UniSat

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#understanding-the-risks)

Understanding the Risks

Browser extension wallets have become an essential tool for managing digital assets, but they come with inherent security risks that every user should understand:

**Browser Sandbox Limitations**

The browser's built-in sandbox mechanism, while important, serves as a single line of defense. This makes it a potential target for sophisticated attacks, as breaking this one mechanism could compromise the entire system.

**Weak Extension Isolation**

Extensions within the same browser environment have limited isolation from each other. This creates a "weakest link" scenario - if one extension is compromised, it could potentially affect all others in the same browser environment, including your wallet extension.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#essential-safety-practices)

Essential Safety Practices

To protect your digital assets when using extension wallets, consider implementing these security measures:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#id-1.-browser-account-separation)

1\. Browser Account Separation

Create a dedicated browser profile for your wallet extensions. This profile should:

*   Install only essential wallet extensions
    
*   Be kept separate from your daily browsing profile
    
*   Use a separate account for each wallet extension where possible
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#id-2.-restricted-browsing)

2\. Restricted Browsing

When using a browser with wallet extensions:

*   Only visit verified, trusted websites
    
*   Avoid general web browsing
    
*   Stay away from unfamiliar or suspicious links
    
*   Always verify website URLs carefully
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#id-3.-duo-browser-strategy)

3\. Duo-Browser Strategy

For maximum security:

*   Use one browser exclusively for wallet extensions and cryptocurrency transactions
    
*   Use a different browser for general web browsing
    
*   Keep your crypto-dedicated browser clean and minimal
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#id-4.-hardware-wallet-integration)

4\. Hardware Wallet Integration

Consider using a hardware wallet as your primary security measure:

*   Hardware wallets provide the highest level of security
    
*   Use them in conjunction with extension wallets for enhanced protection
    
*   Keep critical assets in hardware wallets while using extension wallets for smaller, frequent transactions
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#about-unisat-wallet)

About UniSat Wallet

UniSat is a non-custodial, open-source browser extension wallet. This means:

*   We never store or have access to your private keys
    
*   You have complete control over your assets
    
*   All code is open-source and verifiable
    
*   Your funds remain solely in your possession
    

While we maintain the highest security standards possible for an extension wallet, we believe in complete transparency about the inherent risks of browser-based wallets and empowering users with security best practices.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#looking-forward)

Looking Forward

We understand that in today's increasingly complex digital environment, wallet security cannot rely solely on traditional browser protection mechanisms. At UniSat Wallet, we're committed to strengthening our extension's security mechanisms to provide users with a safer experience, this is a key item on our 2025 Roadmap.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets#final-recommendations)

Final Recommendations

1.  Regular Security Audits
    

*   Review your installed extensions regularly
    
*   Remove unused or suspicious extensions
    
*   Keep your wallet extension updated to the latest version
    

1.  Best Practices
    

*   Always backup your seed phrases securely
    
*   Enable all available security features
    
*   Use strong, unique passwords for your browser profiles
    
*   Enable two-factor authentication whenever possible
    

Remember: Security in the digital asset space requires constant vigilance. While convenience is important, never compromise security for ease of use.

[NextBest Practices for Safetychevron-right](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety)

# How to Inscribe Transfer Using UniSat Wallet | UniSat

According to the brc-20 protocol, all transfers require a TRANSFER inscription before sending tickers to others. Here's how to do it properly using UniSat Wallet:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-inscribe-transfer-using-unisat-wallet#step-1-download-or-update-unisat-wallet)

Step 1: Download or Update UniSat Wallet

Make sure you're using the **official UniSat Wallet** and have updated to the latest version.

Download link: [https://unisat.io/downloadarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/download)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FUVcxNhl2eDduAMtwgCvy%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D95d84d5e-e090-4d15-8d4e-311c263ea22d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2135047f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-inscribe-transfer-using-unisat-wallet#step-2-check-your-assets-in-the-wallet)

Step 2: Check Your Assets in the Wallet

On the UniSat homepage, scroll to view your asset list. Click on any brc-20 assets to access their action buttons: Mint, Send, Trade

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fypp7OLMeOA8Dy6aatpQI%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc96b4bcf-21bf-4d63-a01e-61a4d871adc3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=14d37867&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-inscribe-transfer-using-unisat-wallet#step-3-understand-your-transfer-balance)

Step 3: Understand Your Transfer Balance

Click **Send** to initiate a transfer. You’ll see two balance types:

*   **Transferable Amount**: Already inscribed as TRANSFER — can be sent immediately. _(Note: This amount is not editable. It’s based on your existing TRANSFER inscriptions.)_
    
*   **Available (Inscribe TRANSFER)**: This part of your balance is not yet transferable. You need to inscribe transfer first to make it sendable.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FIp9vFaVKuo9eFaOehE8T%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2da7bcf1-205c-4061-a6b2-7be7217eb01c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=31dab2ed&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-inscribe-transfer-using-unisat-wallet#step-4-inscribe-transfer)

Step 4: Inscribe TRANSFER

Click the **“Inscribe TRANSFER”** button to start.

*   Enter the **amount** you want to inscribe
    
*   Set **Output Value** and **Fee Rate**
    
*   Click **Next**
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F71UORuJtyebzMZdjf0Qz%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd1088105-efa1-4138-ab02-dc2140ea8388&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1ca1af6d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-inscribe-transfer-using-unisat-wallet#step-5-confirm-and-inscribe)

Step 5: Confirm and Inscribe

Preview the details of the inscription. If all looks good, click **Next** \--> **Pay & Pay**

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FErEI3lrNp32WFfgq4Ir2%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0547d9a0-b58f-4cd6-8029-23ce5178dcd9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9e737f1b&sv=2)

Now your TRANSFER inscription is live and ready to be used for sending.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-inscribe-transfer-using-unisat-wallet#step-6-select-transfer-and-send)

Step 6: Select TRANSFER and Send

*   Go back to the **Send** page
    
*   Choose one or more **TRANSFER inscriptions**
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F6kM2BUte54W5G73GpOyz%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b29ba39-aa6e-4103-a10d-95b66e7bbec2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9a86ee6&sv=2)

*   Enter the **receiver’s address** or name
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FfKNt29rE1wx1NZcW4OHa%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1dcb88de-c03f-4409-9207-b1526e24c6c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b9fb1da&sv=2)

*   Carefully check the input and output, then click **Sign & Pay.**
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fh98jpeZxuopAye4kJ3Rd%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13b68574-988a-4d70-8aa4-9d2825c70481&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=753ae40d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-inscribe-transfer-using-unisat-wallet#step-7-done)

🎉 Step 7: Done!

You’ve successfully completed a brc-20 transfer using UniSat Wallet.Check your transaction status via wallet history or a public explorer.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FS4D1JXXyUVBYJYmbdoqR%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91098c19-3e79-46d6-b28d-9a758252edf5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9563cf3b&sv=2)

*   brc-20 Spec: [https://domo-2.gitbook.io/brc-20-experimentarrow-up-right](https://domo-2.gitbook.io/brc-20-experiment)

# Private Keys, Mnemonics & Derivation Paths: How Is Your Wallet Created? | UniSat

In the world of digital assets, your wallet holds all your assets, and controlling the private key of your wallet means controlling the funds associated with it.

So where does your private key come from?

Are mnemonic phrases really secure?

Can derivation paths be cracked?

Are wallets like UniSat truly secure?

Let’s break it down from a technical perspective.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/private-keys-mnemonics-and-derivation-paths-how-is-your-wallet-created#what-is-a-private-key)

What Is a Private Key?

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FzwbT1wDeMtrlCBbGHdYs%252F1.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0907da4-01b5-417b-96d6-3cbfa96e0e29&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ce1ca5e5&sv=2)

Holding the private key gives you the authority to spend funds associated with the corresponding address.

Therefore, _how the private key is generated, managed, and protected is the core of your asset security._

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/private-keys-mnemonics-and-derivation-paths-how-is-your-wallet-created#how-is-the-private-key-generated)

How is the Private Key Generated?

Most Bitcoin wallets follow standards BIP39, BIP32, or BIP44.

*   Step 1: Generate Random Entropy
    

The wallet first creates a high-entropy random number (128–256 bits).This entropy determines the unpredictability of the private key.If randomness is weak or predictable, the key can be at risk.

*   Step 2: Convert to Mnemonic Phrase
    

BIP39 defines how to convert entropy into a set of 12 or 24 human-readable words. These words are your _master key_.

*   Step 3: Generate the Seed
    

Mnemonic + optional Passphrase (“the 25th word”) are fed into PBKDF2, which performs thousands of hashing iterations to derive a strong Master Seed. This computational cost is intentional — it makes brute-force guessing significantly harder.

*   Step 4: Derive Keys Using Paths
    

Using standards like BIP32/BIP44/BIP86, the seed deterministically produces _many private keys_ along hierarchical derivation paths.Examples:`m/44'/0'/0'/0/0 → BIP44 (Legacy addresses) m/86'/0'/0'/0/0 → BIP86 (Taproot addresses)` Each address in your wallet is mathematically derived from the master seed and the derivation path.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/private-keys-mnemonics-and-derivation-paths-how-is-your-wallet-created#can-your-private-key-be-compromised-by-cracking-the-derivation-path)

Can your private key be compromised by cracking the derivation path?

No derivation paths are simply _formulas_ for deriving keys, cracking it does not expose your private key.The true security risks are:

*   Mnemonic or seed leakage
    
*   Vulnerabilities in wallet implementation or device environment (malware, side-channel attacks, insecure hardware)
    

To put it simply:

> The derivation path tells _where the key is_, but only the mnemonic _is the key itself_.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/private-keys-mnemonics-and-derivation-paths-how-is-your-wallet-created#is-the-randomness-safe-can-keys-be-collision-attacked)

Is the Randomness Safe? Can Keys Be “Collision Attacked”?

If the wallet uses a secure cryptographic random number generator (CSPRNG), the key space is astronomically large.A 256‑bit private key space is:`≈ 1.15 × 10^77 possibilities` Brute forcing such a key is infeasible with all computing power available in the universe. However — if a wallet uses:

*   weak pseudorandom sources
    
*   repeated seed patterns
    
*   compromised key generation logic
    

Keys may collide or be guessable — this is a _real_ risk, but it is a wallet implementation problem, not a protocol-level weakness. So the quality of entropy matters _a lot_.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/private-keys-mnemonics-and-derivation-paths-how-is-your-wallet-created#can-developers-or-platforms-know-my-private-key)

Can Developers or Platforms “Know My Private Key”?

If you use a **non-custodial, open-source wallet**, private keys are generated and stored **locally only**, and **developers have no access**.Risk appears only if you:

*   generate mnemonics on online websites
    
*   use closed-source / unknown wallets
    
*   sync keys to cloud services
    
*   input mnemonics into untrusted apps
    

✅ Best practice:

*   Generate mnemonics/keys offline
    
*   Use **open-source** non‑custodial wallets
    
*   Backup mnemonics securely (no screenshots, no cloud storage)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/private-keys-mnemonics-and-derivation-paths-how-is-your-wallet-created#unisat-wallet-security-recommendations)

UniSat Wallet Security Recommendations

UniSat is a fully non-custodial wallet:

*   Private keys and mnemonics are generated and encrypted locally
    
*   They are never uploaded to any server
    
*   All cryptographic logic is open-source and auditable
    

Your private key is encrypted using your wallet password and only you can decrypt it. These are security guarantees from a technical perspective, true wallet security requires your vigilance and good security habits:

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FfEbWl1CRzHUiGekCtPov%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D125ae354-0cf0-40be-8fe4-8a715ef005ea&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef44022e&sv=2)

Even with strong cryptography, compromised devices or phishing sites can still cause loss.

Trust the cryptography — but do not blindly trust the entropy source.

[PreviousBest Practices for Safetychevron-left](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety)
[NextExtension Wallet FAQchevron-right](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/extension-wallet-faq)

# Extension Wallet FAQ | UniSat

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/extension-wallet-faq#how-to-update-your-wallet)

**How to update your wallet?**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Usually, the extension will be auto-updated. If your extension didn't update to the latest version, then you may follow the steps below to update it.

1.  Click on the extension icon on the top right of your screen, then click "Manage extensions" menu.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FeDFIda7RCXQrg2ncvLm3%252Fimg_v3_026q_a2918678-741c-45fc-a0f4-dbc36576b3hu.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf0edf91-e02f-4064-8526-d82afc3691ae&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c488c3a&sv=2)

1.  Switch on to Developer mode, then click the "Update" button
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FV5jZbC3rwjPBgitQV9qw%252Fimg_v3_026q_5231b2ca-3a51-471b-9c38-078f133b53hu.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5612902d-caf4-4da4-a42c-55e93ad0b7d9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7a2b9ff1&sv=2)

1.  Then your wallet will be updated to the latest version.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/extension-wallet-faq#how-to-load-the-chrome-extension-wallet-into-your-chrome-from-manually)

How to load the Chrome extension wallet into your Chrome from manually


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The extension could be temporarily installed this way:

1.  Download the '[**unisat-chrome-xxx.zip**arrow-up-right](https://github.com/unisat-wallet/extension/releases/latest)
    ' file, unzip it to an isolated folder. ![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FtHf0ep2PdhLcbJ0IEhoj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D343f807f-c65b-4138-8b94-b3a65153e182&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56f99ebe&sv=2)
    
2.  Open Google Chrome and enter "**chrome://extensions/**" into address bar ("More Tools | Extensions" from menu) to open the extension page, find the switch "**Developer mode**" in the upper right corner and turn it on. ![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fxiq4m6HasR5Hx1Mid5KP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09c7df65-3d13-4f70-8571-77516cebd29c&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9dceae45&sv=2)
    
3.  Click "**Load unpacked**" button and browse to the unzipped folder. ![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FQfUVYFBDZR0m7JO3GpEg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D160fc102-43cf-4d31-a3ea-d1f89f1ccd96&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=59a040f8&sv=2)
    

*   By doing this, you can experience the new version in advance or install the plugin in cases where you cannot access the Google Chrome Web Store.
    
*   However, please note that versions installed in this way won't receive automatic updates and won't share data with versions downloaded from the Chrome Web Store.
    
*   Make sure you have only one Unisat Wallet plugin installed in the same browser to avoid conflicts.

# UniSat Wallet Recovery and Key Concepts | UniSat

This guide helps you understand the fundamental concepts of private keys and seed phrases, and provides practical instructions on how to recover your UniSat wallet in specific situations.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-recovery-and-key-concepts#what-are-private-keys-and-seed-phrases)

What Are Private Keys and Seed Phrases?

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-recovery-and-key-concepts#seed-phrase)

Seed Phrase

A seed phrase (or recovery phrase) is a human-readable representation of your private key, typically consisting of 12 or 24 random English words. It serves the same purpose as the private key and should be treated with the same level of security.

*   With your seed phrase, you can restore your wallet and recover all your assets.
    
*   Anyone with access to your seed phrase can take full control of your wallet.
    
*   It is critical to keep it private and stored securely (preferably offline, on paper).
    

**Best Practices for Seed Phrase Management:**

*   Back it up immediately after creating a wallet.
    
*   Do not take screenshots or store it on cloud drives.
    
*   Write it down and store it in a secure, offline location.
    
*   Double-check the words and their order for accuracy.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-recovery-and-key-concepts#private-key)

Private Key

A private key is a unique 64-character hexadecimal string that grants control over a blockchain wallet. It is the cryptographic proof required to sign transactions and move funds.

*   Think of it as the password to your blockchain bank account.
    
*   Whoever possesses the private key controls the wallet and its assets.
    
*   If lost, access to the wallet and all associated funds is permanently lost.
    

Because private keys are difficult to remember and risky to write down, wallets often provide a seed phrase as an easier alternative.

> 🔒 Remember: Losing your seed phrase or private key means losing access to your assets forever.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-recovery-and-key-concepts#how-to-import-restore-a-wallet-via-seed-phrase-or-private-key)

How to Import / Restore a Wallet Via Seed Phrase or Private Key

You can add an existing wallet into UniSat using your **mnemonic phrase** or **private key**.Steps:

*   Open the App or Extension Wallet.
    
*   On the homepage, click **HD Wallet (top-left)** → enter Wallet Management.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FehREiEjxOMEPwMtWH6O9%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D148c7c8f-2bab-4ced-9a00-a59177503d27&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4f42f065&sv=2)

*   Click the **+** icon (top-right) to import more wallets.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FJUaWDfONnH7KT4CRLKzF%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17098efb-8dd3-459e-be7d-c2ae3ccf7593&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d76c22b8&sv=2)

*   On the _Create a New Wallet_ page, select **Restore from mnemonics** or other import method.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FBdJSR2mKwPDimnyh4aN9%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D60b93ad8-e9cf-4d8d-a3f3-985d1f35beb0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4a8a6b73&sv=2)

Example: Importing via Mnemonics:

*   Step 1: Select the wallet type. If not listed, choose **Other Wallet**.
    
*   Step 2: Enter your mnemonic phrase. Make sure each word is spelled correctly and separated properly.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FZBWLbpb3lGQGwwaoVu9W%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f28ea44-a77d-4079-9c94-650d4b0ef4cd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74a5c255&sv=2)

*   Step 3: Confirm the account you want to restore and click **Continue**. Done!
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-recovery-and-key-concepts#how-to-recover-your-wallet-if-you-forgot-to-back-up-your-seed-phrase-or-private-key)

How to Recover Your Wallet If You Forgot to Back Up Your Seed Phrase or Private Key

If your UniSat extension wallet won’t open, and you didn’t save your seed phrase or private key, but the browser and extension have not been deleted, there is still a recovery option using local files.

> ✅ You must still remember your wallet password for this method to work.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-recovery-and-key-concepts#step-by-step-recovery)

Step-by-Step Recovery:

1.  Locate Extension Files
    

Find the UniSat extension folder named: ppbibelpcjmhbdihakflkdcoccbgbkpo **For Google Chrome:**

*   **Windows Path:**
    

C:\\Users\\<Username>\\AppData\\Local\\Google\\Chrome\\User Data\\Default\\Local Extension Settings\\ppbibelpcjmhbdihakflkdcoccbgbkpo

*   **macOS Path:**
    

/Users/<Username>/Library/Application Support/Google/Chrome/Default/Local Extension Settings/ppbibelpcjmhbdihakflkdcoccbgbkpo

1.  Important - Back Up the Folder⚠️
    

**Before proceeding with any recovery steps, make sure to back up the entire folder** `**ppbibelpcjmhbdihakflkdcoccbgbkpo**` **to a safe backup location.**

_Do not skip this step — if this folder is lost or deleted before backup, your wallet data cannot be recovered._

1.  Reinstall UniSat Extension
    

*   Open Chrome and uninstall the current UniSat extension.
    
*   Reinstall it from https://unisat.io/download
    
*   Do **not** create a new wallet.
    
*   Close the browser completely.
    

1.  Restore Extension Files
    

*   Reopen the extension data folder location.
    
*   Delete the created `ppbibelpcjmhbdihakflkdcoccbgbkpo` folder.
    
*   Replace it with your backed-up version just now.
    

1.  Open the Extension and Log In
    

*   Launch Chrome.
    
*   Open the UniSat extension.
    
*   Enter your **original wallet password**.
    

If everything is done correctly, your wallet should be restored.

Browsers like Brave and Edge follow a similar approach, for example:

C:\\Users...\\AppData\\Local\\BraveSoftware\\Brave-Browser\\User Data\\Default\\Local Extension Settings\\ppbibelpcjmhbdihakflkdcoccbgbkpo

C:\\Users...\\AppData\\Local\\Microsoft\\Edge\\User Data\\Default\\Local Extension Settings\\ppbibelpcjmhbdihakflkdcoccbgbkpo

> ⚠️ Disclaimer: This recovery method is provided as a last resort. Always back up your seed phrase and private key.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-recovery-and-key-concepts#final-reminders)

Final Reminders

*   Always back up your seed phrase or private key when you create a wallet.
    
*   Store backups offline and in multiple secure locations.
    
*   Never share your recovery details with anyone.
    

Wallet safety is your responsibility. A few minutes of careful backup can save your assets from permanent loss.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-recovery-and-key-concepts#disclaimer)

# How to Manage Your UniSat Wallet | UniSat

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-manage-your-unisat-wallet#download-and-update-unisat-wallet)

Download & Update UniSat Wallet

Always make sure you are using the latest version of UniSat Wallet.

👉 Download here: [https://unisat.io/downloadarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/download)

To create a new wallet, follow this step-by-step guide:

👉 [https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-walletarrow-up-right](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-create-unisat-wallet)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-manage-your-unisat-wallet#how-to-switch-address-types)

How to Switch Address Types

UniSat supports **4 types of addresses**, and all of them can send, receive, and store BTC, Ordinals, Runes, and Alkanes.To switch:

*   On the Wallet homepage, click the ⚙ (Settings).
    
*   Select **Address Type** and choose your preferred type.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FnhdtK1aHPjtTCYYpQgIp%252Fceaf1f4c-0207-45d7-97f3-c83339b1a4b4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a7886b6-7c72-4275-a4d2-a5434506a885&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=143c7edf&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-manage-your-unisat-wallet#how-to-view-secret-recovery-phrase-private-keys)

How to View Secret Recovery Phrase / Private Keys

**View Secret Recovery Phrase**

*   On the wallet homepage, click **HD Wallet**.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FYtBHbPX2RbEqtavgWtLE%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8002f79-48d4-4ad7-b5d4-44549090b4d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f3365c56&sv=2)

*   Go to Wallet Management, select the wallet you want, click the ⚙ icon, and enter your login password.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fru9K9AXOM9tabmWH3f0N%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e6e83ef-7799-4059-a0ba-0a5df2e1c937&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=41853325&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F75AeCcI6mIqrLUvEMkev%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a2f601c-b540-4509-b43d-c548d6218114&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=53e60026&sv=2)

After that, you will be able to see your mnemonic phrase information.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FXuwjtMCy5RTPmyDZnNv5%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01f4bd64-5638-411d-bb6b-40ce469198d1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=439db7b7&sv=2)

_⚠️ Important:_

*   _If you lose your Secret Recovery Phrase, your assets will be gone._
    
*   _If you share your Secret Recovery Phrase, your assets will be stolen._
    
*   _Keep it safe — it’s your sole responsibility_
    

**View / Export Private Key**

*   On the extension wallet homepage, click the address bar. You’ll see the **Address Detail** page.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FS7oZIHNiCjlMBYjMKGIB%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc181798e-a839-4b95-81bb-5479d9636136&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a22e44c7&sv=2)

*   Click the ··· (options) next to your account. Here you can:
    
    *   Edit account name
        
    *   Copy address
        
    *   **View / Export Private Key**
        
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FBt7zzvvZFHoogDLVKvF5%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db65180ac-3ad4-409e-974e-c7c072432a1d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=869047bb&sv=2)

*   Click **Export Private Key**, enter your password, and your private key will be displayed.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FR4mKaBLIBjfBDM2w8mBj%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad972ba8-e2b6-4f43-a494-85ac8f7d298c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2b539eec&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-manage-your-unisat-wallet#q-imported-wallet-addresses-dont-match-my-old-ones.-what-should-i-do)

Q: Imported wallet addresses don’t match my old ones. What should I do?

1.  Double-check your mnemonic phrase is correct.
    
2.  One mnemonic = one HD wallet. Inside, you can create multiple accounts (Account 1, 2, 3). By default, only Account 1 is restored. Try adding more accounts.
    
3.  Each account has its own private key. Export accordingly.
    
4.  Imported address type defaults to **Native SegWit**. Switch to the address type you need (e.g., Taproot).
    
5.  If you previously set a **Custom HD Path or Passphrase**, you must input the same one during recovery. If forgotten, recovery won’t be possible.
    
6.  Still not working? On Step 3, click **Scan in More Addresses** to attempt recovery.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F7cTyOD8pwgTyxaiLi6p5%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e49db09-2402-44e7-9569-7dfe2f3c5f69&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=40ffc30d&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/how-to-manage-your-unisat-wallet#q-what-if-i-forgot-my-wallet-password)

Q: What If I Forgot My Wallet Password?

UniSat does not store or transmit your wallet password. If you've forgotten it: You can restore the wallet using your seed phrase. During the restoration, you can set a new password.

If you don’t have the seed phrase, unfortunately, there is no way to reset or recover the password.

# Best Practices for Safety | UniSat

By staying informed and following these guidelines, you can significantly reduce the risk of falling victim to scams and malicious activities in the cryptocurrency space. Remember, your wallet’s security is ultimately in your hands, so take the necessary precautions to keep your funds safe.

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#avoid-malicious-websites-and-scammers)

**Avoid malicious websites and scammers**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We’d like to make sure you’re aware of common scams and phishing attempts, so you can be ready if you ever encounter them. Most scams use similar tricks, often trying to get your private information to access your cryptocurrency. Stay vigilant!

*   **Beware of Unsolicited Messages** Be cautious about clicking on links received via Discord, Telegram, email, or other social media, especially if they are unsolicited. Scammers often use phishing emails or messages to trick users into visiting malicious websites. If you receive an unexpected communication, verify its legitimacy with UniSat Wallet’s official channels. **UniSat staff will never message you directly.**
    
*   **UniSat & UniSat staff will never ask for your secret recovery phrase or private key.**
    
*   **Double-Check URLs** Always verify the legitimacy of the websites you visit. Scammers often create fake websites that mimic official platforms. Before entering any sensitive information, double-check the URL for spelling mistakes or unusual characters. Official UniSat Wallet websites will always use secure protocols like HTTPS.
    
*   **Verify Announcements** Scammers may create fake announcements that appear to come from official sources. Before taking any action based on an announcement, verify its authenticity by cross-referencing with UniSat Wallet’s official channels.
    
*   **Educate Yourself** Stay informed about common scams and phishing techniques prevalent in the cryptocurrency space. Knowledge is your first line of defense. Familiarize yourself with the typical tactics scammers use, such as fake websites, phishing emails, and fraudulent announcements.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#official-channels)

Official Channels

Ensuring the safety of your UniSat Wallet is our top priority. Unfortunately, scammers and impersonators are on the rise, attempting to deceive users and compromise their assets. To safeguard your funds, it's crucial to only interact with our verified and official channels.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#verified-organization-on-x-yellow-checkmark)

**Verified Organization on X (Yellow checkmark)**

UniSat has been verified as an organization on X, and you can easily identify us by the yellow checkmark associated with our name. This verification serves as a stamp of authenticity, assuring you that you are engaging with the legitimate UniSat organization.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#exclusive-support-channel-on-discord)

**Exclusive Support Channel on Discord**

When it comes to seeking assistance, the only official channel for customer service is the support ticket system on our Discord server. Beware of individuals reaching out to you through other means, especially DMs or external platforms, claiming to be UniSat support.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#safety-tips)

Safety Tips

You should never share your recovery phrase or private key with anyone. Follow these rules to stay safe:

*   Install the official UniSat Wallet browser extension and avoid installing a fake extension.
    
*   UniSat & UniSat staff will never ask for your secret recovery phrase or private key. UniSat staff will never message you directly first.
    
*   Never enter your private key or secret recovery phrase on any website unless you know what you are doing.
    
*   Avoid interacting with suspicious websites using UniSat Wallet browser extension.
    
*   Keep your UniSat Wallet browser extension up-to-date.
    
*   There is no UniSat Airdrop. Don't trust airdrop or giveaway messages. If you’re unsure you can ask our staff about your concerns in discord or twitter.
    
*   Keep your system security/anti-virus updated so your wallet keys do not get compromised.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#keep-your-secret-recovery-phrase-secure)

Keep your Secret Recovery Phrase secure


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

UniSat Wallet is used to sign transactions when interacting with the Bitcoin blockchain, as well as to store your BRC-20s, NFTs, and other kinds of inscriptions. You receive a 12-word Secret Recovery Phrase when you first create your wallet. It provides access to all the addresses within your wallet. You should never share your secret recovery phrase or private key with anyone.

UniSat Wallet does not control any of your personal or private data on servers. Your wallet data is encrypted in your browser and guarded with your UniSat Wallet password.

When you lose password access to your accounts and need to restore them, you can only do that with your Secret Recovery Phrase. So keep your Secret Recovery Phrase safe and secure!

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/unisat-wallet-safety-guide-protecting-your-assets/best-practices-for-safety#protect-yourself-on-discord)

Protect yourself on Discord


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users are increasingly being targeted by scammers and impersonators on Discord. Here's what you can do to increase your safety on Discord. We recommend you adjust the following Discord settings to reduce risks.

*   **Turn off server-specific DMs:** Right-click on a **server icon > Privacy Settings** to allow or disallow direct messages from users of that particular server. Turn it off for large public servers such as UniSat Discord.
    
*   **Turn off DMs:** In user **settings > Privacy & Safety**, you can control who can send you direct messages. Consider turning them off by default for added security.
    
*   **Enable 2-Factor Authentication (2FA):** In **user settings > My Account, s**croll down and set up both an authentication app and SMS authentication. Download your backup codes for 2-FA access in case of emergencies.
    
*   **Verify User Identities:** Right-click a user's profile > Copy ID, verify the ID with the server's staff to confirm the identity. If in doubt, reach out to us via our official channels.
    

By following these tips and staying vigilant, you can protect yourself from scammers and enjoy your time on Discord. Remember, it's always better to be cautious than sorry!

# UniSat Drops | UniSat

*   **What is UniSat Drops**
    

Drops is our way to show our love for Art on Bitcoin and to say thank you to the community by awarding benefits based on Proof of Contribution.

Drops creatively uses UniSat Titles as eligibility to participate so creators can get maximum exposure to UniSat Title holders who represent the most active and significant contributors to the bitcoin community!

*   **What is UniSat Title**
    

UniSat Titles are your personal collection of digital medals that celebrate your journey in the UniSat community!

Each title marks a moment in time when you’ve helped make Bitcoin grow and thrive. As you collect more Titles, you'll unlock exciting new ways to earn benefits from UniSat and our partners, starting with UniSat Drops. More titles will be released as our community continues to grow.

*   **What is Drops Pool**
    

Each Drops Pool contains rewards provided by a Bitcoin project, and has a designated start and end time. Eligible community members can enter the raffle to win rewards for each Pool.

*   **How are winners selected?**
    

Winners are determined by a completely randomized algorithm after the raffle period ends.

The last 6 characters of the latest block hash on Bitcoin or Fractal network is used as a random seed to determine the winner addresses fairly. If the project is issued on Bitcoin, the latest block hash on Bitcoin one hour after the raffle ended will be used.

*   **Which networks do UniSat Drops Support?**
    

UniSat Drops currently supports Bitcoin and Fractal networks.

*   **How to participate in Drops.**
    

1.  Visit [https://unisat.io/dropsarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/drops)
     or navigate to the Drops Icon on the top right hand.
    
2.  Check eligibility: Connect your wallet to check eligibility to participate in pools
    
3.  Join raffle: Click Join Raffle.
    
4.  Raffle results: Raffle results will be announced after raffle ends. You will receive a pop-up notification if you are a winner. You can view all winner addresses under ‘Raffle Winners.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fj1s8fDoWrPQQSQAHjVC0%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6960a5b-96aa-4948-a2fa-3aa834afd2ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eaeb03e5&sv=2)

*   **How to submit your project for Drops**
    

You may reach out to us via [this form for collaborationarrow-up-right](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/11jS_Z3BJ5S7bLemqf12O6PLmTl9ds-OwAAcJuWEz1lQ/edit)
.

# FB Farming | UniSat

UniSat introduces **FB Farming**, a revolutionary native ecosystem incentive program on Fractal Bitcoin that's fully open-sourced and secured by Taproot script.

This feature rewards long-term FB holders while driving sustainable ecosystem growth, with rewards provided by the UniSat team, and bonus rewards **1,000,000 FB** from the Fractal Treasury.

**FB Farming goes live September 29th** with Farming Pool 1, capped at 1 million FB capacity.

Participants can stake for different periods to receive corresponding incentives. These incentives can be further enhanced through the use of Gems. Actual rewards are subject to the activity settlement rules and do not constitute any guarantee or promise.

*   Explore FB Farming [https://fractal.unisat.io/farmingarrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/farming)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming#what-makes-fb-farming-special)

**✨ What Makes FB Farming Special**

FB Farming stands out with unmatched **flexibility and user control**:

*   🔓 **No On-Chain Time Lock** - Unstake whenever
    
*   📊 **Partial Unstaking** - Withdraw what you need, keep the rest active
    
*   ⚡ **Zero Freeze Period** - Immediate access to your funds
    
*   📈 **Real-Time Calculations** - Live APY and rewards tracking.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming#how-fb-farming-works)

🔧 How FB Farming Works

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming#rewards-system)

**💰 Rewards System**

*   **Tier-Based APY**: Unlock higher APY tiers the longer you stake.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FIrJ5M5IRpyJmY2gDLJGH%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05452153-cf6a-45c7-b377-7dd93a1f7c8c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=93535c88&sv=2)

1.  **Choose** unstaking amount (full or partial)
    
2.  **Calculate** - System computes your obtained rewards
    
3.  **Sign** transaction to confirm
    
4.  **Receive** - Get your principal + rewards instantly

# Fractal Bitcoin | UniSat

Fractal Bitcoin is the only Bitcoin scaling solution that uses the Bitcoin Core code itself to recursively scale unlimited layers on top of the world’s most-secure and-held blockchain. UniSat, as one of the core contributors to Fractal Bitcoin, participates in the development and maintenance of its core infrastructure — supporting Fractal’s sustainable growth and long-term stability.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin#fractal-bitcoin-a-truly-native-scaling-solution)

Fractal Bitcoin - A truly native scaling solution

Fractal is the first instance of a virtualization methodology applied to Bitcoin in the world. Fractal gradually extends the Bitcoin blockchain into a scalable computing system without breaking consistency with the Bitcoin main chain.

*   **Native**
    
    Recursive scaling of Bitcoin Core code itself — without any foreign constructs — ensures consistent and unlimited scaling, and native support of current infrastructure (e.g. wallets).
    
*   **Fast**
    
    Block confirmation times are 30 seconds or less, with 20x increase in capacity per layer.
    
*   **Dynamic Scaling**
    
    On-chain interactions can scale up and down as demand changes; it acts as a dynamic “blockspace load balancer” and reduces congestion on any specific layer. This enables internet-scale applications on the Bitcoin blockchain, as has never been done before.
    
*   **Consistent**
    
    Due to each layer’s self-replicating consistency with the main chain, on-chain consensus is preserved. Any layer’s transactions/hashes can be traced back to the source on the Bitcoin chain, without the risks of forks or shards involved.
    
*   **Easy**
    
    Additionally, due to this consistency across layers, assets can be directly transferred from layer to another without the need for additional relays.
    

Learn more: [https://fractalbitcoin.io/fractal-primerarrow-up-right](https://fractalbitcoin.io/fractal-primer)

# How to merge Runes / Alkanes / BTC / FB? | UniSat

The Merge function in the UniSat UTXO Management Tool helps consolidate multiple fragmented UTXOs into a single UTXO, making your asset structure more efficient and easier to manage.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-merge-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#supported-merge-scenarios)

**Supported Merge Scenarios**

*   **Alkanes**: Custom merge up to 500 Alkanes UTXOs UTXOinto a single .
    
*   **Runes**: Custom merge up to 500 Runes UTXOs into a single UTXO.
    
*   **BTC**(on Bitcoin) / **FB** (on Fractal): Merge up to 500 UTXOs into a single UTXO.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-merge-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#how-to-merge-your-utxos)

**How to Merge** Your **UTXOs？**

In this guide, we will use Merging Alkanes UTXOs as an example. The merging process for Runes, Alkanes, and BTC/FB is generally similar, with slight differences based on the asset type. Please refer to the specific merge interface for each asset.

**Visit:** [https://unisat.io/utxoarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/utxo)

**⚠ Always double-check all details before confirming.**

**⚠ Only UTXOs of the same asset type and same asset name can be merged.**

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F4izp44d6PTgsrElSh2KO%252Fmerge.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54b1616c-e756-462e-abcc-7afa6dd43706&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e761c98e&sv=2)

# Inscribing brc-20 and Runes in a single transaction | UniSat

UniSat supports inscribing brc-20 and Runes in a single transaction! This means you can inscribe Runes alongside brc-20 in a more cost-efficient way compared to inscribing them separately.

**How is this achieved?**

Whether you are inscribing a BRC-20 ticker or making a regular BTC transfer, any Bitcoin transaction with an OP\_RETURN data size of 16 bytes or more will automatically mint a runes ticker.

In other words, if the fee rate is 1 sat/vB, the minting cost of 1 runes ticker is 16 sats because of the 16 bytes OP\_RETURN data.

**What's new?**

*   Simultaneously inscribe BRC-20 and Runes in one UTXO
    
*   Save on inscribing fees
    
*   Faster & more efficient inscribing
    
*   On both Bitcoin and Fractal mainnet
    

**What are the potential drawbacks?**

If you mint 1000 A brc-20 tickers for instance, you will also generate 1,000 B runes tickers, each associated with a separate UTXO. If you do not consolidate these B tickers later, you will only be able to sell them one by one.

Additionally, since BRC-20 tokens and Runes tokens exist within the same UTXO, some applications may have difficulty distinguishing between them, potentially leading to asset misidentification and loss.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FYUHk6S1umfIJU54Wzkoj%252Fmut.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2efac2c0-b4b2-40a0-ab3e-cad95dc2ce22&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=13a665e5&sv=2)

# Advanced Features | UniSat

UniSat Inscribe introduces new advanced features for Ordinals creators and degens

*   **Parent/Child Provenance**: Link parent-child inscriptions
    
*   **Delegate**: Save fees when minting copies of an inscription
    
*   **Metadata**: Add metadata to your inscriptions
    
*   **Pointer**: Choose the exact satoshi/utxo you mint on
    

UniSat Inscribe: [https://unisat.io/inscribearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/inscribe)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe/advanced-features#parent-child-provenance)

**Parent/Child Provenance**

Enable the Parent/Child toggle to mint “child” inscriptions linked directly to a parent you own, establishing **on-chain provenance** that verifies their origin.

*   Trustlessly establish the provenance of child inscriptions
    
*   Children and parent inscriptions can used in the same collection
    

Learn more about Parent/Child Provenance: [https://docs.ordinals.com/inscriptions/provenance.htmlarrow-up-right](https://docs.ordinals.com/inscriptions/provenance.html)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FVe21zJUBXxZsaV4vW1kd%252Fparents.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d974386-05a8-4ee0-88d5-c0f5dd84b074&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3f3b62fb&sv=2)

* * *

**🎨 Delegate: Save big when mass-minting copies!**

Delegate lets you create copies of an inscription easily by nominating a “delegate” (the original copy). Imagine repeat-minting 1000 images in one go!

It save storing content for each inscription and therefore saves fees too! Requests for the content of an inscription with a delegate will instead return the content, content type and content encoding of the delegate.

ICYDK, UniSat OG pass collection was minted with this method! This helped us save big on fees.

Learn more about Delegate : [https://docs.ordinals.com/inscriptions/delegate.htmlarrow-up-right](https://docs.ordinals.com/inscriptions/delegate.html)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FAfsUQYH1lbNfYqQjrfNB%252Fdele.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07d06002-bb1f-4f7a-bf6a-b4413f20f945&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4cacb97b&sv=2)

* * *

**📝 Metadata**

Metadata option lets you add metadata to your inscriptions using CBOR format when inscribing.

You can now attach rich, human-readable info like Name and Traits to your inscriptions！

*   Great for NFT and game assets creators.
    
*   More details about Metadata: [https://docs.ordinals.com/inscriptions/metadata.htmlarrow-up-right](https://docs.ordinals.com/inscriptions/metadata.html)
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FL0qEm7wwxFvTlBWwiNcg%252Fmeta%2520%281%29.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De15d0f03-039c-439b-ad6f-b936d19898ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab2fcf51&sv=2)

* * *

**📍 Pointer: Choose Your Sats!**

With the Pointer option, you can choose exactly which utxo or sats (satoshi) your inscription gets minted on, like rare sats!

*   This gives builders more control over sats
    
*   This can be used to create multiple inscriptions in a single transaction on different sats
    

Learn more about pointer: [https://docs.ordinals.com/inscriptions/pointer.htmlarrow-up-right](https://docs.ordinals.com/inscriptions/pointer.html)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fhj8JN53DGgreVeLK5hpS%252Fpointer.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D27c4e5d4-6717-4d3e-8004-a83afecc7e53&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=568a666c&sv=2)

# How to unlock/lock inscription/Runes/Alkanes/ utxo and send as normal BTC in All UTXO Tab | UniSat

The **Lock** function in UniSat UTXO Management Tool allows you to prevent specific UTXOs from being accidentally used in transactions. The **Unlock** function lets you reverse this, making the UTXOs available again for normal operations.

Locking is helpful for protecting assets, reserving UTXOs for specific use cases, or managing wallet behavior.

UniSat UTXO Management Tool: [https://unisat.io/utxo arrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/utxo)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fbp2IXgTh3Hjj02XYhuY2%252Flock.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4f1aaa5-350e-46f9-9ace-c4066b6dd057&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6369c2d3&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-unlock-lock-inscription-runes-alkanes-utxo-and-send-as-normal-btc-in-all-utxo-tab#how-to-unlock-inscription-runes-alkanes-utxo-and-send-as-normal-btc-in-all-utxo-tab)

How to unlock inscription/runes/Alkanes/ utxo and send as normal BTC in All UTXO Tab?

_**📌 Unlock with care**_

_**UTXOs with brc-20, ordinals NFT, Alkanes or Runes assets are treated as BTC after unlocking — you may burn valuable assets if mistakenly select the wrong UTXO.**_

**📌 First please be 100% sure you don't want to keep these assets "inscriptions, Runes, Alkanes" at all, because once you unlock and send, you will lose these assets.**

Here, we use inscription as an example (The process for Ordinals, Runes, Alkanes, and BTC is similar, with slight differences based on asset type. Please refer to the specific interface for each asset.)

1\. select the related utxos and then unlock.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FLNoXddIpEEwt2cqnpOuu%252F31.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8dad628f-7f57-4ce6-a20b-a3429dc23f8b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3726baba&sv=2)

2\. You need to confirm and sign in wallet to finish unlocking.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FF8QaGJWa7Cx5P0u15FlF%252F32.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9d40683-d2ca-4273-8a1c-76a3bd5a0561&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f87bfd80&sv=2)

3\. Then you could see these two utxos being unlocked. Then select them and click Send.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FLimYHDwffMw0zxcrpJLn%252F33.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D774e66a6-c3f8-4f26-87ea-b029722c10cd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b1f6271&sv=2)

1.  There is a Notice that pops out because these utxos are less than 600 sats, to protect your assets, we need you to confirm again, if be sure, you could click Next to continue.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FvD0v1KLU6nCETzUf6eCQ%252F34.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac1d0d3d-23fe-4f86-8c51-66df05ac65f7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c268e1e0&sv=2)

1.  Then you could enter Recipient and Amount, custom fee rate and confirm. In Sign page of wallet, you could see it lists these two utxos as Inputs.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FIa3tg6uCPlSGrP0OMMeo%252F35.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4cc8414c-63ad-41a8-92aa-75a05c62b8b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=17b0a0b5&sv=2)

*   **Note:**
    
    *   After manually unlocking and spending a UTXO with assets, it needs to be unlocked again before the next spend.
        
    *   UTXOs with less than 600 sats, once unlocked, can only be merged or sent through the UTXO Management Tool. The wallet will not automatically select UTXOs below 600 sats for spending.
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-unlock-lock-inscription-runes-alkanes-utxo-and-send-as-normal-btc-in-all-utxo-tab#how-to-lock-inscription-runes-alkanes-utxo-and-send-as-normal-btc-in-all-utxo-tab)

How to lock inscription/Runes/Alkanes/ utxo and send as normal BTC in All UTXO Tab?

Here, we use Alkanes assets as an example (The process for Ordinals, Runes, Alkanes, and BTC is similar, with slight differences based on asset type. Please refer to the specific interface for each asset.)

**⚠ Always double-check before pressing that confirm button!**

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FuOFUg4E0DVf5j6cO7iEp%252Flock.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De71bf49d-4ab7-4406-ae4a-6912840c2c89&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3980fcb&sv=2)

# UniHexa | UniSat

UniHexa reimagines Bitcoin trading by combining the efficiency of CEX-like trading with the security and self-custody of DEX experience.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unihexa#trading-experience-cex--dex-in-one)

**⚡ Trading experience: CEX + DEX in One**

**🔸 CEX-like Experience**

*   Support for all Bitcoin assets and cross-protocol trading
    
*   Set your price/direction; UniHexa handles order-matching instantly
    
*   Unmatched orders auto-convert to listed orders on the orderbook market
    
*   You can access and edit your orders at any given time
    
*   Liquidity thrives with active market makers
    

**🔸 DEX-like self-custody**

*   Every single order is committed onto blockchain before it gets matched.
    
*   Fully non-custodial, peer-to-peer trading.
    
*   Pair with non-custodial wallets like UniSat Wallet for the ultimate decentralized experience.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unihexa#security-and-transparency-by-design)

**🔐 Security & transparency by design**

*   Every transaction committed to blockchain and verifiable as it should be.
    
*   Full orderbook in mempool. No compromises.
    
*   Permissionless access for all.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unihexa#comprehensive-coverage-of-assets-and-protocols)

**🌐 Comprehensive coverage of assets and protocols**

*   Protocol-agnostic: brc-20, Runes, Alkanes, Ordinals, and top 100 Bitcoin assets (ranked on UniSat Marketplace).
    
*   Works alongside Oyl AMM (Alkanes-native swaps) and InSwap (instant swaps) to provide users with choice between price execution and instant liquidity.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unihexa#leverage-the-power-of-fractal-bitcoin)

**📍 Leverage the power of Fractal Bitcoin**

*   Fractal Bitcoin is used as the infrastructure for UniHexa (Fractal-as-a-Service)
    
*   Built for optimal performance: 20x blockspace, 30s confirmation time
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unihexa#development-status)

Currently in invite-only beta testing with select community members. Feedback-driven iteration to ensure stability, usability, and scalability.

Next stop: Bitcoin Mainnet. Pleases Stay tuned.
