# Runes on Fractal | UniSat

Runes on Fractal follows the same set of rules as the Bitcoin mainnet. If you're familiar with the runes protocol on Bitcoin, you'll find that the structure and functionalities on Fractal are fully aligned with it. Here's what you need to know:

**1\. Same Rules as Bitcoin Mainnet**

The Runes protocol on Fractal follows the same fundamental rules as on Bitcoin, with all phases completed within one halving cycle (it takes 4 years on Bitcoin, and takes 2 years on Fractal)

There are 12 phases on both networks. Therefore, any single phase takes 120 days on Bitcoin, and 60 days on Fractal.

**2\. Ticker Names on Fractal**

On the Fractal mainnet, all Runes tickers are displayed in **lowercase** letters.

For more detailed information on the Runes protocol, you can refer to the official documentation here: [Runes Protocol Documentationarrow-up-right](https://docs.ordinals.com/runes.html)
.

**Disclaimer:**

The content of this document is for informational purposes only. It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. Digital assets (including FTs and NFTs) are subject to market volatility, involve high risk, regulatory changes, and may depreciate in value. The information is provided "as is," and we make no warranties regarding its accuracy. Please consult your legal, tax, or investment professionals to determine whether trading or holding digital assets is suitable for you.

# UniSat Marketplace | UniSat

UniSat Marketplace is a decentralized marketplace that makes it easy and secure to trade and manage Bitcoin-native assets, including brc-20, Ordinals, Runes, and Alkanes. Since launching in 2023, UniSat has become a trusted, open-source tool known for its user-first approach, competitive fees, and seamless integration across the Bitcoin and Fractal network.

Whether you're looking to trade your first brc-20 tickers, Runes, or Alkanes, or securely manage your Bitcoin assets, UniSat Marketplace provides the tools and infrastructure to make it simpler, cheaper, and smoother.

UniSat Marketplace: [https://unisat.io/marketarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/market)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/more-products/unisat-marketplace#key-features-of-the-unisat-marketplace)

Key Features of the UniSat Marketplace

*   **Multi-Protocol Asset Support - Ordinals, Runes, Alkanes Assets:** Trade and manage Ordinals, brc-20 tickers, Runes, Alkanes, Names, and Collections—all fully compliant with Bitcoin mainnet standards. No third-party bridges or custodians required.
    
*   **Decentralized & Non-Custodial:** UniSat never stores your mnemonic phrases or private keys. All trades are signed directly via your wallet, giving you full control over your assets.
    
*   **Low & Competitive Fees:** Enjoy just 0.5% service fees for trading brc-20 tickers, Runes, Alkanes, Names, and Collections, ensuring cost-effective market participation. Small orders may even qualify for zero fees—see detailed [fee info](https://docs.unisat.io/products/more-products/unisat-marketplace/unisat-marketplace-fee-rates)
     for more.
    
*   **Seamless Integration:** Compatible with UniSat Wallet, OKX Wallet, Magic Eden Wallet, Xverse, and more and supports switching between Bitcoin and Fractal marketplaces in one click, making transactions and operations more convenient. Deeply integrated with UniSat Wallet, UniScan, Inscribe service, and InSwap, making advanced operations and data access more convenient.
    
*   **Developer-Friendly:** All trading, listing, and indexing logic follows open protocols. With our [public APIs](https://docs.unisat.io/developer-support/unisat-open-api)
    , developers can freely build custom tools or marketplaces without permission.
    
*   **User-Centric Experience:** Clean UI with one-click listing and buying, real-time asset rankings, and automatic UTXO management. Powered by PSBT for enhanced security and flexibility. We continuously improve the experience based on community feedback.
    

UniSat Marketplace is your gateway to exploring Bitcoin-native assets—secure, efficient, and always improving based on community feedback.

# How to reclaim BTC/FB trapped in useless inscription UTXOs | UniSat

UniSat UTXO Management Tool: [https://unisat.io/utxo arrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/utxo)

Consolidate ready-combined useless (mint and transfer) inscriptions in one click.

*   We filter out ‘useless’ brc-20 mint & transfer UTXOs—so you can turn them into BTC/FB with one-click.
    
*   Never worry about selecting the wrong UTXOs or burning valuable assets.
    
*   Clear overview of selected UTXO value, and claimable UTXO value after gas fee deduction.
    

_**Tips: Lower fee = more BTC in your pocket! Consolidating is optimal when network fees are <3 sats/vB!**_

UniSat provides FREE consolidations up to **3000 UTXOs** each month with activities to get more!

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FcuURqNpm3Y9msENeUSbh%252Fcosutxo.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82c52494-aa5f-4a50-ad66-ea6e888bdd63&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ead5823b&sv=2)

# UniSat Inscribe | UniSat

UniSat Inscribe is a powerful and user-friendly tool designed for creators, developers, and users to seamlessly inscribe. Supporting both Bitcoin and Fractal networks, UniSat offers full compatibility with multiple inscription standards—including Ordinals (brc-20, text, files, names) and Runes (mint and etch)—for a secure and efficient inscription experience.

🔗 [https://unisat.io/inscribearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/inscribe)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#why-use-unisat-inscribe)

Why Use UniSat Inscribe?

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#id-1.-multi-protocol-support-and-diverse-inscribing-types)

1\. Multi-Protocol Support & Diverse Inscribing Types

**On Bitcoin:**

*   Ordinals Mint & Deploy
    
    *   4-byte brc-20 tickers & 5-byte brc-20 tickers
        
    *   Inscribing types
        
        *   **brc-20**
            
        *   **Text**
            
        *   **Files:** Including `.jpg`, `.webp`, `.png`, `.gif`, `.txt`, `.mp3`, `.mp4 (H.264)`, and more.
            
        *   **Names:** Including `sats`, `xbt`, `unisat`, `ord`, `btc`, `gm`, and `uniworlds`
            
        
    
*   Runes Mint & Etch
    

**On Fractal:**

*   Ordinals Mint & Deploy
    
    *   **brc-20**
        
    *   **Text**
        
    *   **Files:** Including `.jpg`, `.webp`, `.png`, `.gif`, `.txt`, `.mp3`, `.mp4 (H264)`, and more.
        
    *   **Names:** Including `fb`
        
    
*   Runes Mint & Etch
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#id-2.-batch-minting-capabilities)

2\. Batch Minting Capabilities

UniSat allows up to **1,000 brc-20 or Runes items** in a single batch order on Bitcoin. Users can:

*   Use **Repeat mint** up to 1,000 items in a single transaction.
    
*   Upload multiple files or datasets for batch inscription.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#id-3.-file-size-and-format-limits)

3\. File Size & Format Limits

*   **Maximum file size (per file):** 365 KB
    
*   **Total size per batch:** 10M. UniSat automatically validates file types and size. Unsupported formats or oversized files will be rejected.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#id-4.-affordable-and-transparent-fees)

4\. **Affordable & Transparent Fees**

UniSat Inscribe offers service fees below market average, helping you reduce inscription costs more effectively. Before isncribing, you can customize your network fee, and the system will provide real-time cost estimates based on your selected rate—ensuring both priority and cost-efficiency in your transactions.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#id-5.-advanced-inscription-features)

5\. Advanced Inscription Features

UniSat Inscribe supports advanced minting capabilities:

*   Parent/Child Provenance
    
*   Delegate
    
*   Metadata
    
*   Reinscription
    
*   Combined brc-20 and Runes minting in a single transaction
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe#id-6.-seamless-integration)

6\. Seamless Integration

UniSat Inscribe is tightly integrated with the UniSat services:

*   UniSat Wallet
    
*   UniScan
    
*   UniSat Marketplace
    
*   InSwap
    

Combined, these tools offer a streamlined, end-to-end experience for managing, tracking, and trading inscriptions.

UniSat Inscribe is built to provide a robust and continuously improving isncribing service, offering diverse and customizable minting options—while ensuring a secure and efficient experience across both Bitcoin and Fractal.

# How to Etch Runes? | UniSat

You may visit [https://fractal.unisat.io/runes/inscribearrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/runes/inscribe)
 to get the page.

Input the parameters as needed.

_**For example**_：

The _**Rune**_ Name is everyone.loves.nature.forever,

_**Symbol**_ is E,

It is _**Mintable**_, and _**Amount**_ was settled as 500, _**Cap**_ for 4,000,000.

The _**Premine**_ is 15,000.

**With Logo** option, select whether to add a logo for Runes.

And leave other fields empty.Then you could input the above needed text as shown below,

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FGbnFRY19zfNEeydTRSiK%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e901ae5-bd13-48c4-b085-273e2ac0f417&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ceb6caf2&sv=2)

_Please note: you need to wait for 5 blocks confirmations for etching._

After the Rune is confirmed as valid, the etcher will get 15000E everyone.loves.nature.forever. Meantime, the others can mint Rune everyone.loves.nature.forever.

Following is the introduction for each parameter:

_**Rune:**_ Runes name, (currently you can etch 13-26 characters long, can be separated by a middle dot ·, and the separator does not count towards the character limit).

_**Symbol (optional):**_ The symbol after the number of runes, which can be A-Z or empty. If empty, a general symbol ¤ will be used.

_**Mintable:**_ Toggle off to disable further minting. Runes are only premine upon creation.

_**Amount:**_ The Amount field contains the amount of runes each mint transaction receives.

_**Cap:**_ The number of times a rune may be minted is its cap. A mint is closed once the cap is reached.

_**Advanced options:**_ Set up premining, divisible figures, and the starting or ending block where minting is possible (optional).

_**Premine :**_ The etcher of a rune may optionally allocate to themselves units of the runes being etched. This allocation is called a premine.

_**Divisibility (optional):**_ A rune's divisibility is how finely it may be divided into its atomic units. Divisibility is expressed as the number of digits permissible after the decimal point in the amount of runes. A rune with divisibility 0 may not be divided. A unit of a rune with divisibility 1 may be divided into ten sub-units, a rune with divisibility 2 may be divided into a hundred, and so on.

_**Absolute Height:**_ The absolute block height (based on the current block height).

_**Relative Height：**_The range of relative block heights (based on the block of etching real).

_**Start Height：**_A mint is open starting in the block with the given start height.

_**End Height：**_A rune may not be minted in or after the block with the given end height.

**Disclaimer:**

The content of this document is for informational purposes only. It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. Digital assets (including FTs and NFTs) are subject to market volatility, involve high risk, regulatory changes, and may depreciate in value. The information is provided "as is," and we make no warranties regarding its accuracy. # Understanding UTXO | UniSat

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#what-is-utxo)

What is UTXO?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

UTXO (Unspent Transaction Output) is a fundamental concept in Bitcoin and many other blockchain networks. It represents the unspent outputs of previous transactions that can be used as inputs for new transactions. Essentially, a UTXO is like a physical cash bill—you can only spend it as a whole, and any leftover balance is returned as change in a new bill (UTXO). This model differs from Ethereum’s account-based model, where balances are updated directly. Unlike traditional bank accounts, where money is summed up into a single balance, Bitcoin transactions require selecting specific UTXOs for spending, similar to using exact change when making a purchase.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#how-utxo-increases-and-decreases)

How UTXO Increases and Decreases?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

UTXOs increase when a Bitcoin transaction generates new outputs. For example, if Alice sends 0.5 BTC to Bob, a new UTXO worth 0.5 BTC is created in Bob’s wallet. If Alice had 1 BTC before the transaction, the remaining balance of 0.5 BTC minus any transaction fees is returned to her as a new UTXO.

Conversely, UTXOs decrease when they are used as inputs in transactions. When Bob later sends 0.2 BTC to Charlie, his 0.5 BTC UTXO is consumed, and two new UTXOs are created: one for Charlie (0.2 BTC) and one as change returned to Bob (0.3 BTC minus fees). This mechanism ensures that all Bitcoin transactions follow a clear and traceable path.

Any Bitcoin transaction, including sending BTC, minting or transferring inscriptions, Runes or BRC-20 tickers, may increase or decrease UTXOs.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#unlocking-utxos-benefits-and-risks)

Unlocking UTXOs: Benefits and Risks


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Many users inscribe inscriptions or mint Runes and BRC-20 tickers, resulting in small UTXOs that hold these assets containing only 546 sats. To prevent these asset-containing UTXOs from being spent as miner fees and leading to asset loss, Bitcoin wallets tend to lock them by default, making them unspendable. You may have some 'useless assets' in UTXOs like BRC-20 mint inscriptions, transfer inscriptions.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#benefits-of-unlocking-utxos)

Benefits of Unlocking UTXOs:

**Immediate Usability**: Once unlocked, these UTXOs can be directly used as Bitcoin for transactions.**User Control**: UniSat wallet allows users to decide whether to unlock specific UTXOs. Before confirming a transaction, the wallet will display whether a UTXO contains a particular asset, enabling informed decision-making.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#risks-of-unlocking-utxos)

Risks of Unlocking UTXOs:

**Potential Asset Loss**: If an unlocked UTXO contains inscriptions, Runes or BRC-20 tickers you wanna hold, it will be spent as regular Bitcoin. This means that if such a UTXO is included in a transaction, the associated assets may be irreversibly sent to the recipient, leading to loss.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#splitting-and-merging-utxos)

Splitting and Merging UTXOs:


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/understanding-utxo#when-to-use-them)

When to Use Them?

Splitting UTXOs involves breaking a large UTXO into smaller ones. This is useful in scenarios such as:

**Enabling Multiple Transactions**: Having smaller UTXOs allows users to initiate multiple transactions simultaneously. This is especially useful for minting inscriptions, Runes or BRC-20 tickers, where users may need to broadcast multiple minting transactions quickly without being stopped by pending(unconfirmed) UTXOs.

**Preventing Asset Mixing**: Users who manage both Bitcoin and Bitcoin ecosystem assets (inscriptions, Runes or BRC-20 tickers) may split UTXOs to keep asset-containing UTXOs separate from pure Bitcoin UTXOs.

Merging UTXOs is the opposite process, where multiple smaller UTXOs are combined into a single larger one. This is beneficial when:

**Reducing Transaction Fees**: Users who have accumulated many small UTXOs (e.g., 546 sats, 1000 sats) from minting inscriptions may find that transactions become costly due to the high number of inputs. Merging these UTXOs reduces the input count and lowers transaction fees.

**Wallet Management**: Consolidating UTXOs into fewer, larger UTXOs makes managing funds more efficient, especially for users frequently engaging with Bitcoin-based assets. You can merge many small UTXOs only containing 546 sats or 1000 sats into a larger one.

**Disclaimer:**

The content of this document is for informational purposes only. It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. Digital assets (including FTs and NFTs) are subject to market volatility, involve high risk, regulatory changes, and may depreciate in value. The information is provided "as is," and we make no warranties regarding its accuracy. Please consult your legal, tax, or investment professionals to determine whether trading or holding digital assets is suitable for you.

# How to Trade on UniSat Marketplace | UniSat

UniSat Marketplace makes it easy to buy and sell Bitcoin-native assets like BRC-20, Runes, Alkanes, Names, and Collections—all in a decentralized, non-custodial way. This guide is for general reference. For the best results, please follow the current UI and make decisions based on your actual needs.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/more-products/unisat-marketplace/how-to-trade-on-unisat-marketplace#step-1-access-the-marketplace)

Step 1: Access the Marketplace

*   Go to the official UniSat website: [https://unisat.ioarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/)
    
*   Click **Marketplace**, or go directly to [https://unisat.io/marketarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/market)
    
*   Connect your wallet
    

> **In this guide, we’ll walk you through the process using brc-20 as an example.**

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FhKiAh2etvSJxvN83gNHO%252Fq.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc07781cd-e92d-46e8-933c-088dae299e39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7b2661a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/more-products/unisat-marketplace/how-to-trade-on-unisat-marketplace#how-to-buy-assets)

How to Buy Assets？

On the homepage, select the **asset category** you want to trade from the top menu (e.g., brc-20, Alkanes, Runes, Collections etc.)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FDf8siZnFWxANWHUZxTk1%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7eff1cb-554f-46eb-a7a8-55a02a062268&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ca131870&sv=2)

1.  Under **brc-20**, browse the ticker leaderboard or use the search bar on the right to find the ticker you want.
    
    _**⚠️ Double-check the ticker name to avoid choosing a similarly named asset.**_
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fgz29O7zBg5GhEvX4K3sy%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b02d12c-9d87-4bf3-a17a-44b7b25f8f5f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=25b69caf&sv=2)

1.  Click on the desired ticker to enter its trading detail page. You can also sort listed orders by price, either from highest to lowest or lowest to highest.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fko0l2aKug8v84bgb7udG%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dedc71eef-3ea5-4886-9e24-cc7666d08713&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3c15753d&sv=2)

1.  View all current listings for that asset. Select the amount and price you prefer and click **Buy**.
    

*   You can also use the slider at the bottom left to batch purchase multiple listings.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FvfNHcdJ9NKePvBZqGVPU%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc692e5c2-9966-4a28-b1b6-9547a5b483f2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bafde1f2&sv=2)

1.  On the order confirmation page, double-check: **ticker name, price, and amount**. Click **Confirm**, complete the wallet signature, and the asset will be yours.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FmgQ2dFxq5DJnQDSdjvJb%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddbbb394d-253d-449c-bdc0-7c4c4829a7db&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d675b8c7&sv=2)

✅ Tip: You can also access Buy options via your **My Assets** page:

*   Go to the "**My Orders**" tab at the top right of the Marketplace homepage.
    
*   Click **Assets** to see your full asset portfolio.
    
*   Select any ticker and click **Buy** to proceed.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FDlQT4BhrSeEXiWB07pHy%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1849f8f8-027c-4870-8b58-70060f6b6175&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=188c5317&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FQ5aoMRh2fRYjfn4f0xJF%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b4b427a-a24c-4cf7-a887-289631300f59&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d0bbbc8&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/more-products/unisat-marketplace/how-to-trade-on-unisat-marketplace#how-to-list-sell-assets)

How to List (Sell) Assets

Go to the [UniSat Marketplace homepagearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/market)
 and connect your wallet.

1.  Click the **yellow icon** labeled **My Assets**.
    

*   In the dropdown, find the brc-20 ticker you want to sell and click **List**.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F690PFv0JzFh3Qmls7c9w%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57769200-b26e-44cd-907d-8a51329352ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9e33058&sv=2)

1.  Select the ticker and click **List** to enter a price.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FzWxzfw6uytE16bfElgML%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4157c5b1-1277-4bc7-a75f-cc512d03231b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d03c323&sv=2)

1.  Set your ideal sell price, then click **List** and confirm the signature.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F0QNh6RJ6dJCTbcz5j5qJ%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd80d32aa-7c8d-4cae-b8f8-6dfe345d12d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ce54a2b&sv=2)

*   _Note: Due to how brc-20 works, you’ll need to inscribe a TRANSFER before listing. If prompted, simply click_ _**Inscribe TRANSFER**_ _as directed on the interface and wait for the inscription to complete before listing._

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/more-products/unisat-marketplace/how-to-trade-on-unisat-marketplace#how-to-update-or-unlist-a-sell-order)

How to Update or Unlist a Sell Order

Go to **My Orders** from the top navigation.

1.  Find the order you want to update or remove.
    
2.  Click **Update** to change the price, or **Unlist** to cancel the listing.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FphsRnbzte4XvsR1pGZKU%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0f7d30f-82fb-401d-b66e-f3ec8f1bf006&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9f351034&sv=2)

# FB Farming FAQ | UniSat

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-faq#q-how-fb-farming-works)

Q: How FB Farming works:

• FB farming has launched on [https://fractal.unisat.io/farmingarrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/farming)

• Any user can stake FB to earn standard APY (1.2%–9.8%), the longer you stake, the higher your APY!

• You can use Gems to boost your APY. Stack up to 2 Gems for a maximum bonus APY of **+37%.**

• You may unstake at any time, staking and bonus rewards calculated based on time staked.

• Each address can stake up to **10,000 FB** per pool.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-faq#q-how-can-i-participate-in-the-farming-event)

**Q: How can I participate in the** Farming **Event?**

**• 1,000,000 FB** in farming bonus for the Fractal‘s Anniversary Carnival, fully funded by the Fractal Treasury.

• During the event period (**Sep 12 to Sep 26, 08:00 UTC**), users can claim **Gems** daily at: [https://fractal.unisat.io/farming/eventsarrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/farming/events)

• When FB Farming goes live, you can use claimed Gems to enhance your farming rewards [https://fractal.unisat.io/farmingarrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/farming)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-faq#q-how-are-fb-farming-rewards-structured)

**Q: How are FB f**arming **rewards structured?**

Refer to: [https://fractal.unisat.io/farmingarrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/farming)

**🔸Base APY**: All farming periods start with a base APY of **1.2%**.

**🔸Farming Tier Bonuses**: Up to **9.8%** depending on duration and amount staked.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FKOii5S6NJVkGF8hGfDbL%252F111.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f15d384-c8c0-40c2-b1ab-aa1113149e76&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=840014fd&sv=2)

**🔸Gem Bonuses**: Up to **+37%** APY.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FywD268p9CmEb03EYMAcE%252F222.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da3b40c76-155e-4e04-bc5c-4fa2d2309590&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16c9f9c8&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-faq#q-what-is-gems)

Q: What is Gems?

Maximum possible APY: **46.8%** (9.8% standard APY+ Gem bonus APY)

1,000,000 FB in bonus rewards will be distributed through Gems during the Carnival.

Gems claim period: Sep 12 - Sep 26.

5 types of Gems are available:

*   7-Day Gem: +25% APY
    
*   30-Day Gem: +12% APY
    
*   90-Day Gem: +7.5% APY
    
*   180-Day Gem: +4.5% APY
    
*   360-Day Gem: +3% APY
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F94JSHybL9IpXF6pbWofj%252F333.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D994c9a0e-e5cd-4b63-8c76-81abbcdeabab&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a90ffc1c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-faq#q-how-do-i-use-gems-to-boost-my-fb-farming)

**Q: How do I use Gems to boost my FB farming?**

*   You can stack **up to 2 Gems at a time** (as long as their bonus APY differs). You can stack more Gems after the first expires.
    
*   Example: For a 30-day stake, you can use one 30-Day Gem + one 7-Day Gem. When the 7-Day Gem expires, you can add another.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-faq#q-who-is-eligible-to-claim-gems)

**Q: Who is eligible to claim Gems?**

*   All users must hold **≥100 FB** in their on-chain wallet to claim Gems (balances on InSwap or exchanges are not counted).
    
*   Regular users can claim **1 Gem** per day.
    
*   Whitelisted users can claim **3 Gems** per day.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-faq#q-can-i-unstake-early-what-happens-to-my-rewards)

**Q: Can I unstake early? What happens to my rewards?**

*   Yes, you may unstake at any time.
    
*   **Base APY (1.2%)** is always earned proportionally based on actual staking time.
    
*   However, **Stacking Tier Bonuses** and **Gem Bonuses** are only earned if you complete the full staking duration.
    

Example:

*   You choose a 7-day stake, but unstake on Day 6:
    
    *   You still receive a prorated 1.2% APY based on 6 days.
        
    *   You will **not** receive the +1.5% Tier Bonus or +25% from a 7-Day Gem.
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-faq#q-how-do-i-know-if-im-a-whitelisted-user-when-claiming-gems)

**Q: How do I know if I’m a Whitelisted User when claiming Gems?**

Simplest way to check: If you can claim 3 Gems daily, you are whitelisted. Whitelisted addresses can claim **2 extra Gems** daily per day (3 in total). You qualify if:

💎 Long-term holders that are still holding

• The address first received FB on or before **Jun 9, 2025, and** still holds 500 FB or more at snapshot time.

• The snapshot covers FB balance held on-chain in your wallet, in InSwap, and in Fractal Vote.

💎 Early Inscribers on Fractal

• Minted 4000 or more inscriptions within one month of Fractal mainnet launch

💎 InSwap OGs

• Wrapped at least 50 FB on InSwap on or before Nov 11, 2024, 06:50:00 UTC

💎 Selected addresses that participated in Fractal Voting

• Staked at least 20 FB to participate in Fractal VotingSnapshot was taken on Sep 9, 2025, 02:00 UTC.

🔗 Full eligibility rules: [https://events.fractalbitcoin.ioarrow-up-right](https://events.fractalbitcoin.io/)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-faq#q-why-do-shorter-duration-gems-offer-higher-yields)

Q: Why do shorter-duration Gems offer higher yields?

There are a total of 5 types of Gems, and each day 4 of them are displayed on the event page. The higher the APY of a Gem, the rarer it is—and it’s first come, first served.

[PreviousFB Farming: Step-by-Step Guidechevron-left](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-step-by-step-guide)
[NextInSwap on Fractalchevron-right](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal)

Last updated 4 months ago

# InSwap Events | UniSat

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-events#lpfest)

LPfest

LPfest is an incentive program that provides additional rewards to LPs.

Rewards are calculated based on amount of LPs locked distributed each block. The program is ongoing with 2-week epochs launching regularly.

👉View past events: [https://inswap.cc/swap/lp\_rewardsarrow-up-right](https://inswap.cc/swap/lp_rewards)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-events#inswap-lp-match)

InSwap **LP Match**

UniSat introduces a brand new LP Match program to directly strengthen liquidity of community pools.

What this means:

• For every LP **locked** by the community during the event, InSwap will add 1 LP into the same pool, up to a cap! Users also receive bonus LP rewards by locking LP.

👉View past events: [https://inswap.cc/swap/eventsarrow-up-right](https://inswap.cc/swap/events)

# LPfest: Step-by-Step Guide | UniSat

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-events/lpfest-step-by-step-guide#step-1-access-inswap-bonus-lp-rewards-page)

Step 1: Access InSwap Bonus LP Rewards Page

*   Visit [events pagearrow-up-right](https://pizzaswap.io/swap/events)
     and click on InSwap Liquidity Boost #1
    
*   Connect your UniSat Wallet or OKX Wallet to access LPfest.
    
*   Note: We only support Native Segwit (P2WPKH) and Taproot (P2TR) addresses.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FfXi3k0JJYjoMGLrtiw9U%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D377e63c8-1ac3-428e-88ba-86fc71462f37&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=643351fa&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-events/lpfest-step-by-step-guide#step-2-wrap-assets-into-inswap)

Step 2: Wrap Assets into InSwap

**Supported Pairs for InSwap Liquidity Boost #1 event:**

• FB<>BTC • MoonCats<>FB

*   Go to the **Swap** page. On the right side, find the wrap section, select the ticker you wish to wrap, and click **Wrap**.
    
*   Sign the transaction to complete the wrap.
    

_Note: If you haven't completed an inscription transfer yet, you will need to click_ _**\+ Inscribe TRANSFER**_ _first._ For more details on wrapping assets, check out [herearrow-up-right](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-services/pizzaswap-fractal-swap-service/how-to-interact-with-pizzaswap)
.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FBSCrNUFf0JqNYNrjKVxy%252F88.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7f05224-6d8b-40c2-a87f-ae48d199c440&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b8bd8e6a&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-events/lpfest-step-by-step-guide#step-3-add-liquidity)

Step 3：Add Liquidity

1.  Go to the Bonus LP Rewards section to view available pairs, current LP lock amounts, and reward pool details.
    
2.  Select the pair you wish to lock LP for and click on **Add Liquidity** to navigate to the **Trading Pair** page.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FiPblqvxhIdAUzEQlKUyP%252F222.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38505c39-4729-492d-bfc7-c03f2c9e3bb8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d1ea3017&sv=2)

1.  On the **Trading Pair** page, enter the amount of liquidity you wish to contribute, then click **Supply**.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fz3yW08ErgtcpuMwvnIzp%252F1111.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D543fc74d-ce5c-405e-a683-adbcc707b10e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2f76ffd9&sv=2)

_Note: If you’ve already added LP before, you can go directly to Step 4 by clicking the_ _**Go to LP Rewards**_ _button._

1.  Review the details and click **Confirm Supply** to proceed.
    
2.  Sign the transaction to complete the supply of liquidity.
    
3.  Once completed, you can check your liquidity status on the **My Liquidity** page. From here, you can choose to **add** more liquidity or **remove** liquidity as needed.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FNkw4O2DtnF1QQSYewzn8%252F2222.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14397ae5-91fe-4215-80f8-4238af7f75ab&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=580023e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-events/lpfest-step-by-step-guide#step-4-locking-lp-for-rewards)

Step 4: Locking LP for **Rewards**

*   Return to the **LPfest** page or go directly to LP
    
*   Find the pair you want to lock LP for and click **Lock**.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F2ZiuZm3Zr0MKtqDnEebM%252F33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7c359c9c-04f7-45cc-825c-36528dbd7b25&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7b158be8&sv=2)

*   On the lock confirmation page, enter the amount you wish to lock. You can manually input the amount or use the percentage buttons for a quick selection.
    
*   Confirm the lock amount and the **Rollup Fee**, then click **Lock** and sign the transaction to finalize the lock.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FLebzA0Ro2qsAMEp74fnY%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D247af50d-6b27-4a31-8ba1-2ac6f5c73e94&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9e1cf0a4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-events/lpfest-step-by-step-guide#step-5-claim-your-lp-rewards)

Step 5：Claim Your LP Rewards

*   Reward will be distributed by block, based on your % share of total locked LP for a specific pair in every block.
    
*   Reward calculation starts from the block immediately after locking your LP successfully, and ends at the block immediately after unlocking.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FZGbQYQlBFaQr4qkfCbbt%252F44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db1d54033-aa25-4062-a36b-da9a0e54e8cd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e04f3d41&sv=2)

Once you've locked your LP, rewards will be distributed on a per-block basis, calculated based on your share of the total locked LP for a specific trading pair.

The system will automatically calculate your LP rewards and display them. You can claim your rewards at any time by clicking **Claim**.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FRjALx2TiwxCxXNU8JSxQ%252F444.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db1b40ae9-35cc-43d5-962e-1927480d9548&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12896398&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-events/lpfest-step-by-step-guide#unlock-lp)

Unlock LP

If you wish to stop earning LP rewards or unlock part of your LP, follow these steps:

1.  Go to [LP Rewardsarrow-up-right](https://pizzaswap.io/swap/lp_rewards)
     page
    
2.  Click **Unlock** next to the pair you want to unlock. Enter the amount you wish to unlock and confirm.
    
3.  Sign the transaction to complete the unlock process.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FlCGb8Zx9x5k1OUipkjU1%252F77.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbefd7c9b-46c1-4d92-a21d-2f8ae7037ed1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a3515bce&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fc4hbU3L24JzVpC4ky1Sg%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0da91afe-dae0-4023-9a13-2a15cb988042&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4e7fc865&sv=2)

**FAQ：What does this prompt mean when interacting with InSwap?**

It means that we are currently submitting the rollup inscription. During this process, you’ll need to wait patiently as no other actions can be performed. Usually this prompt will disappear within 10 seconds. But sometimes it may take a long time. Please wait with patience.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FB8uVFbTNqdLFA1C1qDKK%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38aa65dc-7664-4e71-b068-7a8b7be6ce01&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6308883&sv=2)

# Enable the two-factor authentication | UniSat

Two-factor authentication (2FA) is an additional security feature that requires users to enter a six-digit verification code when logging into their accounts. This greatly enhances account security and effectively prevents unauthorized access.

For the safety of your account, we recommend setting up Two-factor authentication immediately after registering to provide an extra layer of protection.

**How to link Two-factor authentication？**

1.  Enter UniSat [Developer Centerarrow-up-right](https://developer.unisat.io/dashboard)
    , click on the avatar on the right side of the page and select '**2FA Setting**' from the dropdown menu.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F8btJoPCiSTK087n6H8rh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4366c70-2bfc-4045-b249-7517ab4efc36&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94a30c4e&sv=2)

1.  Before binding 2FA, you need to confirm your email to ensure the operation is authorized by you. Click '**Send Code**' on the page, input the verification code received in your email, and click '**Submit**' to enter the 2FA binding page.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FkDUfs8dgzOEewucbsQKY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2d440d3-e647-4922-8b73-0829fe024cc2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e54d663d&sv=2)

1.  Follow the instructions on the page to first download and install an **authentication app**.
    

iOS: Search **Google Authenticator** in the App Store

Android: Search **Google Authenticator** in Google Play or use [this download linkarrow-up-right](https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.google.android.apps.authenticator2)

Then, use the authenticator app to scan the QR code on the page and enter the six-digit verification code in the authentication app.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FMyoW9mYM8f2RxjeJTsyI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5f204bc-a5df-4567-b6a9-9b74e9eb9e7a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b29d544a&sv=2)

1.  Now you are done with 2FA! And of course, you can also disable 2FA if needed.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FzitBAQCIznqimmviT8wp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D470acec5-fcce-48d4-8cbe-84f2bc6cae68&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2dd81427&sv=2)

# FAQ | UniSat

*   **When will the previously requested API keys expire?**
    
    *   **A:** Previously issued free API Keys will expire on **August 31st**. You can register and apply for a new API Key in our new [developer centerarrow-up-right](https://developer.unisat.io/account/login)
        .
        
    

*   **What are the differences in the API interfaces before and after the upgrade? Will the data be automatically upgraded?**
    
    *   **A:** There are no changes to the API interfaces before and after the upgrade. The old API Key will automatically expire on August 31st. Users need to register and apply for a new API Key at [Developer Centerarrow-up-right](https://developer.unisat.io/plan)
        
    

*   **Is the data structure of the new API interface consistent with the old API interface?**
    
    *   **A:** Yes, the data structure of the new API interface is consistent with the old one.
        
    

*   **What should I do if my API request limit is not sufficient? What if the rate limit is not enough? What if I exceed my plan's limit?**
    
    *   **A:** This situation typically occurs when your current usage exceeds the limits of your monthly API Key plan. However, there's no need to worry. We offer a "**Pay as you go**" plan that allows you to acquire additional requests as needed. Additionally, we provide **Free**, **Specialist**, **Enterprise**, and **Custom API plans** that you can upgrade to according to your needs, usually with immediate effect.

# LP Operations | UniSat

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/lp-operations#transfer-lp)

Transfer LP

You can transfer your LP positions to another address within InSwap!

Perfect for: Consolidating LPs, securing assets in a new wallet, gifting liquidity!

Before you send, please note:

*   The recipient address will start earning LP rewards from the newly received LP
    
*   The sender will lose any unclaimed pending LP earnings and future LP earnings tied to the transferred LP.
    

_Tips: Only Native Segwit or Taproot addresses are supported_

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FgJ7a89EHiVQ3P3zPNJls%252F88.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25737dca-1e04-4fd2-90c5-f4a1136f13e0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b713362&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/lp-operations#lp-lock)

LP Lock

Why lock LP?

✅ Enjoy long-term LP earnings

✅ Build credibility with your token community

Before locking LP, please note:

• Locked LP continues to earn rewards as usual

• Both LP & rewards remain locked until expiry date

• Please remember to unlock manually via "My Liquidity" page upon expiry

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FDFn6dw2EklHVhSP8tNkN%252FLPlock.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8db0a02b-2c2f-4ec1-8b99-6f59c8b20594&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=78255839&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/lp-operations#lp-burn)

LP Burn

Why burn LP?

✅ Permanently lock liquidity in the pool for added stability

✅ Build credibility & trust within your community

How to Burn LP?

1️⃣ Go to [https://inswap.cc/swap/poolsarrow-up-right](https://inswap.cc/swap/pools)
, and choose your trading pair

2️⃣ Click Burn LP

3️⃣ Enter the amount of LP to burn, read the important notes → confirm that you fully understand the outcome of burning your LP→ Sign the transaction

4️⃣ Once burned, your LP burn record will be visible in both the trading pool’s LP Burn History and LP Holders sections

Whether you're launching a new asset or supporting an existing one, Burn LP helps you show you're here for the long run. But please TAKE NOTE OF THE FOLLOWING.

📌 **Important:**

_**⚠️ Once burned, the liquidity represented by the LP assets will be permanently locked in the pool.**_

_**⚠️ Burned LP and all underlying positions can never be withdrawn by you or anyone.**_

_**⚠️ Any pending earnings tied to the burned LP will be cleared, and the burned LP will not accumulate LP earnings.**_

_**⚠️ This action is irreversible.**_

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fktvu5M0COaWTNjiQglBi%252Flpburn.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9910222c-1469-4fa7-ba05-342217d3e6f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4d5fc9b9&sv=2)

# How to split Ordinals / Runes / Alkanes / BTC / FB? | UniSat

UniSat UTXO Management Tool: [https://unisat.io/utxo arrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/utxo)

Splitting UTXOs to different addresses with custom amounts, or breaking large UTXOs into smaller ones, can help improve asset flexibility, prevent asset mixing, and enable faster, smoother transactions.

UniSat UTXO Management Tool now supports easy UTXO splitting for:

*   Alkanes Assets
    
*   Ordinals
    
*   Runes
    
*   BTC (on Bitcoin Mainnet) / FB (on Fractal Mainnet)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-split-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#how-to-split-your-utxos)

How to Split Your UTXOs？

Let's take Split Alkanes as an example. Please note that the Split process for Ordinals, Runes, and BTC may vary slightly. You can check the specific details on each asset's Split page.

**⚠ Always double-check before pressing that confirm button!**

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FAzBE4c5S6Z0Cun6o2wtB%252Fsplit.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D386b9a7b-b44c-4164-b236-4e8fac3917c7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b718454&sv=2)

**🔸 Alkanes:**

*   **Auto split:** Select and split Alkanes UTXOs to a designated receive address.
    
*   **Manual split:** Select and split Alkanes UTXOs to multiple receive addresses with custom amounts - total control.
    

_Note:_

*   _UTXOs containing mixed assets cannot be operated on._
    
*   _Only UTXOs of the same Alkanes tickers can be operated on._
    

**🔸 Ordinals:**

*   **Batch send** up to 500 inscriptions/collections/name/ brc-20 transfer UTXOs to a designated address to save time and fees.
    
*   **Efficiently split** a UTXO containing multiple inscriptions into separate ones.
    

_Note: UTXOs that contain mixed assets (e.g., both Ordinals and Runes) cannot be operated on._

**🔸 Runes:**

*   **Auto split:** Select and split Runes UTXOs to one designated receive address.
    
*   **Manual split:** Select and split Runes UTXOs to multiple receive addresses with custom amounts.
    

_Note:_

*   _UTXOs containing mixed assets cannot be operated on._
    
*   _Only UTXOs of the same Runes ticker can be operated on._
    

**🔸 BTC / FB:**

*   **Auto split:** Select and split large BTC/FB UTXOs into multiple smaller UTXOs of equal size to a designated receive address.
    
*   **Manual split:** Select & split one or more BTC/FB UTXOs and batch send them to multiple receive addresses with custom amounts.
    

_Note: BTC/FB UTXOs that are locked cannot be operated on in this tab. Once selected, all buttons will be disabled._

**Disclaimer:**

The content of this document is for informational purposes only. It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. Digital assets (including FTs and NFTs) are subject to market volatility, involve high risk, regulatory changes, and may depreciate in value. The information is provided "as is," and we make no warranties regarding its accuracy. Please consult your legal, tax, or investment professionals to determine whether trading or holding digital assets is suitable for you.

[PreviousHow to reclaim BTC/FB trapped in useless inscription UTXOschevron-left](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-reclaim-btc-fb-trapped-in-useless-inscription-utxos)
[NextHow to batch send Ordinals / Runes / Alkanes / BTC / FB?chevron-right](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb)

# UTXO Tool FAQ | UniSat

**UTXO Management Tool:** [https://unisat.io/utxo arrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/utxo)

**Q: What is UTXO?**

Each UTXO (Unspent Transaction Output) represents a spendable balance in Bitcoin or Fractal.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/utxo-tool-faq#consolidate-faq)

**Consolidate FAQ**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_Lower fee = more BTC in your pocket! Consolidating is optimal when network fees are <3 sats/vB!_

**Q: What are useless inscriptions? Will merging them affect my brc-20 assets?**

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fj80RMt4NIGdPO9BSMtQz%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D537ca0ab-76c6-4af2-9c01-0471760a46ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8304050&sv=2)

There are currently two types: **brc-20 Mint inscriptions and used brc-20 Transfer inscriptions.**

These types of brc-20 inscriptions have no value and are not linked to your brc-20 asset holdings. Merging and spending them will not affect your brc-20 balance.

However, each inscription typically occupies 294–546 sats. If you have a large quantity of these types of useless inscriptions, they can take up a significant portion of your balance. Consolidating them when the fee rate is low can help you reclaim at least 60% of usable BTC.

**Q: Since useless inscriptions include brc-20 Transfer inscriptions, are minted but unused brc-20 Transfer inscriptions safe?**

Yes, they are safe. Valid and unused brc-20 Transfer inscriptions will not be classified as useless inscriptions and will appear in the "UTXO list".

**Q: Will consolidated useless inscription UTXOs become spendable BTC in the wallet?**

Yes. After consolidating, they usually exceed 600 sats and will appear as available balance in the wallet.

**Q: Why does consolidating useless inscriptions UTXOs consume high gas fees?**

Gas fee = fee rate × virtual transaction size. The more inputs a transaction has, the larger the size, and thus the higher the fee. We recommend merging when fees are relatively low to process.

**Q: Is there a service fee for consolidating useless inscription UTXOs? Will I earn points?**

You get three free **consolidations up to 3000 UTXOs each month,** effectively no charge. For consolidate with a service fee, corresponding UniSat Points will be awarded. More details [herearrow-up-right](https://docs.unisat.io/unisat-services/guides-and-explanations/unisat-points-explained)
.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/utxo-tool-faq#unlock-utxos-under-all-utxos-tab-faq)

Unlock UTXOs under "All UTXOs" tab FAQ


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_**📌 Unlock with care**_

_**UTXOs with brc-20, ordinals NFT , Alkanes or Runes assets are treated as BTC after unlocking — you may burn valuable assets if mistakenly select the wrong UTXO.**_

**Q: How do I unlock assets using the UTXO Management Tool?**

_Tips: Before unlocking, make sure the UTXOs’ assets are useless/unwanted to avoid losing anything valuable._

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Frkxk5YvagAoZmSF9RrCd%252Funlock%2520new.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2eb2b389-ce29-4015-ac43-a05992f658ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=76ce5468&sv=2)

**Q: Can unlocked inscription/Runes/Alkanes UTXOs be used directly as BTC in the UniSat wallet?**

Yes, and there are two cases:

*   If the UTXO is >600 sats, your available balance in wallet will update its amount after unlocking, and it can be used directly as BTC.
    
*   If the UTXO is <600 sats, your available balance won’t update. It cannot be directly selected in the wallet for sending. You must go to the UTXO Management tool https://unisat.io/utxo to send it. _(Detailed steps_ [_here_](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-unlock-lock-inscription-runes-alkanes-utxo-and-send-as-normal-btc-in-all-utxo-tab)
    _)_
    

**Q: Why do unlocked UTXOs get locked again after being used?**

If a UTXO contains assets that UniSat can recognize—such as inscriptions or runes, the system will require you to manually confirm and unlock it before each spend to ensure your assets remain secure.

**Q: Can unlocked inscription/Alkanes/Runes UTXOs be sent to other addresses such as exchanges' wallet addresses? Will they turn into available BTC?**

Yes, if you do not wish to keep these assets, you can send them anywhere. \*Whether they appear as available BTC on any platform depends on whether that platform recognizes and locks the asset. If not, they will show up as unavailable BTC.

**Q：How many UTXOs can I unlock or merge at once?**

You can unlock or merge up to 500 UTXOs at a time. We may improve this limit in future updates.

* * *

**Q: If I select UTXOs on the current page, then go to the next page, will my selections be saved?**

No. Currently, selection is only valid on the current page. If you have many UTXOs, please increase the number of items displayed per page at the bottom, and use the category filter in the top right to narrow your list.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fz2vf6jtQjmgr6cJeerY4%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56c6210c-163c-4985-b7c8-012ac7f80418&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7ba8be17&sv=2)

* * *

**Q: Will unsupported small UTXOs be spent automatically in my UniSat wallet?**

If your address has unsupported protocol assets stored in UTXOs under 600 sats, you cannot spend them directly unless you manually select and send them via our UTXO Management tool https://unisat.io/utxo. Please operate with caution when doing so.

* * *

**Q: Why does it say "Not enough BTC UTXOs available for network fee payment" when splitting BTC?** This occurs when the user only has one BTC UTXO or selects all BTC UTXOs for splitting, leaving none to pay the network fee. Solution: Reserve enough BTC from the split amount to cover the fee.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FnVkJLHNzcCVDWGXKgQTo%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D796600e2-a509-49c5-ada4-ca6f4656f6a7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b06a46&sv=2)

* * *

**Q: Why does the UTXO quantity show as 0 when trying to split Runes or Alkanes?** If the UTXO quantity shows as 0 on the split interface, it means the current settings do not allow the UTXO to be split. This can happen due to the asset's decimal support, the maximum allowed decimal places, or your specific split configuration. Please refer to the examples below:

*   Example 1: The asset does not support decimals and must be split in whole numbers. Attempting to split 1 unit into 3 parts results in decimals, so splitting is not possible. Illustration:
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FNClwY5SqOKeC6YwkIkyY%252F99.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D89cc00cc-7c96-47f1-908e-dd6abccbe495&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=76c7b66b&sv=2)

*   Example 2: The asset supports 2 decimal places. Attempting to split 0.01 units into 2 parts exceeds the supported decimal precision, so splitting is not possible.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FSC0hYaZTRZtaT8uCtOUj%252F88.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d7c7a8d-360c-4b5b-8682-0e9606a0d212&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=26bd170&sv=2)

*   Example 3: Alkanes assets support 8 decimal places by default. Attempting to split 0.00000001 units into 2 parts exceeds the 8-decimal limit, so splitting is not possible.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fkw5Zc1ys0C6iRlTsdiG1%252F77.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e87f67b-1c97-4ec5-97de-c5170f3c5142&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=88af162b&sv=2)

# How to batch send Ordinals / Runes / Alkanes / BTC / FB? | UniSat

The Batch Send function in UniSat UTXO Management Tool helps you efficiently transfer assets to one or multiple addresses, saving time and optimizing UTXO usage.

UniSat UTXO Management Tool: [https://unisat.io/utxo arrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/utxo)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#supported-batch-send-scenarios)

**Supported Batch Send Scenarios**

*   **Alkanes:** Batch send Alkanes UTXOs to multiple addresses with customizable amounts.
    
*   **Ordinals: Batch send** up to 500 inscriptions/collections/name/ brc-20 transfer UTXOs to a designated address, save time and fees.
    
*   **Runes: Batch send** different amounts of Runes to different addresses.
    
*   **BTC(on Bitcoin)/FB(on Fractal): Batch send** up to 500 UTXOs to a single address or up to 1000 different addresses.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#how-to-batch-send-your-utxos)

How to Batch Send Your UTXOs?

In this guide, we will use Batch Send for Runes as an example. The overall process for Ordinals, Runes, Alkanes, and BTC/FB is similar, with slight differences depending on the asset type. Please refer to the specific batch send interface for each asset.

**⚠️ Note:** _**To avoid sending assets as ordinary BTC, please use the batch send feature within the corresponding protocol-specific page (Ordinals, Runes, Alkanes, BTC/ FB(on Fractal) Tab), don't use batch send under the "All UTXOs" tab.**_

1️⃣ Access the UTXO Management Tool

Visit: [https://unisat.io/utxoarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/utxo)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#id-2-select-the-runes-tab)

2️⃣ Select the "Runes" Tab

Switch to the Runes section to manage your Runes UTXOs.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#id-3-choose-send)

3️⃣ Choose "Send"

Select Runes UTXO and click **Send** button to start the process.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#id-4-enter-receiving-addresses-and-amounts)

4️⃣ Enter Receiving Addresses and Amounts

*   Input different addresses and the amount of Runes to send to each address.
    
*   **Double-check all details before confirming.**
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management/how-to-batch-send-ordinals-runes-alkanes-btc-fb#id-5-confirm-the-transaction)

5️⃣ Confirm the Transaction

Submit the batch send and wait for the transaction to be broadcast to the network.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FTvFzz5M5wQpDBGC0lPki%252Fbatch%2520send.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D26ab445d-6b67-46bd-9b52-705743e96961&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=58205e54&sv=2)

The content of this document is for informational purposes only. It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. Digital assets (including FTs and NFTs) are subject to market volatility, involve high risk, regulatory changes, and may depreciate in value. # Plans | UniSat

UniSat API can still be accessed without an API key. However, to ensure fair allocation of resources, we recommend including an API key in all requests. Requests made without a key, or with a free key, may face strict rate limits or even no response under high load.

To provide everyone with convenient and diverse options for purchasing API keys, we offer several plans: **Free**, **Specialist**, **Enterprise**, **Custom**, and **'Pay as you go'**. For details: [unisat.io/plansarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/plans)

> Enjoy 20% off when you choose an annual Specialist or Enterprise plan

* * *

# FB Farming: Step-by-Step Guide | UniSat

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-step-by-step-guide#how-to-participate-in-fb-famring)

How to Participate in FB Famring

1.  **Visit the Farming Page**
    

Go to: [https://fractal.unisat.io/farmingarrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/farming)
 and connect your wallet.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fvff8LaHtczIC2gcDadSw%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2aaf89bf-eec6-4425-bece-ab012decdd48&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfa07c0a&sv=2)

1.  **Use Rewards Calculator**
    

Understand your returns clearly using the built-in calculator:

*   Input the amount of FB you want to farm
    
*   Choose your staking duration
    
*   If you claimed Gems during the Anniversary Carnival, add Gems for exra bonus APY
    
*   View your estimated APY and FB rewards
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FVThlZoOrJ8uEOgNj1LpY%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd2808acd-43d6-42af-a17d-ff43cb31ae7b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d65dc62&sv=2)

1.  **Start Farming**
    

*   In the Pool #1 or Pool #2 section, click on **Stake** next to Pool 1
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FEu8aIPORYMuIUQipBm7L%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D720290c8-fa44-4d2a-8df0-86f4d585055b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=92109506&sv=2)

*   Enter the amount of FB you want to stake
    
*   Add up to **2 Gems** at same time to boost your returns (2 Gems must have different durations)
    
*   Click **Confirm Stake**
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F3IumuKEvAv2Ss3MeXOPe%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df994c1b7-b213-4f9b-82e9-42b17a055a12&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=493ee4b&sv=2)

1.  **Track and Manage Your Stakes**
    

Go to **My Staking** to:

*   Monitor your rewards
    
*   Add Gems under the **Using Gems** section
    
*   Unstake partially or fully at any time
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FwMbdz6XpIxlNchV2gPlH%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45ed8c90-2fab-45ab-b7b1-9682ca248b8e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1a6629e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-step-by-step-guide#tips)

📌 Tips:

*   **Gems:**
    
    *   You can stack **up to 2 Gems at a time** (as long as their bonus APY differs).
        
    *   When a Gem expires, you can add another one. Example: If you use a 30-Day Gem + 7-Day Gem at a time, when the first 7-Day Gem expires, you can add another one.
        
    *   Ensure your staking duration is **equal or longer** than the Gem's duration for it to take effect
        
    *   The Gem bonus rewards are calculated starting from the Gem’s effective date.
        
    *   Farming rewards are calculated starting from the confirmation time.
        
    
*   **Staking Limits:**
    
    *   Minimum: 1 FB per stake
        
    *   Maximum: 10,000 FB per pool per address
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-step-by-step-guide#how-to-unstake)

🔓 How to Unstake

1.  Go to **My Staking** and find the position you want to unstake
    
2.  Click **Unstake**
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FWIRv4umolLTVHWqNFE2g%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddc31ffcc-382b-4bea-9604-7c12c261b71b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1ff509da&sv=2)

1.  Please make sure you have read the on-page explanation of Gem early-unstake reward calculations. After confirming that you fully understand the content, check the risk alert box and click **Continue to Unstake**.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fnu7v0aTFOneQ6h3YS345%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D301872c4-e24d-4458-96de-28a866405146&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=65c1435c&sv=2)

1.  Confirm Enter the amount you want to unstake
    
2.  Confirm the **receiving address** (default: connected wallet)
    
3.  Click **Confirm Unstake**
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FcUVe7sPqJcvklGY9FgpM%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd8cb9d7-073a-4ccd-bdcc-404a8f944bb6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=de457d16&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-step-by-step-guide#important-notes)

📍 Important Notes

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-step-by-step-guide#you-may-unstake-at-any-time.-however-please-note-the-implications-of-early-unstaking)

You may unstake at any time. However, please note the implications of early unstaking.

*   **Base APY (1.2%)** is always earned based on time staked
    
*   **Tier Bonuses** and **Gem Bonuses** are **only earned if the full stake duration is completed**
    

**Example:**

*   You choose to stake for 7 days but unstake on Day 6
    
    *   ✅ You receive a prorated 1.2% APY based on 6 days
        
    *   ❌ You forfeit +1.5% Tier Bonus and +25% Gem Bonus
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/fb-farming/fb-farming-step-by-step-guide#track-your-activity)

🧾 Track Your Activity

You can find all your staking-related actions and history under **My Activity**.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FifAQIQWTsJaiHtniaoI2%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D117998e7-9f30-4b2b-9825-11a465ed8a5f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f415e53&sv=2)

# How to Trade Runes？ | UniSat

This guide will walk you through the step-by-step process of trading with Runes. Please do your own research. This guide serves only as a reference for users.

Go to [https://fractal.unisat.io/runes/marketarrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/runes/market)
, and search for rune.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FKwueBrLkvrnRw6k2n4GF%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47ae6dbd-6d1c-472a-8603-fa400afbf79a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fa41646&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F9OCOofCbiH8ltKkN7zuc%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df24c9ea4-c698-4ee8-8815-dda7357f2d57&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a52a5357&sv=2)

You can buy the Rune one by one or in batches.

You can also list/unlist or update prices for your rune assets by clicking ‘My Assets’.

*   List Runes: Click ‘My Assets’ and then click ‘List’ button beside Rune, then you will get the List page as below,
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fh66RqHtyezaPDZdj4IFU%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7112a9ec-24d0-43b7-bb13-aab5abb0b3b4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd19ad0f&sv=2)

*   After setting the price and signing via Wallet, it will be listed.Comment
    
*   You may go to My Orders to view the listed order, update price or unlist your Rune asset.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F5h21fbpTgLVGpDOsIAp2%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0f94d53f-5b83-45eb-bd28-e6e3c555c8d5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fc8dbd7e&sv=2)

**Legal Disclaimer**The Fractal Bitcoin One Year Anniversary Carnival (the “Carnival”) is a goodwill gesture by the Fractal Bitcoin project team (the “Team”) to express appreciation to our community. Participation in this event is subject to the following disclaimer:

1.  **No Investment or Financial Advice** The Carnival does not constitute an offer to sell, a solicitation of an offer to buy, or a recommendation of any kind regarding any financial product or digital asset. Nothing in connection with the Carnival should be construed as investment, financial, legal, or tax advice.
    
2.  **Eligibility and Allocation** Eligibility criteria and allocation details are determined solely at the discretion of the Team and may be modified, suspended, or cancelled at any time.
    
3.  **No Warranties** FB are provided “as is” without warranties of any kind, express or implied, including but not limited to merchantability, fitness for a particular purpose, or non-infringement. The Team makes no guarantee of value, usability, or availability of FB, either now or in the future.
    
4.  **Regulatory and Jurisdictional Restrictions** Participation may be restricted or prohibited in certain jurisdictions. It is the sole responsibility of participants to ensure compliance with applicable laws, regulations, and restrictions in their respective locations.
    
5.  **Assumption of Risk** By participating, you acknowledge and accept the inherent risks of blockchain-based systems, including but not limited to technological issues, system vulnerabilities, regulatory uncertainties, and potential changes in access conditions. The Team shall not be responsible for failures caused by network issues, system errors, third-party services, or other factors beyond its reasonable control.
    
6.  **No Guarantee of Future Benefits** Any anniversary badges, recognitions, or associated features are symbolic in nature. While they may provide access to certain community initiatives, the Team provides no guarantee as to their utility, duration, or value.
    
7.  **Limitation of Liability** In no event shall the Team be liable to you for any loss of profits, revenue, goodwill, or for any indirect, incidental, special, consequential, or punitive damages arising out of or related to participation in the Carnival.
    

**By participating in the Carnival, you acknowledge that you have read, understood, and agreed to this Legal Disclaimer.**
