# InSwap API Guide | UniSat

InSwap Community Edition is now available on GitHub with the latest version of its full source code. Here’s a quick guide to using InSwap.

For full details, please refer to the InSwap API guide: [https://github.com/unisat-wallet/inswap-community-editionarrow-up-right](https://github.com/unisat-wallet/inswap-community-edition)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-api-guide#how-do-i-use-inswap-api)

How do I use InSwap API?

To use InSwap, follow these steps:

1.  Clone the repository:
    
    Copy
    
        git clone https://github.com/brc20-devs/brc20-swap-api.git
    
2.  Install the project dependencies:
    
    Copy
    
        yarn
    
3.  Copy the `config.json.example` file and rename it to `config.json`:
    
    Copy
    
        cp conf/config.json.example conf/config.json
    
4.  Configure the OpenAPI API key by updating the `config.json` file with your API key. For example:
    
    Copy
    
        "openApi": {
           "url": "https://open-api.unisat.io",
           "apiKey": "YOUR_API_KEY"
         },
    
    Replace `YOUR_API_KEY` with your actual API key. Note: If you don't have an API key, you can obtain one by signing up on the OpenAPI website: [https://developer.unisat.ioarrow-up-right](https://developer.unisat.io/)
    
5.  Configure the MongoDB connection by updating the `config.json` file with your MongoDB connection details. For example:
    
    Copy
    
        {
          "mongoUrl": "mongodb://127.0.0.1:27017/"
        }
    
    Make sure you have MongoDB installed and running on your machine.
    
    Note: If you don't have MongoDB installed, you can download it from the official MongoDB website: [https://www.mongodb.com/download-center/communityarrow-up-right](https://www.mongodb.com/download-center/community)
    
6.  Start the development server:
    
    Copy
    
        yarn start-dev
    
7.  Open your web browser and navigate to `http://localhost:3000/documentation/static/index.html` to access the application.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-api-guide#how-do-i-deploy-a-new-inswap-module-instance)

How do I deploy a new InSwap module instance?

To build a new InSwap module instance, follow these steps:

1.  Refer to the `script/deploy-on-testnet-example.ts` file for an example of how to deploy a new module and contract.
    
2.  Once you have the new module and contract, update the corresponding configuration in the `config.json` file.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-api-guide#how-can-i-contribute-to-inswap)

How can I contribute to InSwap?

If you would like to contribute to this project, please follow these guidelines:

1.  Fork the repository on GitHub.
    
2.  Create a new branch for your feature or bug fix.
    
3.  Make your changes and commit them with descriptive messages.
    
4.  Push your branch to your forked repository.
    
5.  Submit a pull request to the main repository.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-api-guide#can-i-refer-to-any-inswap-api-demos)

Can I refer to any InSwap API demos?

Please check the demo here: [https://github.com/unisat-wallet/unisat-dev-examples/tree/master/brc20-swap-demoarrow-up-right](https://github.com/unisat-wallet/unisat-dev-examples/tree/master/brc20-swap-demo)

[NextInSwap Eventschevron-right](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/inswap-events)

# Unwrap Assets | UniSat

Please note that this guide is for reference only; we recommend conducting your own research as well.

* * *

[I. How to unwrap your assets from the brc20-swap on bitcoin mainnet ？](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/unwrap-assets#i.-how-to-unwrap-your-assets-from-the-brc20-swap-on-bitcoin-mainnet)

[II. How to unwrap your Fractal assets from InSwap?](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/unwrap-assets#ii.-how-to-unwrap-your-fractal-assets-from-inswap)

[III. How to unwrap sFB to FB?](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/unwrap-assets#iii.-how-to-unwrap-sfb-to-fb)

[IV. How to unwrap bFB to FB?](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/unwrap-assets#iv.-how-to-unwrap-bfb-to-fb)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/unwrap-assets#i.-how-to-unwrap-your-assets-from-the-brc20-swap-on-bitcoin-mainnet)

I. How to unwrap your assets from the brc20-swap on bitcoin mainnet ？

The brc-20 swap on Bitcoin mainnet is still in the black module, you couldn't unwrap your assets directly. But with our Green channel, you may easily get your assets out to your wallet. Please follow the steps below.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/unwrap-assets#step-1-use-green-channel-to-bridge-your-assets-to-inswap)

Step 1: Use Green Channel to bridge your assets to InSwap

*   Visit [brc20-swaparrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/swap)
    , connect to your wallet, then click **My Module Assets**.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fvdg97wTZBDaveiIi6z2T%252F1280X1280.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd1d4014b-a477-494f-a3d3-c01194ac0941&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=33aa9eea&sv=2)

*   Choose the assets you want to unwrap, then click the "Bridge" button. (Note, only the assets which Simple Bridge supported have this button) In the brc-20 swap, ticker sats is the gas, so you want to unwrap multiple assets, please bridge sats at last.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fz5P7aAoSDA1bsBLc59MT%252F1280X1280%2520%281%29.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db921e2d7-84a4-4202-8f68-e34293ca24d1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9c73a0dc&sv=2)

After bridging, you may click "Bridge" to check the status of the transaction. It takes about 32 hours to finish the whole process.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fzy9PgBAIZTIkE9fkCeee%252F3.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9faed22c-b934-486a-ab53-ecf5807830ed&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8923f83d&sv=2)

Once the status becomes "Completed", then you may go to InSwap "My Module Assets" to check your assets.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F2TQno4n1XaBeBJJXFdXb%252F4.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D150a2255-fed4-4022-b686-438bbcab3c2a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=544f03f1&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/unwrap-assets#step-2-unwrap-from-inswap)

Step 2: Unwrap from InSwap

*   Once the assets are already in your InSwap, then you may unwrap it directly. Click "Unwrap" menu, choose the asset you want to unwrap, input the amount then click "Unwrap" to continue.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FKPrcT9e2GCFSwTAwNr0B%252F5.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4c340bea-b525-4c42-ba24-af880890a940&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e48b4c7&sv=2)

Once the unwrapping process is completed, then you may go to step 3.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/unwrap-assets#step-3-bridge-assets-back-to-bitcoin-mainnet)

Step 3: Bridge Assets back to Bitcoin mainnet

*   Go to [Simple Bridgearrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/bridge)
     and click the menu marked below to switch to unwrap mode.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FbnHmOwHbLOaXzTJEphh5%252F6.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De64152a9-f4fb-4bb6-be7f-e0a1f828c882&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4f80382a&sv=2)

*   Choose the asset you want to unwrap from the dropdown list.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FViOOzYxv164cdbj10hLk%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96ef3395-b4c1-4ce3-bb97-148fe8f62bb7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a455e9a7&sv=2)

First, you need to inscribe a transfer. Click the ‘+Inscribe TRANSFER’ button to inscribe transfer.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FeXD9Sq6wBsyS5A6HH7Kv%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5b6b1c91-8e77-4e84-9e61-e1f566730ced&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d7ad9795&sv=2)

When it is confirmed, then you can choose that transfer, and click the "Unwrap" button to continue.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FbPJdlFFj6zrNedh5j6S1%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45317585-e51e-48b1-9eb3-a319bb6bf50f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe7310d8&sv=2)

When the transaction is completed, you will get the asset on Bitcoin mainnet. You may open UniSat wallet, switch to the "Bitcoin Mainnet" network to check it.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/unwrap-assets#ii.-how-to-unwrap-your-fractal-assets-from-inswap)

II. How to unwrap your Fractal assets from InSwap?

*   Visit [InSwap arrow-up-right](https://inswap.cc/)
    and connect to your wallet address.
    
*   Click on Swap menu, then click the "Unwrap" menu , select the ticker you want to unwrap.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FhsyWZYpvvfmPm6WXO8au%252F10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b81cf7c-8848-4814-9e8a-a6e8bc6dc5c9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22541702&sv=2)

*   Input the amount, click the Unwrap button to continue.
    
*   When the transaction is confirmed, you may open UniSat wallet, switch to Fractal Mainnet network, click "Ordinals/brc-20" to check it.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/unwrap-assets#iii.-how-to-unwrap-sfb-to-fb)

III. How to unwrap sFB to FB?

After unwrapping sFB from InSwap , you will get sFB in your wallet under the brc-20 tab. If you want to use them as FB, you need to use [Simple Bridgearrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/bridge)
 to turn sFB to FB.

Step 1: Visit Simple Bridge [https://fractal.unisat.io/bridgearrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/bridge)
 and connect to your wallet.

Step 2: Click the button marked below to switch to unwrap mode.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FoCMXzI6l9DCHtUgGZniI%252F11-12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9b997f1-d79f-471e-a16a-10a46755d1be&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0bd84ca&sv=2)

Step 3: Choose sFB from the dropdown list. Then click the button marked below to inscribe a transfer first.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FhE5WD6jR9tKYdPeifTOE%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D11431a9a-7c5d-4715-9d88-d59f57b3a68b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a649a744&sv=2)

Step 4: Choose the transfer, then click the "Unwrap" button to continue.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F79yetendG2R5G3JR1uml%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d867efd-7c63-42ed-80ae-69840429b55f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=25998960&sv=2)

Once the process is completed, then you can open UniSat wallet to check the FB balance.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F9Ku09lODGXXhDI2YpC6m%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db85ac240-411d-4a9d-8120-d683df01442c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f64d9b&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/unwrap-assets#iv.-how-to-unwrap-bfb-to-fb)

IV. How to unwrap bFB to FB?

After unwrapping bFB from InSwap, you will get bFB in your wallet under the brc-20 tab. If you want to use them as FB, you need to use [Bool Bridgearrow-up-right](https://fractal.boolbridge.com/)
 to turn bFB to FB.

Step 1: Visit [Bool Bridgearrow-up-right](https://fractal.boolbridge.com/)
 and connect to your wallet address.

Step 2: Choose 'FB⇄bFB' , then click ⇅ .

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fr1OhwLOrfC1u3HifYL7G%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2fae6ac2-79d3-4dfe-b902-53f6e26b65b6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22c1fad4&sv=2)

Step 3: Click the button marked below to inscribe a transfer first.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FaiVUS7B7EPdC18fdzD5a%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2040fe30-8365-4775-bbdf-09c2ac1ee992&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd8bee0b&sv=2)

Step 4: Choose the transfer and click "Unwrap" to continue.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FA65sAj8xqeJg8yR0HUhr%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D138a719f-d72a-49fa-b82c-40fe9d048ce6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c26891d5&sv=2)

Once the process is completed, then you can open UniSat wallet to check the FB balance.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FlW3Dot90xBE4r7IgLdH4%252F19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29a6781e-672c-475b-a2e9-c08b3e0b3ff1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6183421b&sv=2)

# How to Acquire a UniSat API Key | UniSat

Previously, API keys were requested by contacting the UniSat team and applying via email. With the new Developer Center, you will need to register with your email and choose the appropriate plan.

Here are the steps to acquire a UniSat API Key:

1.  Visit [UniSat websitearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/)
     and click 'API' in the homepage navigation bar. From the dropdown menu, select 'API Service' to access the detailed API plans page. Alternatively, you can directly click [herearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/plans)
     to view the API plans.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FgyPpFm3k9e4siuJPh5GN%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35112f4a-33db-4750-a2d6-06a29c27fbd3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=25c1607d&sv=2)

1.  Choose the plan that suits your needs and click '**Get Started**' under the detailed description of the plan to go to the Developer Center plan acquire page. Or you can click '**Developer Center**' in the yellow box on the page to enter the Developer Center.
    

> Enjoy 20% off when you choose an annual Specialist or Enterprise plan.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FMLVTVh8Gi7EM3mMASvLP%252F22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D27add4a5-d6a1-46b5-98ee-feaf8f7655bc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8bda935f&sv=2)

1.  Before acquiring a plan, you need to register a Developer Center account using your email.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FBlkwVnfSxnSD4tZOWYtX%252F20240716-205021.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D40744b9b-b4e3-49d0-bb93-9f5905579447&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44e14a5&sv=2)

1.  Once registered, go to the Dashboard page where you will see your API Key, Current API Key Configuration, and your API Request Log. For newly registered accounts, we will continue to offer developers a monthly free access quota of 5 calls/second, up to 2,000 calls/day.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FUAhMoqaGxp2JstQxIrRO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D10328495-ef97-44dc-acf9-6bcf40dd08b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=90717a9e&sv=2)

Click '**Plan**' in the upper left corner to go to the API Key acquire page.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FSKvkjw6abXz0S2iW7o8E%252F33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ec07ced-b820-41f5-b5b7-1ddd18c279bc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86073bf9&sv=2)

1.  Choose the plan you need and click the '**Buy**' button under the specific plan to enter the acquire page.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FfCVFykrOfF0PD1eTYkMn%252F44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1825143-6e14-4c2d-9346-b1474b44a3a1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c53c306b&sv=2)

1.  Payments are currently accepted via PayPal and BTC. If you choose PayPal, the page will redirect to the PayPal payment page. If you choose BTC, you can pay using a BTC wallet address or your UniSat wallet.
    

Here is an example of a BTC payment method, click '**Pay with BTC**', then select '**Pay with Wallet**'. The page will prompt you to sign; confirm the input and output information carefully, and click 'Sign & Pay' to complete the acquire.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fw1zcL9rjBCnkyjfIEH8X%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1e81f91-f4f7-46bc-9935-a47eafe95956&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=779bf631&sv=2)

1.  After the acquire is complete, you can view your plan acquire record on the **Billing** page.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FD7eU8reBYzfB1dTHwEZH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5339f0b8-1ca4-4ef5-9396-0246332a24fc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e3519781&sv=2)

# How to Mint Runes? | UniSat

Step 1: find the mint interface

*   Go to the Mint option on page [https://fractal.unisat.io/runes/inscribearrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/runes/inscribe)
    .
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Ffm3ZkJ4oLr9jnFEEfW6Y%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df3081f07-6733-4775-93d7-ad990b60779b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf232266&sv=2)

Or you could explore Rune information on [https://fractal.unisat.io/explorer/runesarrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/explorer/runes)
, search the ticker you want to mint and then Click ‘Mint’ -> ‘Mint Directly’ button if the rune can be mintable for more convenience.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FEFS5Gy4deCdMBqozzoJS%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61123130-e082-416c-9e83-8fd8754c7329&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80a047d9&sv=2)

Step 2: Start minting Runes

*   You could input the _**Rune or Rune ID**_ as below.
    
*   You can input the number of _**Repet Mint**_ or use the slide bar for batch minting.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FeInPIsMzSgdwcfEX6CZm%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da3ec3460-4163-4625-ab35-c73c01dff487&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44819226&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F22jwP8n9tTvjjQLBBEF0%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db909f8c0-4062-4fce-bb30-93a4e6d4eb76&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d82809b8&sv=2)

After your transaction is confirmed on chain, you may check your runes balance in your wallet.

**Disclaimer:**

It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. # Privacy Policy | UniSat

Last Updated: August 07, 2025

UniPro Technology Limited (“Company”, “we”, “our”, or “us”) recognizes that people who use our product value their privacy. This privacy policy (“Policy”) describes how the Company collects, uses, shares, and stores personal information of users of our website, [https://unisat.ioarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/)
 (together with the sub-domains, collectively the “Site”). This Policy applies to the Site, applications, products and services (collectively, “Services”) on or in which it is posted, linked, or referenced.

By using the Services, you accept the terms of this Policy and our Terms of Use, and consent to our collection, use, disclosure, and retention of your information as described in this Policy. If you have not done so already, please also review our Terms of Use. The Terms of Use contain provisions that limit our liability to you and require you to resolve any dispute with us on an individual basis and not as part of any class or representative action. IF YOU DO NOT AGREE WITH ANY PART OF THIS POLICY OR OUR TERMS OF USE, THEN PLEASE DO NOT USE ANY OF THE SERVICES.

Please note that this Policy does not apply to information collected through third-party websites or services that you may access through the Services or that you submit to us through email, text message or other electronic message or offline. If you visit any links to third-party websites, pages, contents or platforms which may be accessible through links from the Site or any link of any of our third-party partners, you must and will be required to agree to and comply with the separate and independent privacy policy of such third parties. We will not bear any liability for the contents and activities of such sites operated by third parties.

If you are visiting this site from the European Union (EU), see our Notice to EU Data Subjects below for our legal basis for processing and transfer of your data.

**1\. WHAT WE COLLECT**

When you interact with the Services, information we collect from you includes:

*   Network information regarding transactions, only the publicly-availiable blockchain data, such as publicly-available blockchain address;
    
*   Contact information, such as your email address;
    
*   Feedback and correspondence, such as information you provide in your responses to surveys, when you participate in market research activities, report a problem with the Services, receive customer support or otherwise correspond with us;
    
*   Usage information, such as information about how you use the Services and interact with us;
    
*   Marketing information, such as your basic marketing preferences for receiving marketing communications. We will only collect data related to behavioral analytics, including your interactions with emails and advertisements (e.g., opens, clicks), if you have given your explicit consent.
    
*   Information We Get From Others. We may get information about you from other third party sources and we may add this to information we get from your use of the Services. Such information may include:
    
    *   Information Automatically Collected. We may automatically record certain information about how you use our Site (we refer to this information as “Log Data“). Log Data may include information such as a user’s Internet Protocol (IP) address, device and browser type, operating system, the pages or features of our Site to which a user browsed and the time spent on those pages or features, the frequency with which the Site is used by a user, search terms, the links on our Site that a user clicked on or used, and other statistics. We use this information to administer the Services and we analyze (and may engage third parties to analyze) this information to improve and enhance the Services by expanding its features and functionality and tailoring it to our users’ needs and preferences.
        
    
*   We use HTTP request headers to transmit session information, and we use local storage to support certain functionalities within the Site. For more information, please see the sections entitled “Local Storage Policy” below. We will update this policy and notify users if there are any changes.
    
*   We also use Google Analytics to help us offer you an optimized user experience. You can find more information about Google Analytics’ use of your personal data here: [https://policies.google.com/privacy?hl=enarrow-up-right](https://policies.google.com/privacy?hl=en)
    .
    
*   Information we will never collect: (1)We will never ask you to share your private keys or wallet seed. Never trust anyone or any site that asks you to enter your private keys or wallet seed; (2) Our wallet app supports biometric login using your device’s built-in face or fingerprint authentication. All biometric data is processed locally by the device’s secure system (e.g., Apple Face ID, Android Biometric API). We do not collect, store, or transmit any biometric information.
    

**2\. USE OF PERSONAL INFORMATION**

To provide our Services, we use your personal information only where permitted by applicable law and for the limited purposes described below:

*   To enable you to access and use the Services
    
*   To provide and deliver products and services that you may request
    
*   To send information, including confirmations, technical notices, updates, security alerts, and support and administrative messages
    
*   To comply with law
    

We use your personal information as we believe necessary or appropriate to comply with applicable laws, lawful requests and legal process, such as to respond to subpoenas or requests from government authorities.

*   To communicate with you
    

We will not use your personal data for direct marketing activities unless we have obtained your prior written consent. With your consent, we may send you direct marketing communications that may be of interest to you, including but not limited to providing promotional information, upcoming events, and other news about products and services offered by us and our selected partners.

Personal data supplied by you will not be provided to third parties for direct marketing activities of products or services by such third parties unless we have obtained your prior written consent and such data transfer shall be in accordance with the requirements set out under the Personal Data (Privacy) Ordinance (Chapter 486 of the Hong Kong laws) and any other applicable law before we use your personal data for direct marketing activities.

If you do not wish to receive our direct marketing activities, you may opt out anytime by emailing us at contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.unisat.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#6f030a080e032f1a01061c0e1b410600)
.

*   To optimize our platform
    

In order to optimize your user experience, we may use your personal information to operate, maintain, and improve our Services. We may also use your information to respond to your comments and questions regarding the Services, and to provide you and other users with general customer service.

*   With your consent
    

We may use or share your personal information with your consent, such as when you instruct us to take a specific action with respect to your personal information, or you opt into third party marketing communications.

*   For compliance, fraud prevention, and safety
    

We may use your personal information to protect, investigate, and deter against fraudulent, unauthorized, or illegal activity. These purposes are based on our legitimate interest in ensuring the security and integrity of our Services.

**3\. SHARING OF PERSONAL INFORMATION**

We do not share or sell the personal information that you provide us with other organizations without your express consent, except as described in this Policy or required by law or legal reporting obligations. We disclose personal information to third parties under the following circumstances:

*   Affiliates. We may disclose your personal information to our subsidiaries and corporate affiliates for purposes consistent with this Policy.
    
*   Business Transfers. We may share personal information when we do a business deal, or negotiate a business deal, involving the sale or transfer of all or a part of our business or assets. These deals can include any merger, financing, acquisition, or bankruptcy transaction or proceeding. If such a transfer occurs, we will require the recipient to continue to use your personal information in a manner consistent with this Policy or otherwise obtain your consent.
    
*   Compliance with Laws and Law Enforcement; Protection and Safety. We may share personal information for legal, protection, and safety purposes.
    
*   We may share personal information to comply with laws.
    
*   We may share personal information to respond to lawful requests and legal processes.
    
*   We may share personal information to protect the rights and property of the Company, our agents, customers, and others. This includes enforcing our agreements, policies, and Terms of Use.
    
*   We may share personal information in an emergency. This includes protecting the safety of our employees and agents, our customers, or any person.
    
*   Professional Advisors and Service Providers. We may share personal information with those who need it to do work for us. These recipients may include third party companies and individuals to administer and provide the Services on our behalf (such as customer support, hosting, email delivery and database management services), as well as lawyers, bankers, auditors, and insurers. All service providers with whom we share personal information are contractually obligated to protect the data in compliance with applicable privacy laws and use it only for the specific purpose of providing Services to us.
    
*   Other. You may permit us to share your personal information with other companies or entities of your choosing. Those uses will be subject to the privacy policies of the recipient entity or entities. We may also share aggregated and/or anonymized data with others for their own uses.
    

**4\. INTERNATIONAL TRANSFER**

We operate globally, and your personal data may be stored and processed in any country where we conduct business or where we engage service providers. We may disclose your information to third-party storage providers or affiliates located within your country/region, or transfer it to those located outside of your country/region.

We may also transfer your personal data to recipients in countries other than the one in which the data was originally collected. These countries may have different data protection or privacy laws from those in your own jurisdiction. However, we will take appropriate steps to ensure that any such transfers comply with applicable data protection laws and that your personal data remains protected to the standards described in this Policy. By using our Services, you acknowledge and agree to your personal information being processed in this way.

EU users should read the important information provided below about transfer of personal information outside of the European Economic Area (EEA).

**5\. HOW INFORMATION IS SECURED**

We retain information we collect as long as it is necessary and relevant to fulfill the purposes outlined in this Policy. In addition, we retain personal information to comply with applicable law where required, prevent fraud, resolve disputes, troubleshoot problems, assist with any investigation, enforce our Terms of Use, and other actions permitted by law. To determine the appropriate retention period for personal information, we consider the amount, nature, and sensitivity of the personal information, the potential risk of harm from unauthorized use or disclosure of your personal information, the purposes for which we process your personal information and whether we can achieve those purposes through other means, and the applicable legal requirements. If you stop using the Services or close your account on the Site, we will continue to retain your personal information as necessary to comply with our legal and regulatory obligations.

In some circumstances we may anonymize your personal information (so that it can no longer be associated with you) in which case we may use this information indefinitely without further notice to you.

We employ industry standard security measures designed to protect the security of all information submitted through the Services, including—where appropriate—data encryption (in transit and at rest), access controls, multi-factor authentication, regular security assessments, and secure coding practices. However, the security of information transmitted through the Internet can never be guaranteed. We are not responsible for any interception or interruption of any communications through the Internet or for changes to or losses of data. Users of the Services are responsible for maintaining the security of any password, biometrics, user ID or other form of authentication involved in obtaining access to password protected or secure areas of any of our digital services. In order to protect you and your data, we may suspend your use of any of the Services, without notice, pending an investigation, if any breach of security is suspected.

**6\. INFORMATION CHOICES AND CHANGES**

*   Accessing, Updating, Correcting, and Deleting your Information
    

You may access information that you have voluntarily provided through your account on the Services, and to review, correct, or delete it by sending a request to contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.unisat.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#cca0a9abada08cb9a2a5bfadb8e2a5a3)
. You can request to change contact choices, opt-out of our sharing with others, and update your personal information and preferences. We may need to verify your identity before processing such requests. In certain cases, we may retain information where required by law or for legitimate business purposes.

You may also opt out of receiving promotional communications from us by following the unsubscribe instructions in those messages. Please note that you may still receive transactional or service-related messages.

*   Google Analytics
    

You may exercise choices regarding the use of cookies from Google Analytics by going to [https://tools.google.com/dlpage/gaoptoutarrow-up-right](https://tools.google.com/dlpage/gaoptout)
 and downloading the Google Analytics Opt-out Browser Add-on.

*   CONTACT INFORMATION. We welcome your comments or questions about this Policy, and you may contact us at: contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.unisat.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#f19d9496909db1849f98829085df989e)
    .
    
*   CHANGES TO THIS POLICY. We may change this Policy at any time. We encourage you to periodically review this page for the latest information on our privacy practices. If we make any changes, we will change the Last Updated date above.
    

Any modifications to this Policy will be effective upon our posting of the new terms and/or upon implementation of the changes to the Site (or as otherwise indicated at the time of posting). In all cases, your continued use of the the Site or Services after the posting of any modified Policy indicates your acceptance of the terms of the modified Policy, except where your explicit consent is required under applicable laws.

**7\. ELIGIBILITY**

If you are under the age of majority in your jurisdiction of residence (“Minor Users”), you may use the Services only with the consent of or under the supervision of your parent or legal guardian. We do not knowingly offer Services to or collect personal information from Minor Users without verified parental/guardian consent. If we learn that we have received any information directly from Minor Users without first receiving his or her parent's verified consent, we will use that information only to respond directly to that Minor Users (or his or her parent or legal guardian) to inform the child that he or she cannot use the Site. We will then promptly delete that information from our records.

**8\. NOTICE TO EU DATA SUBJECTS**

*   Personal Information
    

With respect to EU data subjects, “personal information,” as used in this Policy, is equivalent to “personal data” as defined in the European Union General Data Protection Regulation (GDPR).

*   Sensitive Data
    

Some of the information you provide us may constitute sensitive data as defined in the GDPR (also referred to as special categories of personal data), including identification of your race or ethnicity on government-issued identification documents. We do not intentionally collect sensitive data, and where such data is collected, it is processed only where legally permitted and with appropriate safeguards.

*   Legal Basis for Processing
    

We only use your personal information as permitted by law. We are required to inform you of the legal basis of our processing of your personal information, which are described in the table below. If you have questions about the legal basis under which we process your personal information, contact us at contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.unisat.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#6c00090b0d002c1902051f0d18420503)
.

**Processing Purpose**

**Legal Basis**

To provide and deliver the Services

Contract performance (Art. 6(1)(b))

To send transactional or service communications

Legitimate interests (Art. 6(1)(f))

To send marketing communications

Consent (Art. 6(1)(a))

To optimize and maintain our platform

Legitimate interests (Art. 6(1)(f))

To ensure compliance, prevent fraud, ensure safety

Legitimate interests / Legal obligation (Art. 6(1)(c)/(f))

To respond to legal or data subject requests

Legal obligation (Art. 6(1)(c))

These processing activities constitute our legitimate interests. We make sure we consider and balance any potential impacts on you (both positive and negative) and your rights before we process your personal information for our legitimate interests. We do not use your personal information for activities where our interests are overridden by any adverse impact on you (unless we have your consent or are otherwise required or permitted by law).

*   With your consent
    

Where our use of your personal information is based upon your consent, you have the right to withdraw it anytime in the manner indicated in the Services or by contacting us at contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.unisat.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#b2ded7d5d3def2c7dcdbc1d3c69cdbdd)
.

*   Use for New Purposes
    

We may use your personal information for reasons not described in this Policy, where we are permitted by law to do so and where the reason is compatible with the purpose for which we collected it. If we need to use your personal information for an unrelated purpose, we will notify you and explain the applicable legal basis for that use. If we have relied upon your consent for a particular use of your personal information, we will seek your consent for any unrelated purpose.

*   Your Rights
    

Under the GDPR, you have certain rights regarding your personal information. You may ask us to take the following actions in relation to your personal information that we hold:

*   Opt-out. Stop sending you direct marketing communications which you have previously consented to receive. We may continue to send you Service-related and other non-marketing communications.
    
*   Access. Provide you with information about our processing of your personal information and give you access to your personal information.
    
*   Correct. Update or correct inaccuracies in your personal information.
    
*   Delete. Delete your personal information.
    
*   Transfer. Transfer a machine-readable copy of your personal information to you or a third party of your choice.
    
*   Restrict. Restrict the processing of your personal information.
    
*   Object. Object to our reliance on our legitimate interests as the basis of our processing of your personal information that impacts your rights.
    

You can submit these requests to contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.unisat.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#0c60696b6d604c7962657f6d78226563)
. We may request specific information from you to help us confirm your identity and process your request. Applicable law may require or permit us to decline your request. If we decline your request, we will tell you why, subject to legal restrictions. If you would like to submit a complaint about our use of your personal information or response to your requests regarding your personal information, you may contact us at contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.unisat.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#8be7eeeceae7cbfee5e2f8eaffa5e2e4)
 or submit a complaint to the data protection regulator in your jurisdiction.

*   Cross-Border Data Transfer
    

Please be aware that your personal data will be transferred to, processed, and stored in jurisdictions outside your country of residence. Some data may be routed through or temporarily stored on servers located in the other countries for technical and operational reasons. Data protection laws in these jurisdictions may differ from those in your country of residence. You consent to the transfer of your information, including personal information, as described in this Policy by visiting our Site or using our Services.

Whenever we transfer your personal information out of the EEA to the countries not deemed by the European Commission to provide an adequate level of personal information protection, the transfer will be based on a data transfer mechanism recognized by the European Commission as providing adequate protection for personal information.

Please contact us if you want further information on the specific mechanism used by us when transferring your personal information out of the EEA.

**9\. LOCAL STORAGE POLICY**

To enhance your experience, we use browser-based local storage to temporarily save certain preferences and settings on your device. This data is stored locally and is not transmitted to our servers. Specifically, we store the following types of information in your browser:

*   Language Preference – To remember your selected language for future visits.
    
*   Wallet Connection Status – To recall the type of wallet you previously connected for quicker access.
    
*   Watchlist Items – To store digital assets or projects you follow, making them easier to revisit.
    
*   Local Identifier – To distinguish between devices or browsers, used solely for local interface optimization.
    

This local storage data is never used for advertising, user profiling, or tracking, and is accessible only within your own browser. It is not shared with third parties.

You may clear this data at any time via your browser settings. Please note that deleting local storage may affect certain features or preferences on the Site.

# UniSat Open API | UniSat

UniSat Open APIs provide standardized RESTful interfaces and an online interactive Swagger UI for quick exploration and testing: [https://open-api.unisat.ioarrow-up-right](https://open-api.unisat.io/)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FIiqW0kOfslVgDeapQp9q%252F111.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda932c0e-7e41-4304-98d2-86ac7d4359a1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1ea30fae&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/developer-support/unisat-open-api#apply-for-a-unisat-api-key)

Apply for a UniSat API Key

Before you start using UniSat API, you need to apply for a UniSat API Key.

We offer several plans: Free, Specialist, Enterprise, Custom, and Pay-as-you-go. Visit [https://developer.unisat.io/arrow-up-right](https://developer.unisat.io/)
 and follow the on-page instructions to apply.

How to Acquire a UniSat API Key: [https://docs.unisat.io/dev-center/developer-center/how-to-acquire-a-unisat-api-key](https://docs.unisat.io/developer-support/how-to-acquire-a-unisat-api-key)

Note: UniSat API can still be accessed without an API key. However, to ensure fair allocation of resources, we recommend including an API key in all requests. Requests made without a key, or with a free key, may face strict rate limits or even no response under high load.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/developer-support/unisat-open-api#usage)

Usage

1.  Use the Swagger UI [https://open-api.unisat.ioarrow-up-right](https://open-api.unisat.io/)
     and read the documents [https://github.com/unisat-wallet/unisat-dev-docsarrow-up-right](https://github.com/unisat-wallet/unisat-dev-docs)
     to test API calls.
    
2.  Register at [https://developer.unisat.io/arrow-up-right](https://developer.unisat.io/)
     and authenticate as required by each API.
    
3.  Handle error codes and messages according to the [error codes documentationarrow-up-right](https://github.com/unisat-wallet/unisat-dev-docs/blob/master/errors/README.md)
    

* * *

For any questions, support, or discussions, please reach out to us on Discord: [http://discord.gg/unisatarrow-up-right](http://discord.gg/unisat)
 Thank you for using UniSat Open API!

# How to Inscribe on UniSat | UniSat

Getting started with the UniSat Inscribe service is simple. Let’s walk through the process using brc-20 inscription as an example. This guide is for reference — actual UI and options may vary slightly, please follow what’s displayed on the inscribe page.

**Limited-Time Offer!**

Enjoy 0 **service fee** for the **first 20 inscriptions** in the first batch inscribe order per day!

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe/how-to-inscribe-on-unisat#step-1-connect-your-wallet)

Step 1: Connect Your Wallet

Visit [https://unisat.io/inscribearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/inscribe)
 and connect your UniSat Wallet (or any supported wallet).

_Download or upgrade UniSat Wallet:_ [_https://unisat.io/download_arrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/download)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FN8P2clAB8gwC1tIEKpdP%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D51e089ca-1499-4bd3-ac0c-63a5df50f83a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=62a2d133&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe/how-to-inscribe-on-unisat#step-2-choose-inscribe-type)

Step 2: Choose Inscribe Type

After entering the Inscribe page:

*   The left-side panel shows an overview of all brc20 and Runes tickers. You can switch between “Mintable” and “Finished” brc-20 and Runes tickers.
    
*   Use the search bar to look for specific brc-20/Runes tickers.
    
*   Use the 1h / 6h / 24h filters to view popular tickers by time range.
    
*   Use the view toggle icon to switch to the Heat Map view.
    

Choose your desired protocol: Ordinals or Runes, Then select the content type to inscribe (e.g., brc-20, Files, Name, Text).

For this guide, we'll use brc-20 as an example.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F5YytZx9xwvrkK4j4F5qH%252F2.1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fe7745b-2ed0-4f03-a1f7-d4b13057c5d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ed920e0&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FNP3iyem1ukjeRZBiAdtE%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a576752-ac7a-4fcf-be8b-3ac134804dc9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22eda9a0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe/how-to-inscribe-on-unisat#step-3-start-inscribing)

Step 3: Start Inscribing

*   Search or click on the brc-20 ticker you want to mint.
    
*   On the result page, click the **Mint** button on the right.
    
*   In the panel on the right:
    
    *   Confirm that it's a 4-byte Mint inscription.
        
    *   Verify the ticker name and mint amount.
        
    *   Use the input box or slider to batch mint multiple times.
        
    

Once you've reviewed all the details, click **Next**, and confirm again on the next screen.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fe2r2jW3y3SpjErj8xZub%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f453d06-752d-4b8b-afb7-cae105abe7d5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=188abb74&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FEUbtqlsWanmZkZhiJJjt%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db01b454b-c17b-4671-b790-7f0cdbcd6c12&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2088b688&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe/how-to-inscribe-on-unisat#step-4-choose-receiving-address-and-fee)

Step 4: Choose Receiving Address & Fee

*   Select **"To Single Address"** to inscribe to one address or **"To Multiple Addresses"** for batch inscribing.
    
*   Customize your network fee as needed.
    
*   Please carefully read the Risk Warning, and confirm by checking the box.
    
*   Click **Submit & Pay Invoice** to proceed.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FaRuPS9tX76AbNd7hk6yg%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D995f99b1-d51c-4667-8ace-4fdb68817d5b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9c4eaaee&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe/how-to-inscribe-on-unisat#step-5-payment)

Step 5: Payment

On the order confirmation page:

*   Double-check your inscription details and total cost.
    
*   Select a payment method.
    
*   Complete the payment to submit your inscription order.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FzFnMdUPtZtxyDVaXt9Oe%252F7.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24e7993a-9af5-4161-8ba5-c0cb327a039b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bc4b0e1a&sv=2)

💡 **Tips:**

*   Before the transaction is broadcasted, you can click **Cancel** to abort the order.
    
*   To speed up confirmation, use the **Boost** option.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FQnNmE1alH56n1i62KVyR%252F8.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d052466-79db-40e9-aaad-b7dbb2e062bd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f7038ef9&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe/how-to-inscribe-on-unisat#inscribe-via-uniscan)

Inscribe via UniScan

You can also access the inscribe service through the **UniScan explorer**:

*   Go to [https://uniscan.ccarrow-up-right](https://uniscan.cc/)
    
*   Click on **Ranking** to see tickers for Alkanes, brc20, Runes (Note: Alkanes inscribe service not yet supported).
    
*   Search the ticker you want, and click the **Mint** button to jump directly to the inscribe page.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FmhhffoZW5cqd8i99IDoo%252F9.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db8b1c89d-6ade-4cbe-aef0-053e9e0406c9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7fa84ab7&sv=2)

**Notes:**

1.  In case of platform order congestion, there might be delays in on-chain processing, and we cannot guarantee the on-chain processing time.
    
2.  The rate you submit now does not represent the real-time on-chain rate. Please be aware of the fluctuating on-chain rate.
    
3.  If there are unconfirmed outbound transactions in your payment account, please stop the payment or switch to another account for operation.
    
4.  When encountering orders with ongoing engraving, please patiently wait for the miner's confirmation, as the transaction cannot be revoked.
    
5.  Please note the inscribing transaction delivers the inscription to the receiving address directly.

# v1.3.0 | UniSat

*   Runes Support
    

\- View and send Runes assets on the testnet.

\- Before mainnet launches, we will enhance the display and user experience. Your feedback is highly valued.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fv4c1fl581ns.sg.larksuite.com%2Fspace%2Fapi%2Fbox%2Fstream%2Fdownload%2Fasynccode%2F%3Fcode%3DNzc4ZDY0MzM4YjRkYjA1YTczNjEzNmEzYjQxMjRmNDdfTUNEVkQ2b1pkdnVIN0k2Y3dBaHpaRUk3aHdqMDBKc2ZfVG9rZW46VW5vR2JLTHdBb28wMGx4aE5UQ2xRaExlZ1doXzE3MTM0Mjg2NjE6MTcxMzQzMjI2MV9WNA&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1c4c68ad&sv=2)![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fv4c1fl581ns.sg.larksuite.com%2Fspace%2Fapi%2Fbox%2Fstream%2Fdownload%2Fasynccode%2F%3Fcode%3DZTc2MGMzMTI1MzZiYjA5MDQxMjdlODQ5MDc1YTI5OGRfQ2cwcWZvMmRFdVdRNkF4eEdZS1hjSnBlWXNEdHhSeWNfVG9rZW46STVRUmJSa2JBb2R0YmZ4TTZqcmxWQmlHZ3NkXzE3MTM0Mjg2NjE6MTcxMzQzMjI2MV9WNA&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71ed4a68&sv=2)

*   Unconfirmed Balance Mode
    

\- Introduced a toggle for enabling unconfirmed balances.

\- Unconfirmed balance usage is automatically disabled when holding ARC-20 or Runes assets.

\- You can re-enable it in Advanced Settings, but be cautious as these asset types are currently not recognized in the mempool, which could lead to asset burning risks.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fv4c1fl581ns.sg.larksuite.com%2Fspace%2Fapi%2Fbox%2Fstream%2Fdownload%2Fasynccode%2F%3Fcode%3DY2IyZjRjYzMwMGRhODAxMGM5MTQwNWViOWE3MDE3OTBfTnlsNjlyVkZPY2gyWDgxYjNSZEV3S3NsOHpzZTI3RVZfVG9rZW46RW5POGJ0b0lZb1EzTFp4OEhaU2xXS05oZ2ZvXzE3MTM0Mjg2NjE6MTcxMzQzMjI2MV9WNA&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef96f7a1&sv=2)

*   About Unavailable Balances
    

\- We've added explanations for balances labeled as 'Unavailable', which include inscriptions, ARC20, and Runes asset balances. When Unconfirmed Balance is disabled, this will also include unconfirmed balances.

\- Due to the system handling a maximum of 500 UTXOs at a time, any excess UTXOs at an address will temporarily be classified as 'Unavailable'.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fv4c1fl581ns.sg.larksuite.com%2Fspace%2Fapi%2Fbox%2Fstream%2Fdownload%2Fasynccode%2F%3Fcode%3DZjFjZjM2ODkxMTg3ZGZlZGJiMGFjOWQ4MmIxNGMxNmJfUTNuQllQc0ZxelJERlZJM1ZFM3hlbGZPMWR1eUFOMXVfVG9rZW46RUx1YmIzWlBGb3A2UG14dEF6Qmw3bTVDZzBiXzE3MTM0Mjg2NjE6MTcxMzQzMjI2MV9WNA&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1432e9a2&sv=2)

*   Fee Rate Alerts
    

\- No longer forcing pop-up warnings for transactions with high or low fee rates.

\- Risk level downgraded, now indicated by a subtle tag.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fv4c1fl581ns.sg.larksuite.com%2Fspace%2Fapi%2Fbox%2Fstream%2Fdownload%2Fasynccode%2F%3Fcode%3DZGYwOTg1MjU1M2NmYTU3ZGYxZTNkMzY2NmRlZTZkZmRfOXBmYXlmSVN6RzdVMFhFUFBzeHBXUDh3emlna2UydkJfVG9rZW46UHBoV2JiaVIwb29FbkZ4QXhFYWx1c05YZ2hiXzE3MTM0Mjg2NjE6MTcxMzQzMjI2MV9WNA&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5da3399d&sv=2)

*   Default OutputValue Adjustment
    

\- Reverted the default inscribe outputValue to 546 satoshis for simplified operations.

\- For certain addresses, manual adjustment to 330/294 is still possible if necessary.

[Previousv1.3.1chevron-left](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/release-notes/v1.3.1)
[Nextv1.2.9chevron-right](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/release-notes/v1.2.9)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Beginner's Guide | UniSat

Welcome to InSwap, the first open-source AMM DEX for Bitcoin-native assets, built natively on Bitcoin and Fractal. The platform provides a seamless trading experience while maintaining the security standards of Bitcoin assets, enabling users to swap, provide liquidity, and earn native protocol assets across both networks without intermediaries. This guide will focus on InSwap’s interface and how to use it.

The InSwap service functions as a brc-20 module and scales efficiently through rollups, enabling high-volume transactions directly on Bitcoin.

**Try it here**: [https://inswap.ccarrow-up-right](https://inswap.cc/)

* * *

Before you begin, please make sure you are familiar with the following information:

*   **Supported Addresses**: InSwap supports **Native Segwit (P2WPKH)** and **Taproot (P2TR)** addresses. Ensure your wallet is using one of these address types.
    
*   **Fees:**
    
    *   Swap Fee: A 1.5% fee is applied to each swap - 1/6 of the fee supports the platform, while the rest is distributed to liquidity providers (LPs).
        
    *   Rollup Fee: To reduce transaction costs, InSwap implements a rollup mechanism, bundling transactions into a single submission to the Bitcoin or Fractal network, ensuring lower fees for users.
        
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/beginners-guide#navigating-the-inswap-interface-visit-here)

Navigating the InSwap Interface - Visit [herearrow-up-right](https://pizzaswap.io/swap)



----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FM3yMLfEIGStsgHcxKb53%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73333673-7333-4cd2-be2e-a8a9c6bdef39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e5e2739&sv=2)

**Section 1: InSwap Navigation Bar - Key Sections**

*   **Swap** – The trading interface where users execute swaps.
    
*   **Trading Pairs** – The liquidity provider (LP) interface, where LPs can add/remove liquidity and check their liquidity positions.
    
*   **LPfest** – Special event page for rewards programs (e.g., [LPfest Epoch 3arrow-up-right](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1913146188809015337)
    . Follow [@UniSatWalletarrow-up-right](https://x.com/unisat_wallet)
     on X for event updates!
    
*   **Leaderboard** - Keep up with the hottest communities and trading pairs.
    
*   **Overview** – Displays past interactions and an overview of InSwap activity.
    

**Section 5: Key Sections for Trading**

*   **Swap:** The main trading page where users can swap tickers.
    
*   **Wrap:** The wrap page, where users wrap assets from Bitcoin or Fractal mainnet into InSwap before swapping.
    
*   **Unwrap:** The Unwrap page, where users move assets from InSwap back to Fractal or Bitcoin mainnet.
    

**Section 2: Popular Trading Pairs -** Top trading pairs by 24H volume will be highlighted by default in this section.

**Section 3: K-Line for Trading Pairs -** View K-Line charts to track price movements of trading pairs.

**Section 4: Pair Information -** Get the full details on trading pairs here: Market Cap (Community pairs) / Volume (24h) & Volume (30d) / TVL / Pooled Balance

**Section 6: History** \- Full swap history /LP holders list / Liquidity history / LP burn history

Now you're all set to explore InSwap!

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/beginners-guide#wrap-assets-to-inswap)

**Wrap assets to InSwap**

As mentioned earlier, you need to wrap assets into the InSwap module before swapping.

Let's take the example of BTC, after connecting to your wallet, click "Wrap **"** tab, Select BTC or another asset from the dropdown list, then choose a transfer to wrap it.

For brc20 tickers, if there is no transferable amount available, please click "**Inscribe TRANSFER**" to inscribe a transfer inscription first.

Wrapping requires block confirmations. Please be patient during this process.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FUCjpS5PfWyYwYMPlDSYr%252Fwrap.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc54c8cc5-393e-49ab-b448-08d2dd955b41&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e2c422f1&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/beginners-guide#adding-liquidity-to-earn-rewards)

**Adding Liquidity to Earn Rewards**

_Every swap incurs a 1.5% transaction fee. 5/6 allocated to liquidity providers (LPs) rewards, 1/6 used to support platform maintenance._ By adding liquidity, you can earn rewards from every trade.

*   Click the **"Trading Pairs"** button and search for the trading pair you want add liquidity.
    
*   If the pair is available, click the **"Add"** button on the right to add liquidity.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F8qi9N27amcf237Q38eyE%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c11d153-9369-4406-b2a7-c20e272495e1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f5a4aa00&sv=2)

*   Input the amount of liquidity you wish to contribute, then click the "**Supply**" button.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FtTBsM9F5HdE5ZKz7uDIa%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D76091cb9-4a2a-4950-9bff-753e0e604604&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd148e&sv=2)

*   Confirm your transaction by clicking the "**Confirm Supply**" button and signing in your wallet.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FOQahRS4w9re156XfPkpG%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D29d5b36d-927a-41d2-8318-6e986720ffef&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=df7af17b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/beginners-guide#viewing-your-liquidity-and-lp-earnings)

Viewing Your Liquidity & LP Earnings

You can check your liquidity positions and earnings in several ways:

1.  Go to [**My Liquidity**arrow-up-right](https://inswap.cc/swap/pools?tab=mine)
     directly.
    
2.  From **Trading Pair** page, click **“My Liquidity.”**
    
3.  Or click your **wallet icon (top right)** → **My Assets** → **Liquidity** to view your positions.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F9F7e1nw4YDkvWCZ0UQ0Q%252F666.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90279097-33fe-45be-b564-d80286af7365&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=371e4eff&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/beginners-guide#managing-your-liquidity)

Managing Your Liquidity

To **add more liquidity**, click **“Add”** next to your existing position.To **remove liquidity**, click **“Remove.”**Your **LP earnings** will be automatically settled when you remove liquidity.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FuL749NX8ElGbcbqEFazr%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0c6e26fa-4903-4798-b95a-246cd29d2311&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2497038b&sv=2)

**Tips: Creating a Liquidity Pool**

If you can’t find the trading pair you want, it means the liquidity pool doesn’t exist yet.

To create a new pool, click **"Create Trading Pair"**, select the brc-20 asset from the dropdown list, and then click **"Create"** to set up a new pool.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F4SSsvnzGhaS1lvlfkOn7%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D607ec37a-2ac8-4fd2-88ea-a05d13c78a17&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=963a86a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FTBgCyzPXQjFbTrVEvKSn%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deafff286-75be-4d8a-a436-59dae5303cd0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7420fba7&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/beginners-guide#swapping-assets)

**Swapping Assets**

Click on the [**Swap** arrow-up-right](https://inswap.cc/swap)
button to begin the asset swapping process.

Choose the asset you want to pay with. Then input the amount you wish to pay.

Review the swap details and click the **Swap** button to initiate the transaction.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fy2PhLxZUePvtDi8dbE7D%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07d515e2-b097-4525-9c6e-76ea95853d57&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=17a657f5&sv=2)

Confirm the swap information, then click the "Swap" button. And then sign in your wallet.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FxxPm1Oc1UPXj7V6a5sps%252F18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D642ad849-b83c-4d1d-bd2f-df4a421457cc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=888e4879&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/fractal-bitcoin/inswap-on-fractal/beginners-guide#unwrap-assets)

**Unwrap Assets**

To unwrap assets from InSwap, simply go to the **"unwrap"** page and follow the instructions:

Click the "**Swap**" button, then click the "**unwrap**" tab. Click on the asset you want to unwrap, input the unwrap amount. Then click "unwrap" button.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FKSwMfq0WNd0byxMujRHG%252Funwrap.gif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9688f0c7-4088-449a-a7cf-f535c51acd93&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af4cc44&sv=2)

# Developer Service Legal Disclaimer | UniSat

Last Updated: August 07, 2025

Please read this carefully before using the API service provided by UniPro Technology Limited and/or its affiliates (“UniSat”, “we”, “us” or “our”). This Developer Service Legal Disclaimer (“Disclaimer”, “Agreement” or “Terms”) takes effect from the date you (“Developer” or “Users”) first use the API. In this Disclaimer, “API” means (i) any form of machine accessible application programming interface that UniSat makes available which provides access to UniSat Offerings (as defined below), including all associated tools, elements, components and executables therein, (ii) any UniSat sample code that enables interactions with UniSat Offerings, and (iii) documentation that UniSat makes available to help enable your access to the API.

1\. Technical and Infrastructure Terms

1.1 UniSat API Data Query Service: By accessing the UniSat API platform or using the API data query service provided by UniSat (the “API Service” or “Service”), including within a software application, website, tool, service, or product you create or offer to customers (your “Application”), you are agreeing to this Disclaimer and any other terms and conditions in respect of the API Service entered into by you and UniSat.

1.2 Fees: The API Service is currently provided in different tiered packages, each with its own fee level, and UniSat reserves the right to change the fee levels for the API Service from time to time.

1.3 Availability and Reliability of the API Service: UniSat does not guarantee the availability and reliability of the API Service to Users. Users need to assess the risks associated with using the API and bear any resulting faults, issues, risks, and losses.

1.4 Service Changes and Termination: UniSat reserves the right to modify or terminate the API Service at any time at its sole discretion without prior notice. UniSat is not responsible for any losses or inconveniences resulting from such actions.

1.5 Data Accuracy: UniSat does not guarantee that the information returned by the API is accurate, timely, complete, valid, or error-free. UniSat is not responsible for any losses caused by inaccuracies, delay or data errors resulting from using the API Service.

1.6 Technical Compatibility: UniSat is not responsible for the incompatibility of the API with any devices, platforms, browsers, services, software or hardware. Users must ensure that their technical environment is compatible with the API Service.

1.7 Third-Party Content and Links: The API Service may contain content or links from third parties, solely as a convenience. Such third-party content or links are not under the control of UniSat and UniSat is not responsible for the quality, accuracy, completeness, performance or reliability of this content, nor for any losses incurred by Users using third-party content or accessing third-party links through the API. The fact that such content or links may be included in, provided by, or accessed through the API Service does not imply endorsement by UniSat or the third-party of either party’s sites or services. Depending on Users’ jurisdiction, some third-party content may not be available to Users.

1.8 Open-Source Code. To the extent our Service incorporates open-source code, any third-party use of such code shall be at the Users’ sole risk. We disclaim all liabilities, whether express or implied, for technical flaws, security vulnerabilities, or fitness for purpose in any open-source components. In particular, any open-source code provided by us (including ad-hoc libraries without an explicitly stated license) is licensed under the MIT License, which expressly disclaims all warranties and liabilities. Users should review and comply with the terms of the MIT License.

1.9 Emergency Maintenance: UniSat has the right to perform emergency maintenance on the API Service at any time at its sole discretion, which may result in temporary service interruptions or suspensions. UniSat is not responsible for any losses or inconveniences caused by this. Nothing herein shall be construed as an obligation for UniSat to maintain or provide technical support of any kind for the API Service.

2\. User, Anti-Spam, and Privacy Terms

2.1 User Eligibility:

(a) To use this Service, you must declare that you are of legal age, have the legal capacity to enter into contracts, and possess full legal authority to agree to and comply with this Agreement on behalf of yourself and any company/entity. You will not be accessing the Service in a jurisdiction where such Service is not permitted, restricted or illegal;

(b) You further represent and warrant to us that you, the legal entity you represent, or any person(s) owning or controlling you or such legal entity, are not listed on any trade or economic sanctions lists maintained by any competent authorities, and you shall not engage in transactions with any listed parties, including but not limited to (1) the Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant (ISIL/Daesh), Al-Qaeda, the Taliban, and associated individuals, groups, enterprises, and entities; any individuals or entities designated by the United Nations Security Council or the United Arab Emirates; (2) the Democratic People’s Republic of Korea (DPRK), the Islamic Republic of Iran, or individuals, groups, enterprises, entities listed on sanctions lists maintained by the UN Security Council, the U.S. government (e.g., OFAC Sanctions List), the European Union or its member states, the Monetary Authority of Singapore (MAS), the Hong Kong Monetary Authority (HKMA), the Hong Kong Customs and Excise Department, or other applicable governmental authorities; and (3) you are not a “U.S. Person” as defined under 17 CFR § 230.902.

(c) We reserve the right, at our sole discretion, to construe, limit, and modify the scope of Service in any jurisdiction at any time and to determine, at our sole discretion, your eligibility to access or use this Agreement and the Service. You acknowledge that such determinations may affect your ability to access or use the Service and agree to bear all associated risks and consequences. If you fail to meet such eligibility requirements, we may, temporarily or permanently, suspend, restrict or terminate your access to the Service.

2.2 Security Assurance: UniSat is not responsible for any losses or damages caused by unauthorized access, data leaks, or other security vulnerabilities. # v1.5.1 | UniSat

🔗 [https://github.com/unisat-wallet/extension/releases arrow-up-right](https://github.com/unisat-wallet/extension/releases)

**Features:**

🔸 Multi-Signature Support for Whitelisted SitesFor whitelisted websites, you can now sign multiple transactions with a single click, simplifying batch transactions.

⚠️ _Please note that UniSat Wallet will not verify each transaction individually. We strongly recommend using this feature only on trusted and familiar websites to minimize the risk of potential losses._

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FKouVWvcRJhD04Lqh92bV%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1c2440ad-ac13-49ea-ba9b-f278cb9c8645&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f8f16db4&sv=2)

🔸 Keystone USB Connection Support.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F3RYAH5UaVXnuOX8eBbk3%252F12.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D653015c0-5372-44e9-b0f5-d9603393ef3b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49f01444&sv=2)

🔸 Improved Wallet Navigation

When switching between wallets or accounts, UniSat Wallet will automatically scroll to the selected wallet/account and display a scrollbar, making it easier for users managing multiple wallets.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FRKFR7b7YMClIrXWNlsq7%252F13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a91b996-881c-45d5-9591-5a3383d47073&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5eb3c1bf&sv=2)

🔸 For Developers:-Added the `useTweakedSigner` option to the `signPsbt` method for more flexibility in signing workflows.

# v1.4.2 | UniSat

**Features:**

*   Added support for switching to the **Signet network** _(_[`_What is Signet?_`arrow-up-right](https://docs.unisat.io/knowledge-base/what-is-signet)
    _)_
