# Single-Step Transfer (brc-20) | UniSat

**What is Single-Step Transfer?**

Simply put, Single-Step Transfer combines what used to be a two-step process — inscribing a transfer and sending it — into a single, seamless action.

❌ Inscribe transfer inscription > send brc-20

✅ Send brc-20 in ONE STEP!

* * *

**Simplified Transfer Process**

Previously, if you wanted to transfer brc-20 assets (e.g., 100 ORDI) from Address A to Address B:

*   You had to inscribe a transfer, creating a Transfer inscription that locks part of Address A’s available balance into a transferable balance.
    
*   Only after that, you could send your ORDI to Address B, enabling B to receive the assets.
    

Two steps, two transactions, higher fees.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F9S4WXpaJBvgC1UkVofVp%252Fimage%2520%2823%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07ef6169-aaeb-4c02-b558-7748bbc6f83d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=baf9f290&sv=2)

* * *

**Now with Single-Step Transfer:**

On the Send page, simply enter the recipient's address and the amount you want to send — just like sending FB.

One step, one transaction — fast and simple!

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FAT98QvyLI52rQdQfin72%252Fimage%2520%2824%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc23651df-7b47-4ed6-86d0-cce7e36489db&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ec538fc7&sv=2)

* * *

**Why It Matters:**

*   Cuts Costs: By combining two transactions into one, you pay significantly lower fees, making brc-20 transfers more affordable.
    
*   Saves Time: Skip the tedious step of creating a Transfer inscription. Enter the recipient’s address, set the amount, and send—done!
    
*   Streamlines Experience: Simplifies the process when trading brc-20 in a DEX like InSwap or in marketplace.
    
*   Batch transfers: Future updates will allow transferring to up to 1,000 addresses in a single transaction with multiple single-step transfers.
    

* * *

**New Features with Single-Step Transfer:**

**🔸 Signed Mint Inscriptions:** Inscribe mint operations using the Single-Step Transfer method - directly inscribe into OP\_RETURN to prevent creating useless UTXOs at your address.

**🔸 Batch inscribing for Single-Step Transfers (deploy/mint/traditional transfers remain individual)**, and allows spending from UTXOs carrying useless inscriptions to reduce waste and improve efficiency.

* * *

**Why Launch on Fractal First?**

As a Bitcoin-native extension, Fractal resembles Bitcoin closely in its design and adopts the Bitcoin core code, making it the perfect testing ground for upgrades before Bitcoin mainnet deployment.

Our approach to upgrades has always been to remain optimistic about innovations while maintaining steady, careful rollouts to safeguard network integrity and protect user interests. We anticipate that real-world usage on Fractal will help developers to harness the real potential of these brc-20 upgrades.

Fractal’s Highlights:

*   30-second block time — 20× faster than Bitcoin — enabling quicker confirmations and much shorter transaction wait times.
    
*   Perfect for fast-trading scenarios, such as swapping brc-20 assets on InSwap!
    

* * *

**What's Next?**

*   brc-20 Single-Step Transfer now live on Fractal Mainnet. Support will gradually roll out across UniSat services.
    
*   We will closely monitor its performance on Fractal network and continue to advocate for its deployment on Bitcoin mainnet.

The information is provided "as is," and we make no warranties regarding its accuracy. # UTXO Management | UniSat

UniSat’s UTXO Management Tool is a game-changer for Bitcoin and Fractal users juggling Ordinals, brc-20, Runes. Unlike basic unlocking tools, UniSat offers _full ecosystem integration_ and advanced UTXO optimization.

UniSat UTXO Management Tool: [https://unisat.io/utxo arrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/utxo)

Here’s why our approach is more challenging, but worth it:

**Smart Management**

*   **Reclaim BTC/FB trapped in useless inscription UTXOs:** Effortlessly consolidate UTXOs that are no longer useful like mint and transfer inscriptions in one click.
    
*   **Efficient Splitting:** Split Alkanes, Runes, BTC and FB UTXOs with clarity and control.
    
*   **Batch Send:** Send Alkanes, Ordinals, Runes, BTC and FB UTXOs in batches to different addresses to save time.
    
*   **One-Click Merge:** Easily merge Alkanes, Runes, BTC and FB UTXOs. Keep your wallet clean, organized, and reduce transaction fees.
    
*   **Clear Categorization:** UTXOs are grouped by asset type — Alkanes, Runes, Ordinals, BTC and FB — for improved clarity and reduced risk of misoperations.
    
*   **“All” Tab Features**
    
    *   View detailed UTXO information for your address — including lock/unlock status, protocol type, amount, and more.
        
    *   Custom merge useless UTXOs.
        
    *   Batch Unlock: Unlock multiple UTXOs in one sweep.
        
    *   Beyond Unlocking: Enjoy the freedom to lock any UTXOs.
        
    *   One-Click Filter: Instantly filter for locked or unlocked UTXOs for easy management.
        
    

**Power Through Integration**

*   **Cross-Platform Usability**: Unlocked UTXOs can be used seamlessly across UniSat ecosystem (Inscribe, Marketplace, InSwap, Voting) and other third-party applications through UniSat API.
    
*   **Protocol-Agnostic**: Manage Ordinals, brc-20, and Runes UTXOs in one place.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management#id-7b5a)

UniSat UTXO Management Tool


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management#id-7434)

Visual Management


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Organized by asset type: Alkanes, Runes, Ordinals, BTC(on Bitcoin) / FB(on Fractal), and All
    
*   Clear categorization for easier and more efficient asset management
    
*   Detailed breakdown of assets within each UTXO
    

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management#reclaim-btc-on-bitcoin-fb-on-fractal-trapped-in-useless-inscription-utxos)

Reclaim BTC(on Bitcoin) / FB(on Fractal) trapped in useless inscription UTXOs


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Consolidate ready-combined useless (mint and transfer) inscriptions in one click.

*   We filter out ‘useless’ brc-20 mint & transfer UTXOs—so you can turn them into BTC or FB with one-click.
    
*   Never worry about selecting the wrong UTXOs or burning valuable assets.
    
*   Clear overview of selected UTXO value, and claimable UTXO value after gas fee deduction.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fj80RMt4NIGdPO9BSMtQz%252F17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D537ca0ab-76c6-4af2-9c01-0471760a46ec&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8304050&sv=2)

**🔸 Ordinals**

*   **Batch send** up to 500 inscriptions/collections/name/ brc-20 transfer UTXOs to a designated address, save time and fees.
    
*   **Efficiently split** a UTXO containing multiple inscriptions into separate individual inscriptions.
    

_**Note:**__UTXOs that contain mixed assets (e.g., both Ordinals and Runes) cannot be operated on._

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management#runes)

**🔸 Runes**

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FHOJKgdERwqrC3gaa1TEK%252F14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5864bafc-704e-49f5-8bd8-09b88f4f91da&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3ea8a202&sv=2)

*   **Batch send** different amounts of Runes to different addresses.
    
*   **Efficiently split** Runes UTXOs for finer control.
    
    *   **Auto split:** Select and split Runes UTXOs to a designated receive address.
        
    *   **Manual split:** Select and split Runes UTXOs to multiple receive addresses with custom amounts.
        
    
*   **Custom merge** up to 500 Runes UTXOs into a single UTXO.
    

_**Note:**_

*   _UTXOs containing mixed assets cannot be operated on._
    
*   _Only UTXOs of the same Runes ticker can be operated on._
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management#btc-on-bitcoin-mainnet-and-fb-on-fractal-mainnet)

**🔸 BTC on Bitcoin Mainnet & FB on Fractal Mainnet**

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FHvC7NsxvOy90tmYKukds%252F15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D127ee432-cd90-4fd8-a7af-49e36eca4394&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7835be40&sv=2)

*   **Efficiently Split BTC/FB UTXOs**
    
    *   **Auto split:** Select and split large BTC/FB UTXOs into multiple smaller UTXOs of equal size to a designated receive address.
        
    *   **Manual split:** Select & split one or more BTC/FB UTXOs and batch send to up to 1000 receive addresses with custom amounts.
        
    
*   **Merge** up to 500 UTXOs into a single UTXO.
    
*   **Batch send** up to 500 UTXOs to a single address or up to 1000 different addresses.
    

_**Note:**_ _BTC_/FB _UTXOs that are locked cannot be operated on in this tab. Once selected, all buttons will be disabled._

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/products/utxo-management#all-utxos)

**🔸 All UTXOs**

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fh4M9ToopKoej4xHocKVs%252F16.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90a6c5e8-0f90-4486-8aa2-dc7b3b52655b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c5aac50&sv=2)

**Smart Unlocking**

*   Batch select and unlock UTXOs containing assets such as Ordinals, brc-20, Runes, and Alkanes.
    
*   Unlocked UTXOs can be used in transfers, UniSat Inscribe, and the UniSat Marketplace.
    
*   Unlock up to 500 UTXOs at once.
    
*   No fees for unlocking!
    

**Custom Locking**

*   Manually lock any UTXOs to prevent unintended spending.
    
*   Use locking to safeguard valuable UTXOs and avoid accidental transfers.
    

**Custom Merge**

*   Select and merge spendable UTXOs and dust UTXOs.
    
*   **Tip:** Unlock unused inscription UTXOs first, convert them into spendable UTXOs, and then merge them into a larger one.
    

**One-Click Filter**

*   Instantly filter for locked or unlocked UTXOs for easy management.
    

**N**_**ote:**_ _All operations under this tab are treated as BTC(Bitcoin mainnet) or FB(Fractal Mainnet) operations. For example, unlocked Runes UTXOs under this tab will be interpreted as spendable BTC/ FB . Please proceed with caution. More guidance:_ [_https://x.com/unisat\_wallet/status/1922313056996229509_arrow-up-right](https://x.com/unisat_wallet/status/1922313056996229509)

* * *

# FB Farming Legal Disclaimer | UniSat

UniSat ( “we” or “us”) provides the FB Farming / Staking feature (“Staking Feature”) to reward ecosystem users and promote sustainable growth of the Fractal Bitcoin ecosystem. Users should carefully read, understand, and accept this disclaimer and related terms before participating.

1.  **No Investment Advice**
    

This staking feature is part of product functionality and ecosystem incentives. It does not constitute any form of investment advice, financial commitment, or guaranteed returns. Participation is at the user’s own discretion and based on their risk tolerance.

1.  **Reward Structure and Risk of Forfeiture**
    

  a. Rewards are determined by multiple factors, including base APY, Tier Bonuses, Gem boosts, etc. Some rewards are only granted upon fulfilling specific criteria (e.g., staking duration, Gem expiry, etc.).

  b. If a user unstakes early (before completing the chosen staking duration), certain bonus rewards may be forfeited. The base APY will be prorated, but tier-based staking rewards and Gem boost rewards can only be obtained upon completion of the full staking period.

1.  **Market and Value Volatility Risk**
    

  a. The market price of FB may rise or fall. During the staking period, if price depreciation of FB exceeds the value of rewards earned, user’s net asset value may be reduced.

  b. Rewards when converted, traded, or withdrawn may incur losses due to market prices, liquidity issues, transaction fees, or slippage.

1.  **Reward Pool Capacity and Staking Limits**
    

  a. Some staking or bonus farming pools have a maximum reward allocation (e.g., Pool 1 with 1,000,000 FB). Early participants may consume a large portion of rewards, leaving limited or no rewards for later participants.  

b. Minimum or maximum staking amounts per address / wallet may apply. Exceeding or not meeting these limits may result in inability to stake as expected or reward calculations being different.

1.  **Technical and System Risks**
    

  Although FB Farming utilizes Taproot scripts, the UTXO model, and a non-custodial design for enhanced security, technical upgrades, protocol changes, third-party factors, or force majeure events may still lead to modifications, interruptions, or termination of the staking program.

1.  **Compliance and Taxation Obligations**
    

  a. Users must ensure their participation complies with applicable laws and regulations in their jurisdiction.  

b. Any taxes or obligations arising from reward earnings are the sole responsibility of the user. We are not liable for any tax consequences.

1.  **User Operation Risk**
    

  a. Users may make mistakes during staking, adding Gems, selecting staking duration, or unstaking, which may result in loss of certain rewards or assets.  

b. Before any such operation, user should carefully read on-screen warnings, risk alert boxes, and all relevant terms.

1.  **Limitation of Liability**
    

We shall not be liable for any losses of asset value, reduced or delayed rewards, interruption or termination of service, or failure to attain expected returns caused by market volatility, system or network failure, protocol changes, third-party actions, force majeure, or any other cause. In no event shall UniSat be liable to you for any loss of profits, revenue, goodwill, business opportunities, or for any indirect, incidental, special, consequential, or punitive damages arising out of or related to your participation in the staking program.

1.  **Right to Modify, Suspend, or Terminate and Final Interpretation**
    

We reserve the right to modify, suspend or terminate the staking feature or related activities at any time (including but not limited to changes to reward structures, duration, Gem conditions, APY etc.), and retain the final right of interpretation over this feature and its activities.

# How to Trade Runes？ | UniSat

Go to [https://unisat.io/runes/marketarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/runes/market)
, and search for rune.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F3Vfdv8pnq8yWTjkbX35n%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31d68f25-607a-46e4-a18f-06aed6872a70&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6e37fc5&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fhh3wIfgHcvohreZgdFVF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63061aaa-9e21-4356-a101-06ba198c38e6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=395a3fe8&sv=2)

You can buy the Rune one by one or in batches.

You can also list/unlist or update prices for your rune assets by clicking ‘My Assets’.

*   List Runes: Click ‘My Assets’ and then click ‘List’ button beside Rune, then you will get the List page as below,
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FhZ4rQYycnAd2N5hHQ8a5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddaa1eb34-d259-4be1-b4ef-6e3788a4f2d7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c0ca2f39&sv=2)

*   After setting the price and signing via Wallet, it will be listed.
    
*   You may go to My Orders to view the listed order, update price or unlist your Rune asset.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F46C1KNObzDmUlfIhjcX4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D37ad3484-3f09-479d-8d57-86f5f3402b84&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=10843115&sv=2)

# InSwap Terms Of Use | UniSat

Last Updated: October 09, 2025

These InSwap Terms of Use (“Agreement”) constitute a binding agreement between you (“User” or “you”) and UniPro Technology Limited (“UniPro”, “we”, “us”, or “our”) and any of our affiliates regarding your access to and/or use of the InSwap services (collectively, “Services”). This Agreement applies to all actions you perform through InSwap.

By using our Services, you acknowledge that you have read, understood, and accepted this Agreement, the UniSat Terms of Use (“Service Terms”), the Privacy Policy, and any and all other rules or policies. Regardless of your jurisdiction, nationality, or the Services you use, you are legally bound by all terms and conditions herein. If you do not agree to be bound by this Agreement, do not access or use the Services. This Agreement supplements the Service Terms. In the event of any conflict or inconsistency between the terms of this Agreement and the Service Terms, such conflict or inconsistency shall be resolved by prioritizing this Agreement. All provisions of the Service Terms not modified by this Agreement shall remain in full force and effect. Any capitalized terms not defined herein shall have the meanings assigned to them in the Service Terms.

**1\. The Services.**

1.1 Product Description of InSwap.

InSwap is the first open-source AMM DEX for Bitcoin-Native Assets, built natively on Bitcoin and Fractal. The platform provides a seamless trading experience while maintaining the robust decentralization and security standards of Bitcoin assets, enabling Users to swap, provide Liquidity, and earn native protocol assets across both networks without intermediaries. For more detailed product information, please refer to [https://docs.unisat.io/services/products/inswaparrow-up-right](https://docs.unisat.io/services/products/inswap)
.

1.2 Scope of Eligible Assets.

The Services currently support only Bitcoin-Native Assets. The following categories of assets are explicitly excluded:

1.  Legal and Regulatory Requirements: Assets deemed by resolution of a competent government authority, court ruling, or internal legal review to constitute regulated financial instruments (e.g., securities or derivatives);
    
2.  Fraud Allegations: Assets whose owners or controllers are subject to fraud allegations by major financial or criminal regulatory authorities;
    
3.  Intellectual Property Claims: Assets alleged by third parties to infringe intellectual property rights; and
    
4.  User Risks: Assets we determine to pose technical, fraudulent, or other risks that may materially compromise user safety.
    

1.3 Service Offerings.

Based on the characteristics of the AMM model, InSwap provides the following functions for Users to use:

1.  Create Trading Pair and Deploy Liquidity Pool;
    
2.  Deposit and withdraw funds from modules;
    
3.  Add or remove Liquidity;
    
4.  Send assets to other addresses within the module, assets are restricted to use within the module only; and
    
5.  Swap assets.
    

**2\. User Eligibility and Responsibilities.**

2.1 To use the Services, you must declare that you are of legal age, have the legal capacity to enter into contracts, and possess full legal authority to agree to and comply with this Agreement on behalf of yourself and any company/entity. You will not be accessing the Services in a jurisdiction where such Services are not permitted, restricted or illegal.

2.2 You further represent and warrant to us that you, the legal entity you represent, or any person(s) owning or controlling you or such legal entity, are not listed on any trade or economic sanctions lists maintained by any competent authorities, and you shall not engage in transactions with any listed parties, including but not limited to (1) the Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant (ISIL/Daesh), Al-Qaeda, the Taliban, and associated individuals, groups, enterprises, and entities; any individuals or entities designated by the United Nations Security Council or the United Arab Emirates; (2) the Democratic People’s Republic of Korea (DPRK), the Islamic Republic of Iran, or individuals, groups, enterprises, entities listed on sanctions lists maintained by the UN Security Council, the U.S. government (e.g., OFAC Sanctions List), the European Union or its member states, the Monetary Authority of Singapore (MAS), the Hong Kong Monetary Authority (HKMA), the Hong Kong Customs and Excise Department, or other applicable governmental authorities; and (3) you are not a “U.S. Person” as defined under 17 CFR § 230.902. We reserve the right, at our sole discretion, to construe, limit, and modify the scope of Services in any jurisdiction at any time and to determine, at our sole discretion, your eligibility to access or use this Agreement and the Services. You acknowledge that such determinations may affect your ability to access or use the Services and agree to bear all associated risks and consequences. If you fail to meet such eligibility requirements, we may, temporarily or permanently, suspend, restrict or terminate your access to the Services.

2.3 You are solely responsible for managing your private keys and safeguarding your assets. We do not custody, possess, or control your assets. We assume no liability or obligation for your use of wallets. We shall not be liable for any claims, damages, losses, or liabilities arising from infringement of your wallet or assets.

2.4 Prohibited Activities. You affirm that your access to and use of the Services will fully comply with applicable laws and regulations, and you shall not engage in, promote, or facilitate any illegal activities through the Services, including but not limited to, money laundering, market manipulation, cyberattacks, fraud, or misrepresentation.

**3\. Fees and Payments.**

3.1 Network Fees. While accessing and using the Services, you are required to pay transaction fees to the relevant network.

3.2 Swap Fees. Every swap incurs a 1.5% transaction fee. 1/6 of this fee goes to the platform, while the rest is distributed among Liquidity Providers (LPs).

3.3 Third-Party Service Fees. During your access and use of the Services, additional third-party protocol fees may apply. You are solely responsible for paying any and all third-party protocol fees that may arise.

3.4 We reserve the right to modify fees at any time with or without prior notice to you.

**4\. Risks and Disclaimers.**

4.1 Market Volatility Risk. You acknowledge that asset prices are subject to uncontrollable factors such as market supply/demand, industry events, regulatory changes, and macroeconomic conditions, which may cause extreme price fluctuations or even total devaluation. You alone bear all losses arising from market volatility, including asset depreciation, slippage, or unexpected exchange ratios in Liquidity pools.

4.2 Fake Asset Risk. You understand that anyone may create assets, including counterfeit versions of existing assets or fraudulent claims of project representation. You accept the risk of inadvertently swaping such assets, and we assume no liability for losses caused by your participation in counterfeit asset transactions.

4.3 AMM Impermanent Loss Risk. Impermanent Loss refers to the potential loss where the value of Liquidity Provider (LP) assets falls below the value of holding the original assets due to price divergence within a Liquidity pool. This is an inherent feature of decentralized exchanges (DEX) directly tied to market volatility. By providing Liquidity, you fully acknowledge and voluntarily assume this risk, and we disclaim all liabilities for such losses.

4.4 Regulatory Risk. You recognize that digital asset markets are nascent, and regulatory policies vary across jurisdictions and may evolve, potentially adversely impacting service availability or asset value. You must ensure your use complies with local laws and regulations.

4.5 Technical Risk. We assume no liability for losses caused by technical failures, including hacker attacks, viruses, system adjustments, website upgrades, legal/government-mandated shutdowns, or third-party blockchain disruptions affecting InSwap’s operations.

4.6 Derivative Function Risks. You acknowledge that during your use of the Services, you assume risks arising from operating various features, including but not limited to: Burning LP, which will cause permanent lockup of Liquidity, forfeiture of assets, and irrevocable loss of all associated rights, value/utility.

4.7 Force Majeure. We disclaim responsibility for losses arising from force majeure events such as natural disasters, wars, network failures, or power outages or damages arising from any event beyond our reasonable control.

4.8 Non-Investment Advice. For the avoidance of doubt, we do not provide any financial, investment or legal advice in connection with the Services. Any incentives provided to enhance user experience, including those involving third-party community assets accessed through activities, shall not be construed as investment advice. Your use of the Services and participation in activities are unsolicited, self-directed, and solely your responsibility.

4.9 You agree that the above factors may lead to abnormal trading conditions, price fluctuations, market disruptions, or other irregularities. This disclaimer is non-exhaustive, and we reserve the right to perform special handling operations on certain assets or their transaction orders. You further agree that we assume no liability for losses related to these risks.

If no settlement is reached within sixty (60) days of our first email to commence the negotiations, the Dispute shall be resolved exclusively by arbitration in accordance with Section 8.2 below.

8.2 Any Dispute shall be referred to and finally resolved by arbitration administered by the Hong Kong International Arbitration Centre (HKIAC) in accordance with the HKIAC Administered Arbitration Rules in force when the Notice of Arbitration is submitted. The law of this arbitration clause shall be Hong Kong law. The number of arbitrators shall be one. The arbitration proceedings shall be conducted in English. The fees and expenses of the arbitral tribunal shall be determined on the basis of \[Schedule 2/ Schedule 3\] of these Rules. The arbitration shall take place in Hong Kong, unless both you and us mutually agree on an alternative location.

8.3 Class Action Waiver. YOU AND WE AGREE THAT EACH MAY BRING CLAIMS AGAINST THE OTHER ONLY ON AN INDIVIDUAL BASIS, AND NOT AS A PLAINTIFF OR CLASS MEMBER IN ANY PURPORTED CLASS OR REPRESENTATIVE PROCEEDING. YOU AND WE EXPRESSLY WAIVE ANY RIGHT TO FILE A CLASS ACTION OR SEEK RELIEF ON A CLASS BASIS. Unless both you and we agree, no arbitrator or judge may consolidate more than one person’s claims or otherwise preside over any form of a representative or class proceeding. The arbitrator may award injunctive relief only in favor of the individual party seeking relief and only to the extent necessary to provide relief warranted by that party’s individual claim. If a court decides that applicable law precludes enforcement of any of this paragraph’s limitations as to a particular claim for relief, then that claim (and only that claim) must be severed from the arbitration and may be brought in court. If any court or arbitrator determines that the class action waiver set forth in this paragraph is void or unenforceable for any reason or that an arbitration can proceed on a class basis, then the arbitration provision set forth above shall be deemed null and void in its entirety and the parties shall be deemed to have not agreed to arbitrate disputes.

**9\. Miscellaneous.**

9.1 When using the Services, if there is any conflict between the terms of this Agreement and the Service Terms regarding the interpretation, division of responsibilities, or rights and obligations related to InSwap services, the explicit provisions of this Agreement shall prevail.

9.2 To this Agreement. We reserve the right, at our sole discretion, to add, modify or replace any part of this Agreement (including any Policies) at any time, and all modifications will be effective when they are posted. It is your responsibility to check this Agreement periodically for changes. Your continued use of or access to the Services following the posting of any changes to this Agreement constitutes acceptance of those changes. If you do not agree with any modifications to this Agreement, you must immediately stop accessing and using all of our Services.

9.3 If you encounter intellectual property infringement, need to report a complaint, or have a potential Dispute with us while using our Services, you may contact us by emailing contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.unisat.io/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#4c20292b2d200c3922253f2d38622523)
 or through other official communication channels.

**10\. Definitions.**

“Bitcoin-Native Assets” means Cryptographic assets created directly on the Bitcoin blockchain or its core extension protocols, without relying on external independent blockchains, including but not limited to Ordinals, Alkanes, and related protocol assets to be created in the future.

“Automated Market Maker” or “AMM” means a decentralized exchange mechanism that facilitates peer-to-peer asset trading through algorithmically managed Liquidity pools, eliminating the need for traditional order books. Prices are determined by predefined mathematical formulas (e.g., constant product formulas), and Liquidity Providers contribute assets to these pools in exchange for proportional transaction fees and Liquidity pool assets.

“Liquidity” refers to digital assets deposited by users into algorithmically managed pools on InSwap to enable peer-to-peer trading through its Automated Market Maker (AMM) infrastructure. Liquidity is deployed in paired configurations and the ratio of assets within a pool determines exchange rates for swaps.

“LP/LPs (Liquidity Provider/Liquidity Providers)” means a user who contributes digital assets to a Liquidity pool on InSwap.

“slippage” means the difference between the price you expect to receive after swapping and what you actually receive after the swap is complete, occurring due to market volatility or insufficient Liquidity in a pool during the execution interval.

# Runes | UniSat

Runes is a fungible token protocol built natively on Bitcoin. It aims to provide a simple, efficient, and UTXO-friendly way to issue and transfer fungible tokens on Bitcoin, without requiring off-chain infrastructure or complex indexers. Runes defines a method for creating and transferring fungible tokens on Bitcoin using standard transaction fields like OP\_RETURN.

*   Simple: The protocol logic is minimal and does not rely on external systems.
    
*   On-chain: All state and transfer data are embedded within Bitcoin transactions.
    
*   UTXO-native: Assets are stored and moved through Bitcoin’s native UTXO structure.
    

UniSat provides full protocol-level support for Runes, including:

*   Mint & Etch Runes: Users can define new Rune tickers(etch) or mint runes through [UniSat Inscribearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/runes/inscribe)
    
*   Wallet Integration: Rune balances and transactions are supported directly in the UniSat Wallet, enabling send and receive functions
    
*   Marketplace: UniSat's marketplace enables the trading of Runes tickers through [UniSat Marketplacearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/runes/market)
    
*   Explorer: Users can browse Rune assets, holders, and activity via the Rune section of [UniScanarrow-up-right](https://uniscan.cc/runes)
    

More information: [https://docs.ordinals.com/runes/specification.html arrow-up-right](https://docs.ordinals.com/runes/specification.html)

# How to Participate in BTC Staking on Babylon Using UniSat Wallet | UniSat

We support you in using UniSat Extension Wallet to participate in Babylon’s BTC staking activities, offering a seamless Bitcoin staking experience. This guide is for reference only. Participation in staking is at the user’s own discretion and responsibility.

**Step 1: Prepare Your UniSat Wallet**

Please ensure that your UniSat Extension Wallet or UniSat App Wallet is updated to the latest version. Click this link to download or update: [https://unisat.io/downloadarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/download)

**Step 2: Access the Babylon DApp**

*   Switch your network to Bitcoin Mainnet.
    
*   Open the wallet menu at the bottom, click Discover (DApp Center), find Babylon, and click to enter.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FD8PQsKARKUmx9Oo7nlnm%252F1.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcb5b0457-0e0c-4489-bf98-99e6f618e81b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d1b4500b&sv=2)

**Step 3: Participate in Babylon Phase 2 Staking**

1.  After entering the Babylon Bitcoin Staking interface, you will see the **Babylon Bitcoin Staking Phase 2** page. Click the **Go to Babylon** button to proceed to the staking page.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FFsHiwFmy0egTREf4QSLr%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D420bd808-5108-4c77-be04-54c4d5c99a7f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ce9c3e8e&sv=2)

1.  Click the **Connect Wallet** button in the top right corner. You will be prompted to connect your Bitcoin wallet address and your Babylon chain wallet address. Please select your **UniSat Wallet** for both.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FScCKSEWSuABQ2CfUBY58%252F3.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1fa0ba11-9e71-4314-922d-a5f2e3546c90&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4862c7b9&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F1lRAZEJUaSnfUYeJjxyZ%252F4.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db170cbd1-fd8e-4f83-abc6-b7ce47a8a4bc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=76960ec9&sv=2)

1.  Choose the staking pool you want to participate in, enter the amount of BTC you wish to stake, confirm the amount, and click **Preview** to sign and complete the transaction.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F0i4Ct8VfVoBagMHgntgA%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D329872a8-dbbb-45bc-8165-1d3cf7943a1b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b64fd038&sv=2)

1.  Once your staking is complete, you can view your staking history in the **Staking History** section.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FvoYf2xBtKeDOr5PsRggj%252F6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2dfd9469-8e0e-4b4f-b23b-b394119b5267&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f8c60069&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/events/babylon-staking-activity/how-to-participate-in-btc-staking-on-babylon-using-unisat-wallet#tips)

# What is Bitcoin? | UniSat

Instead of relying on a central bank to issue and manage the currency, Bitcoin utilizes a distributed ledger, the blockchain, to record all transactions in a transparent and immutable manner. This ledger is maintained by a network of computers, known as miners, who compete to solve complex cryptographic puzzles. By solving these puzzles, miners not only verify transactions but also earn Bitcoin rewards, ensuring the network's security and incentivizing further participation.

Beyond its unique infrastructure, Bitcoin offers individuals a new form of digital currency. Transactions are conducted quickly and securely, without the need for intermediaries or cross-border restrictions. This opens up a world of possibilities, from sending money across the globe to making online purchases with newfound ease.

However, Bitcoin's decentralized nature also presents its own set of challenges. Scalability remains a hurdle, as the current network struggles to handle large volumes of transactions. Additionally, the absence of central oversight raises concerns about regulatory uncertainty.

Despite these challenges, Bitcoin's impact on the financial world is undeniable. It has paved the way for a new era of digital currencies and decentralized finance, sparking innovation and challenging traditional financial systems. With its limited supply of 21 million coins, Bitcoin's value is primarily driven by market demand, leading to significant price fluctuations. This volatility, coupled with its revolutionary technology and potential for future growth, continues to attract investors and enthusiasts alike.

**Disclaimer:**

# How does Bitcoin work? | UniSat

At the heart of Bitcoin lies the blockchain, a distributed ledger system that records every transaction ever made. This public ledger ensures transparency and immutability, preventing fraudulent activity. Transactions are initiated by users with digital signatures, verified by miners, and then added to the blockchain in blocks.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/bitcoin/how-does-bitcoin-work#securing-and-validating-the-network)

Securing and Validating the Network

Mining is the process of verifying and adding new transactions to the blockchain. It also serves the essential role of securing the network through a computational puzzle called proof-of-work (PoW).

**Mempool**

New transactions are broadcast to the network by users. These transactions can involve sending Bitcoin, creating new contracts, or changing existing ones. The transactions are temporarily stored in a distributed memory pool, accessible by all nodes on the network. Fees act as a digital tipping system, guiding miners towards transactions that promise greater rewards.

**Block Creation**

Miners compete to collect and group unconfirmed transactions into blocks. Each block has a limited capacity, so miners choose transactions that maximize their potential reward. Miners add a "coinbase" transaction to each block, which is essentially a reward for themselves for successfully creating the block.

**Hashing**

Hashing is a cryptographic function that takes any data as input and generates a unique, fixed-length output. In the context of Bitcoin mining, the input consists of the block header, including the previous block's hash, timestamp, and Merkle root. Miners use specialized hardware called ASICs to perform billions of calculations per second, attempting to find a hash that starts with a certain number of zeros. It is often described as "solving a complex mathematical puzzle". This difficulty is adjusted automatically to maintain the average block creation time at approximately 10 minutes.

**Block Validation**

Once a miner finds a valid hash, they broadcast the new block to the network. Other nodes on the network verify the block by:

*   Recalculating the hash and ensuring it meets the difficulty requirements.
    
*   Validating all transactions within the block.
    
*   Checking the block header information for accuracy and consistency.
    

If the block is valid, it is added to the blockchain, and the successful miner receives their reward in Bitcoin. Blocks are considered confirmed after a certain number of subsequent blocks have been added to the chain. This typically requires six confirmations, making it very difficult to alter or tamper with previously confirmed blocks.

**Disclaimer:**

The content of this document is for informational purposes only. It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. Digital assets (including FTs and NFTs) are subject to market volatility, involve high risk, regulatory changes, and may depreciate in value. The information is provided "as is," and we make no warranties regarding its accuracy. # FAQ | UniSat

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/alkanes/faq#id-1.-how-do-i-import-other-wallets-into-unisat)

1\. How do I import other wallets into UniSat?

We recommend creating a new UniSat wallet and sending your Alkanes assets to this new wallet.

❌ Directly importing your mnemonic or private key is not advised. Doing so may expose your assets to risk if your key is leaked or stolen during the process.

* * *

**2\. How do I create a new Alkanes wallet in UniSat?**

First, make sure your UniSat Wallet is updated to the latest version or download it [herearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/download)

*   On the wallet homepage, tap the **HD Wallet** icon in the top-left corner to access wallet management.
    
*   Click the **“+”** button to create a new wallet.
    

When creating a new wallet, you can choose from **four address types** — **all are fully compatible with Alkanes.** Select the one that suits your preferences; you can switch later if needed.

_Important: Be sure to securely back up your mnemonic phrase — this is essential for future recovery._

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FYtiRgG63CtvkqeLbRzIl%252F22.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D47b01d02-f3ce-427a-b706-c3d1123998e4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb8050d8&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F6OPn62R5acaazDM6qViW%252F23.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5c15660-2167-47a0-a760-2dd0ee8cb4db&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2d99e84a&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/alkanes/faq#id-3.-do-i-need-to-care-about-address-type-when-sending-or-receiving-alkanes-in-unisat)

3\. **Do I need to care about address type when sending or receiving Alkanes in UniSat?**

*   Sending to UniSat wallet: No. UniSat supports Alkanes across all address types.
    
*   Receiving in UniSat wallet: No. UniSat wallet supports Alkanes across all address types
    
*   Sending from UniSat Wallet to other wallets: yes. Because other wallets may be double-address wallets that only support Alkanes on specific address types. - Please refer to target wallets for instructions on which address you should send your Alkanes to. For example, only bc1p address type supports Alkanes on Oyl Wallet. When sending to Oyl wallet, please send to bc1p.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/alkanes/faq#id-4.-can-i-batch-send-alkanes-assets-to-multiple-wallets-through-idclub-using-unisat-wallet)

4\. **Can I batch-send Alkanes assets to multiple wallets through idclub using unisat wallet??**

Yes, you can batch-send Alkanes via UniSat.

⚠️ However, the number of assets you can send in one batch is limited by OP\_RETURN data size.  

If your batch exceeds the limit, you will receive a pop-up warning message.

*   Improved balance display: Now differentiates between "**Available**" and "**Unavailable**" balances.
    

\- Available: BTC you can safely spend now.

\- Unavailable: Includes BTC in inscriptions, ARC20, pending balances for addresses with Atomicals enabled, and BTC beyond the first 500 UTXOs for those holding a large number of UTXOs.

\- You'll be able to pick specific UTXO from the "Unavailable" set in the next update.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252F3eT97nLlzR1rmGJKba1O%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5f7b9c2-67a6-42d7-8003-26cc0a06cfd9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6fc6ebe7&sv=2)

[Previousv1.3.0chevron-left](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-wallet/release-notes/v1.3.0)
[NextUniSat Inscribechevron-right](https://docs.unisat.io/products/unisat-inscribe)

Last updated 1 year ago

# UniSat Credits | UniSat

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/unisat-credits#id-5b65)

What is Credits?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Credit is a ‘virtual’ FB that can be used towards service fee offset and other benefits across our products. It is designed to reward users who have been long-term supporters and have made significant contributions to our network.

Please note that **Credit is not an on-chain asset. It is non-transferable, non-tradable, and can only be used within the UniSat ecosystem.**

The first batch of eligible addresses that will receive the Credits includes miners that have successfully mined blocks during Fractal Testnet, early testers of brc20 swap on Bitcoin mainnet, and users who had difficulties with claim during the Fractal Bitcoin Mainnet Bootstrap Program.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FKE1lGQFz3B5P5mDHR1qc%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb45f5df-97aa-4782-b952-a3f3af944f04&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db1d26fd&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/unisat-credits#id-6221)

How Does Credits Work?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Credits can be used to offset Rollup Fee on InSwap and to offset service fees in UniSat Inscribe & Marketplace, replacing the FB or BTC you would typically use. When trading on InSwap or inscribing, simply select “Credits” for rollup fee deductions.

Over time, we plan to expand the use of these Credits to other UniSat services, such as UniSat Inscribe, UniSat Marketplace, and other features in the future.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/unisat-credits#id-6dfb)

Eligibility for Credits


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users eligible to receive **Goodwill Credit** include:

1.  **Initially eligible users who were later unable to claim during the Fractal Bitcoin Mainnet Bootstrap Program**
    

*   90FB worth of credit in total for each address, with 15FB credits distributed monthly over six consecutive months.
    

**2\. Miner addresses that participated in Fractal Testnet mining and successfully mined blocks:**

*   Credit will be distributed based on the total number of successful blocks mined. Each block is worth 0.5 FB. For addresses that mined fewer than 40 blocks (inclusive), a minimum threshold of 20 FB worth of credit will be granted. The maximum cap is 1500 FB per address. Addresses with 0 blocks mined will not be eligible for this benefit.
    
*   For addresses eligible to receive more than 20 FB worth of Credits, the Credits will be distributed monthly with a cap of 20 FB worth of Credits each month until the full amount is dispersed.
    
*   If you are a Fractal testnet miner who has mined blocks but has not received any credits, please contact us and create a ticket on Discord [http://discord.gg/unisatarrow-up-right](http://discord.gg/unisat)
    

**3\. Addresses that participated in early testing of the brc20-swap on the Bitcoin Mainnet:**

*   20 FB worth of credit for each address, distributed monthly over six consecutive months.
    

**4\. Addresses with 1,000 or more UniSat Points:**

*   If you have 1000 or more UniSat Points, you’re eligible to receive a total of 60FB worth of credit, with 10 FB Credits distributed monthly over six consecutive months.
    

**Note:** Monthly Credits not claimed in the current month will expire when next month’s Credits become available.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/unisat-credits#d3ea)

How to Get Started with the Credit?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  If you qualify, please visit [https://unisat.io/address/creditarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/address/credit)
     or connect your wallet and click on “Credits” to claim it.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FdLztanjPZHTuoUXgCAAj%252F33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D06b8c896-4bcd-4c76-a8e0-4e510d1fb2ce&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e442e6a3&sv=2)

2\. When inscribing or trading on InSwap /Marketplace, select “Credits” for rollup fee deductions.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FaZe3vJY0g393rEqiqvku%252F666.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1b5829fd-ff9d-4216-809b-9117b47c6a07&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=912f463c&sv=2)

# UniSat Points | UniSat

UniSat Points is a tool designed by UniSat to count the number of user inscriptions and calculate how many users participate in UniSat interactions.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/unisat-points#points-can-be-earned-through-inscribing)

**Points can be earned through i**nscribing

**🔸 On Bitcoin mainnet**

Points can be earned when using the inscribe service **and a service fee is charged**. The specific rules for earning points are as follows:

> _No points will be awarded for fee-free inscriptions._

*   1 ≤ Inscribing quantity in a batch ≤ 4 👉 Earn **1 Point**
    
*   5 ≤ Inscribing quantity in a batch ≤ 20 👉 Earn **2 Points**
    
*   21 ≤ Inscribing quantity in a batch ≤ 32 👉 Earn **3 Points**
    
*   33 ≤ Inscribing quantity in a batch ≤ 1000 👉 Earn **4 Points**
    

_The points are accumulated on the receiving address of the inscription, not the payment address._

**🔸 Fractal Bitcoin Mainnet**

*   Inscribing quantity in a batch = 1000 👉 Earn **1 Point**
    

_(Batch Minting: Up to 1000 inscriptions per batch )_

_The points are accumulated on the receiving address of the inscription, not the payment address._

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/unisat-points#points-can-be-earned-through-consolidating-useless-inscriptions-utxos)

**Points can be earned through c**onsolidating **u**seless inscriptions UTXOs

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FiqiAS3uDqSOhFRRK3JGY%252F22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D433ebb50-9093-4455-b771-5106d059d1ac&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b25c6b7&sv=2)

**🔸 On Bitcoin Mainnet** ([UTXO Management Toolarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/utxo)
)

Points are awarded based on the number of UTXOs you consolidate(X) - _Points are awarded only when a service fee is incurred._

*   50 ≤ X < 300 👉 Earn **1 Point**
    
*   300 ≤ X < 500 👉 Earn **2 Points**
    
*   X = 500 👉 Earn **3 Points**
    

**🔸 On Fractal Mainnet** ( [UTXO Management Toolarrow-up-right](https://fractal.unisat.io/utxo)
)

Points are awarded based on the number of UTXOs you consolidate (X)

*   X = 500 👉 Earn **1 Point**
    

* * *

**Benefits of UniSat Points**

*   Enjoy discounted transaction fees on UniSat Marketplace. More details: [https://docs.unisat.io/services/unisat-marketplace-fee-ratesarrow-up-right](https://docs.unisat.io/services/unisat-marketplace-fee-rates)
    
*   brc20-swap is currently accessible only to addresses with either 200 UniSat Points or those owning brc20-swap Prime Access inscription on mainnet.( Currently, the swap module only supports viewing balances, removing liquidity, and in-module transfers of BRC-20 assets. The trading service is temporarily under maintenance.)
    

**Disclaimer:**

Digital assets (including FTs and NFTs) are subject to market volatility, involve high risk, regulatory changes, and may depreciate in value. # Alkanes | UniSat

**What is Alkanes？**

Alkanes is a token-based smart contract metaprotocol built on the protorunes framework using the protorunes standard, designed to enable smart contract functionality through a combination of WebAssembly (WASM) and UTXO-based transactions.

**Key Features**

*   UTXO-Based Smart Contracts
    

Alkanes leverages Bitcoin’s UTXO model to deploy smart contracts, embedding WASM code through inscriptions similar to Ordinals for on-chain execution.

*   WASM-Driven with Storage Optimization
    

Contracts are written in Rust, compiled into gzip-compressed WASM binaries, and embedded in Bitcoin transactions to align with storage constraints.

*   Protorunes Framework
    

Built on the Protorunes standard, inheriting design patterns from Ordinals and Runes, using a witness envelope to deploy WASM files and enable contract interactions.

*   Metashrew Open-Source Indexer for Contract State Tracking
    

Integrates the open-source Metashrew indexer to track contract states, supporting real-time data access and validation on Bitcoin.

**UniSat Product Support for Alkanes**

*   UniSat Wallet
    
*   UniScan
    
*   UniSat UTXO Management Tool
    
*   UniSat Marketplace
    

Learn more: [https://alkanes.build/docs/developers/disclaimerarrow-up-right](https://alkanes.build/docs/developers/disclaimer)

It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. # Happy April Fool’s Day! | UniSat

This is not an April 1st joke

We just decided to make UniSat API COMPLETELY FREE across all features for the next three months.

All existing subscriptions will be automatically extended by three months. For example, if your subscription was set to expire on May 1, you will now have access until August 1—three extra months for free.

We’ve noticed that many projects and services are actively working to reduce their costs. We’re happy to support developers by making our API free for them, ensuring that more Bitcoin developers feel comfortable to build with our help.

To better prepare for the upcoming brc-20 upgrade, we’ll also be rolling out more events and activities for developers and the community. Stay tuned! 🚀

# How to Etch Runes? | UniSat

You may visit [https://unisat.io/runes/inscribearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/runes/inscribe)
 to get the page.

Input the parameters as needed.

_**For example**_：

The _**Rune**_ Name is EVERYONE.LOVES.NATURE.FOREVER,

_**Symbol**_ is E,

It is _**Mintable**_, and _**Amount**_ was settled as 500, _**Cap**_ for 4,000,000.

The _**Premine**_ is 15,000.

And leave other fields empty.Then you could input the above needed text as shown below,

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FCR5zzd7NfA9OxQmXXcH1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1752c894-051b-4b5d-8286-1d86bdd0bff7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=87ccaf05&sv=2)

_Please note: you need to wait for 5 blocks confirmations for etching._

After the Rune is confirmed as valid, the etcher will get 15000E EVERYONE.LOVES.NATURE.FOREVER. Meantime, the others can mint Rune EVERYONE.LOVES.NATURE.FOREVER.

Following is the introduction for each parameter:

_**Rune:**_ Runes name, (currently you can ethi 13-26 characters long, can be separated by a middle dot ·, and the separator does not count towards the character limit).

_**Symbol (optional):**_ The symbol after the number of runes, which can be A-Z or empty. If empty, a general symbol ¤ will be used.

_**Mintable:**_ Toggle off to disable further minting. Runes are only premine upon creation.

_**Amount:**_ The Amount field contains the amount of runes each mint transaction receives.

_**Cap:**_ The number of times a rune may be minted is its cap. A mint is closed once the cap is reached.

_**Advanced options:**_ Set up premining, divisible figures, and the starting or ending block where minting is possible (optional).

_**Premine :**_ The etcher of a rune may optionally allocate to themselves units of the runes being etched. This allocation is called a premine.

_**Divisibility (optional):**_ A rune's divisibility is how finely it may be divided into its atomic units. Divisibility is expressed as the number of digits permissible after the decimal point in the amount of runes. A rune with divisibility 0 may not be divided. A unit of a rune with divisibility 1 may be divided into ten sub-units, a rune with divisibility 2 may be divided into a hundred, and so on.

_**Absolute Height:**_ The absolute block height (based on the current block height).

_**Relative Height：**_The range of relative block heights (based on the block of etching real).

_**Start Height：**_A mint is open starting in the block with the given start height.

_**End Height：**_A rune may not be minted in or after the block with the given end height.

Minded: You can find the Premine setting on the pop-up page after clicking _**Advanced Options**_.

**Disclaimer:**

The content of this document is for informational purposes only. It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. Digital assets (including FTs and NFTs) are subject to market volatility, involve high risk, regulatory changes, and may depreciate in value. The information is provided "as is," and we make no warranties regarding its accuracy. Please consult your legal, tax, or investment professionals to determine whether trading or holding digital assets is suitable for you.

# Name recognized and resolved | UniSat

A name can be recognized and resolved to an address by an inscription. Each name have a unique inscription associated with it.

Once a name inscription is inscribed or transferred, it is only resolved to an address after achieving 3 confirmations. At present, we support the following name inscription protocols, with more domains being gradually made available based on user demand.

name

protocol

network

.sats

[satsnamearrow-up-right](https://docs.sats.id/)

Bitcoin

.unisat

[satsnamearrow-up-right](https://docs.sats.id/)

Bitcoin

.x

[satsnamearrow-up-right](https://docs.sats.id/)

Bitcoin

.btc

[btcnamearrow-up-right](https://docs.btcname.id/)

Bitcoin

.fb

[satsnamearrow-up-right](https://docs.sats.id/)

Fractal

It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. Digital assets (including FTs and NFTs) are subject to market volatility, involve high risk, regulatory changes, and may depreciate in value. The information is provided "as is," and we make no warranties regarding its accuracy. Please consult your legal, tax, or investment professionals to determine whether trading or holding digital assets is suitable for you.

Whether you're a curious newcomer or a seasoned enthusiast, this category is designed to demystify the complexities surrounding Bitcoin and empower you with essential knowledge. Let's build a foundational understanding of the world of Bitcoin together.

# How to Mint Runes? | UniSat

Go to Mint option on page [https://unisat.io/runes/inscribearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/runes/inscribe)
.

Or you could explore Rune information on [https://unisat.io/runes/listarrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/runes/list)
 and Click ‘Mint Directly’ button if the rune can be mintable for more convenience.

You could input the _**Rune or Rune ID**_ as below.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252Fz482fDtRbiXaXfQuqapK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64f5a17e-2d65-4c8c-9e4e-73e4c7b70fdb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6509337&sv=2)

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FODmNseZuYgBrpa3nIwih%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a78de5b-191b-4d71-82bb-e5188f2fb8d7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4d7fa101&sv=2)

You can input the number of _**Repet Mint**_ or use the slide bar for batch minting.

_**Let’s take the Rune: EVERYONE.LOVES.NATURE.FOREVER for example.**_

There will be 500E for one minting. If _**Repeat Mint**_\=53, the balance is 500\*53=26500E

EVERYONE.LOVES.NATURE.FOREVER after minting transaction was confirmed. At the same time, the _**Cap**_ of this Rune was reduced from 4,000,000 to 3,999,947.

After the transaction (including etching, minting, etc) has been confirmed on chain, you may refer to the following formula for the current total supply of Rune：

_**Supply=Premine+Amount\*Mints**_

1) If Premine=1000, the Rune is mintable and Amount=100, Mints=90, then Supply=1000+100\*90=10000;2）

2) If Premine=0, the Rune is mintable and Amount=100, Mints=90, then Supply=0+100\*90=9000;3）

3) If Premine=10000, the Rune is non-mintable, then Supply=10000+0\*0=10000;4）

4) If Premine=0, the Rune is non-mintable, then Supply=0+0\*0=10000.(This Rune is Cenotaph)

# What is Signet? | UniSat

Signet is a Bitcoin test network designed for developers to test their applications in a controlled environment. Unlike the traditional testnet, Signet doesn't rely on miners. Instead, blocks are created by a trusted party, providing predictable and consistent block times.

**What are the Key Features?**

*   Blocks are created every 10 minutes by a trusted party, ensuring consistency.
    
*   Mimics the mainnet environment closely, making it ideal for development and testing.
    
*   Endorsed and supported by Bitcoin Core, widely adopted by the developer community.
    

**How is Signet Different from Testnet?**

*   Testnet relies on miners, leading to unpredictable block times, while Signet uses a trusted party, ensuring consistent block production.
    
*   Signet offers a more stable environment for testing compared to the often erratic testnet.
    
*   Signet is preferred by developers for its reliability and consistency, whereas testnet is used for broader testing purposes.
    

More information:

[![Logo](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fbitcoinops.org%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ad6e507&sv=2)SignetBitcoin Optechchevron-right](https://bitcoinops.org/en/topics/signet/)

# Sub 1 sat/vB Mode Setup Guide | UniSat

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/articles/understanding-sub-1-sat-vb-bitcoin-transactions/sub-1-sat-vb-mode-setup-guide#id-1.-what-is-sub-1-sat-vb-mode)

1\. What is Sub 1 sat/vB Mode ?

This refers to selecting a fee rate lower than 1 sat/vB when inscribing or using UTXO management features. Most network nodes enforce a default relay policy requiring ≥1 sat/vB. But **Sub 1 sat/vB transactions is more common now that network fee is generally low.**

✨ **Advantage of Sub 1 sat/vB Mode**:

Save transaction fees, suitable for non-urgent or large batch minting.

⚠️ **Risk of Sub 1 sat/vB Mode**:

Most pools _**do not**_ mine sub **1 sat/vB transactions.** Confirmation is **not guaranteed** may take a long time (from several hours to several days) or never get processed.

**‼️ Check Current Network Fee Rate**

Before setting sub 1 sat/vB fee rate, we recommend checking the current Bitcoin network congestion. A fee rate of 1 sat/vB or lower means it may result in longer confirmation times.

You may use [mempool.spacearrow-up-right](https://mempool.space/)
 to view the fee rate and estimated confirmation time in real time.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FZCvxNNwzRMwcgwm32SOV%252F1.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D061e83d8-eb62-40c9-b05e-15ac81b15728&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5281b08&sv=2)

1.  ### 
    
    [hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/articles/understanding-sub-1-sat-vb-bitcoin-transactions/sub-1-sat-vb-mode-setup-guide#how-to-set-sub-1-sat-vb-fee-order)
    
    How to Set **Sub 1 sat/vB Fee** Order
    

Currently, UniSat Inscribe and UTXO Management Tool services have supported **sub 1 sat/vB mode**, allowing users to set fee rates below 1 sat/vB to reduce inscribing costs.

*   In the fee selection area, set your custom fee rate manually or use the slider, e.g., `0.2 sat/vB`.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FAI0Iek3qcZ3h1QcxqBMw%252F22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9478a19-5359-410e-b36d-76ede472f96c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a75c522f&sv=2)

**Acknowledge Risk Warning**

*   The system will display a risk alert when enabling sub 1 sat/vB fee mode. Please read the on-page warning carefully, and confirm that you fully understand the risks.
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FOJv2iG0I01uh9wDyPjA7%252F33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c77f3b8-dea0-4e48-b31c-3ea6628151a0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60ce0d7c&sv=2)

**Submit the Order or transaction**

*   Click **Submit** to complete the process.
    

1.  ### 
    
    [hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/articles/understanding-sub-1-sat-vb-bitcoin-transactions/sub-1-sat-vb-mode-setup-guide#difference-between-payment-and-minting-transactions-important)
    
    Difference Between Payment and Minting Transactions (Important)
    

Please note:

*   **Under Sub 1 sat/vB Mode, you are only adjusting the fee rate for minting transaction, not for the payment transaction.**
    
*   Please **do not** manually change the fee rate for payment to ensure quick order submission
    

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FG436OOJ4t7zR4icbpMrX%252F5.PNG%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd4b66ca-b2d4-49fd-9ac2-33279d712d9d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=558ac051&sv=2)

# Glossary | UniSat

**Blockchain**

A decentralized and distributed ledger that records all transactions across a network of computers. The Bitcoin blockchain is the founding technology that enables the existence of cryptocurrency.

**Cryptocurrency**

Digital or virtual currency that uses cryptography for security. Bitcoin is a prime example of a cryptocurrency.

**Private Key**

A secret cryptographic key that allows the owner to access and control their cryptocurrency holdings. It must be kept confidential to maintain the security of the wallet.

**Public Key**

A cryptographic key derived from the private key and used to generate the wallet address. It is shared publicly and is used for receiving cryptocurrency.

**Wallet Address**

A unique identifier associated with a cryptocurrency wallet, used to receive funds. It is derived from the public key.

**Seed Phrase (or Secret Recovery Phrase)**

A series of words that serve as a backup for the private key. It is essential for wallet recovery in case of loss or device failure.

**Multi-Signature (Multisig)**

A security feature requiring multiple private keys to authorize a Bitcoin transaction. It adds an extra layer of protection against unauthorized access.

**Hardware Wallet**

A physical device designed to securely store private keys offline, reducing the risk of online hacking.

**Software Wallet**

A digital application or program that allows users to store and manage their cryptocurrency. UniSat Wallet is an example of a software wallet.

**Decentralized Finance (DeFi)**

A financial ecosystem built on blockchain technology, aiming to recreate traditional financial systems with decentralized, open-source alternatives.

**Smart Contracts**

Self-executing contracts with the terms of the agreement directly written into code. They run on blockchain networks like Ethereum, facilitating trustless and automated transactions.

**Transaction Fee**

The fee paid to miners to process and verify transactions on the blockchain. It varies based on network congestion and transaction complexity.

**Non-Fungible Token (NFT)**

Unique digital assets representing ownership or proof of authenticity for items like art, collectibles, or virtual real estate.

**Cold Storage**

Keeping private keys or seed phrases in an offline, secure environment to protect against online hacking attempts.

**Peer-to-Peer (P2P)**

Transactions that occur directly between two parties without the need for intermediaries.

**Confirmation**

The process of validating a transaction on the blockchain by multiple nodes, ensuring its accuracy and security.

**KYC (Know Your Customer)**

Verification processes to confirm the identity of wallet owners, complying with regulatory requirements.

**HD Wallet (Hierarchical Deterministic Wallet)**

A wallet that generates a hierarchical tree of keys from a single seed, making it easier to manage multiple addresses.

**Web3**

The next generation of the internet, focused on decentralized protocols and applications, including blockchain-based technologies.

**Disclaimer:**

The content of this document is for informational purposes only. It does not constitute (i) investment advice or recommendations, (ii) an offer, solicitation, or inducement to purchase, sell, or hold digital assets, or (iii) financial, accounting, legal, or tax advice. Digital assets (including FTs and NFTs) are subject to market volatility, involve high risk, regulatory changes, and may depreciate in value. The information is provided "as is," and we make no warranties regarding its accuracy. Please consult your legal, tax, or investment professionals to determine whether trading or holding digital assets is suitable for you.

# UniSat Titles | UniSat

UniSat Titles are your personal collection of digital medals that celebrate your journey in the UniSat community!

Each Title marks a moment when you helped Bitcoin grow and thrive. As you collect more, you'll unlock exciting new ways to earn benefits from UniSat and our partners, starting with exclusive allocations in UniSat Drops.

Claim your titles here by connecting your wallet to verify eligibility: [https://unisat.io/address/my\_titlearrow-up-right](https://unisat.io/address/my_title)

There is no fee involved in claiming Titles. Titles are awarded for free and exist off-chain, making them non-transferable and non-tradable digital achievements.

💡This list keeps track of all available Titles, and will continue to be updated as more Titles are released.

*   **Diamond Hand**
    
    *   WZRD (brc-20) Diamond Hand
        
        *   Acquired/minted and held of any amount of $wzrd for more than 90 days consecutive
            
        
    *   Bitcoin Wizard (NFT) Diamond Hand
        
        *   Acquired/minted and held a Bitcoin Wizard for more than 90 days consecutive
            
        
    *   UniSat OG Pass Diamond Hand
        
        *   Acquired/minted and held a UniSat OG Pass for more than 90 days consecutive
            
        
    *   Prime Access Pass Diamond Hand
        
        *   Acquired and held a UniSat Prime Access Pass for more than 90 consecutive days.
            
        
    *   Early Access Pass Diamond Hand
        
        *   Acquired and held a UniSat Early Access Pass for more than 90 consecutive days.
            
        
    *   UniSat Emblem Diamond Hand
        
        *   Acquired and held a UniSat Emblem for more than 90 consecutive days.
            
        
    
*   **Product Pioneer**
    
    *   UniSat Points Hodler (>500)
        
        *   Collected more than 500 UniSat points, on Fractal and Bitcoin network combined.
            
        
    *   Early Contributor to brc-20 Swap

    *   Fractal Inaugural Voters
        
        *   Voted in the first Fractal Vote and first Fractal Eco vote(include all 7 eco projects vote)
            
        
    

*   **Community Builder**

        *   Received any UniSat emblem for participating in community events and still hold the emblem in the wallet

# .unisat Names | UniSat

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/ordinals/.unisat-names#so-what-is-.unisat)

So what is .unisat?

It's easy to explain what .unisat is - **.unisat follows exactly the same protocol as .sats** ([the documentationarrow-up-right](https://docs.sats.id/)
), except it produces accumulative benefits to your account in UniSat Products.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FQTJTX6kQTf5ZFGWioscB%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7325e080-1560-4a9b-be41-89ffa88091c4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=68e63d3c&sv=2)

Just like what happens to .sats

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/ordinals/.unisat-names#inscribe-.unisat-directly)

Inscribe .unisat directly

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FVXIkRJ3SD5RNWYwEjUj7%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05e4fb41-06a1-43b2-8de0-1c0861eb8508&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f5745b8&sv=2)

the first class tab of UniSat Inscribe for .unisat

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/ordinals/.unisat-names#search-for-.unisat-directly)

Search for .unisat directly

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FpzInog7qAKLinNtdIfEI%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da75874e1-8092-46d3-b829-2cfcc8c50de8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=860410d0&sv=2)

the first class tab of UniSat Search for .unisat

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/ordinals/.unisat-names#accumulative-benefits)

Accumulative benefits

Specifically for UniSat Inscribe, one .unisat in your address produces a 1% discount. There are five .unisat names at most that take effect in one payment.

![](https://docs.unisat.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3523236551-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ4NHAHIVnWQiEecvs1By%252Fuploads%252FLIT1wrmUd9Je2gZLTpj8%252F5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4432a79-038b-47e7-8a45-97145f8066d5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1ff36780&sv=2)

Two .unisat names produce 2% discounts.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.unisat.io/misc/knowledge-base/ordinals/.unisat-names#extra-resources)

Extra resources

*   For a complete reference, please check out [the documentation of .sats herearrow-up-right](https://docs.sats.id/)
    .
    
*   For a video tutorial, please check out the tutorial about inscribing multiple .unisat here.
    

Yes, it's that easy.

Fair Mint

Free
